  14 /*
  15  * 1.传入window
  16  * 通过传入window变量，使得window由全局变量变为局部变量
  17  * 当在jQuery代码块中访问window时，不需要将作用域链回退到顶层作用域，这样可以更快的访问window
  18  * 更重要的是，将window作为参数传入，可以在压缩代码时进行优化
  19  * (function(a,b){})(window);window 被优化为 a,压缩后文件更小
  20  * 2.传入undefined
  21  * 是为了在"自调用匿名函数"的作用域内，确保undefined是真的未定义
  22  * 因为undefined能够被重写，赋予新的值 
  23  * undefined = "now it's defined";
  24  * alert( undefined );
  25  * 浏览器测试结果：
  26  * ------------+----------------------+-------------
  27  *   浏览器    |    测试结果          |   结论
  28  *   ie        |    now it's defined  |   可以改变
  29  *   firefox   |    undefined         |   不能改变
  30  *   chrome    |    now it's defined  |   可以改变
  31  *   opera     |    now it's defined  |   可以改变
  32  * ------------+----------------------+-------------
  33  */
  34 (function( window, undefined ) {
  35 var
  36     // A central reference to the root jQuery(document)
  37     // 对根jQuery对象的主要引用
  38     rootjQuery,
  39 
  40     // The deferred used on DOM ready
  41     // 在DOM准备好时调用
  42     readyList,
  43 
  44     // Use the correct document accordingly with window argument (sandbox)
  45     // 根据window参数设置正确的文档对象
  46     document = window.document,
  47     location = window.location,
  48     navigator = window.navigator,
  49 
  50     // Map over jQuery in case of overwrite
  51     // 防止被覆盖
  52     _jQuery = window.jQuery,
  53 
  54     // Map over the $ in case of overwrite
  55     // 防止被覆盖
  56     _$ = window.$,
  57 
  58     // Save a reference to some core methods
  59     // 为核心方法创建引用
  60     core_push = Array.prototype.push,
  61     core_slice = Array.prototype.slice,
  62     core_indexOf = Array.prototype.indexOf,
  63     core_toString = Object.prototype.toString,
  64     core_hasOwn = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty,
  65     core_trim = String.prototype.trim,
  66 
  67     // Define a local copy of jQuery
  68     // 构建jQuery对象
  69     jQuery = function( selector, context ) {
  70         // The jQuery object is actually just the init constructor 'enhanced'
  71         /* 
  72          * jQuery对象实际上只是增强的初始化构造方法,使用原型上的prototype上的init方法构建对象
  73          * jQuery.fn即为jQuery.prototype，通过将jQuery的原型赋给jQuery.fn.init的原型
  74          * 来解决使用init创建实例，创建出的对象继承的是init的prototype上的方法而不会继承jQuery prototype上的方法的问题
  75          */
  76         return new jQuery.fn.init( selector, context, rootjQuery );
  77     },
  78 
  79     // Used for matching numbers
  80     /* 用来匹配数字的正则，可匹配可选正负号，浮点型，整型，科学计数法
  81      * 没有使用?来表示可选而是通过|来选择
  82      * (?:\d*\.|)匹配浮点数时，|前的\d*\.可以匹配整数部分和小数点，小数部分由后面的\d+匹配
  83      * 匹配整数时，|)可以保证匹配继续向下进行，整数由后面的\d+匹配，同样的\d+在匹配整型和浮点型时负责的匹配部分不同
  84      * [eE][\-+]?\d+|)处理科学计数法的匹配，同样没有使用?表示可选
  85      */
  86     core_pnum = /[\-+]?(?:\d*\.|)\d+(?:[eE][\-+]?\d+|)/.source,
  87 
  88     // Used for detecting and trimming whitespace
  89     // 用来探测和裁剪空格
  90     // 匹配任何非空白字符。等价于[^ \f\n\r\t\v]
  91     // ' '为空格，\f为换页符，\n为换行符，\r为回车符，\t为制表符，\v为垂直制表符
  92     core_rnotwhite = /\S/,
  93     // 匹配多个任何非空白字符。等价于[ \f\n\r\t\v]+
  94     core_rspace = /\s+/,
  95 
  96     // Make sure we trim BOM and NBSP (here's looking at you, Safari 5.0 and IE)
  97     // 确信裁剪BOM和NBSP，non-breaking spaces，即nbsp,详见http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nbsp 需要特殊处理
  98 
  99     rtrim = /^[\s\uFEFF\xA0]+|[\s\uFEFF\xA0]+$/g,
 100 
 101     // A simple way to check for HTML strings
 102     // 一种检查HTML字符串的简便方式
 103     // Prioritize #id over <tag> to avoid XSS via location.hash (#9521)
 104     // 优先检测#id,防止XSS
 105     rquickExpr = /^(?:[^#<]*(<[\w\W]+>)[^>]*$|#([\w\-]*)$)/,
 106 
 107     // Match a standalone tag
 108     // 匹配一个独立的tag,<></>或者</>
 109     rsingleTag = /^<(\w+)\s*\/?>(?:<\/\1>|)$/,
 110 
 111     // JSON RegExp
 112     // 匹配json格式数据
 113     rvalidchars = /^[\],:{}\s]*$/,
 114     rvalidbraces = /(?:^|:|,)(?:\s*\[)+/g,
 115     rvalidescape = /\\(?:["\\\/bfnrt]|u[\da-fA-F]{4})/g,
 116     rvalidtokens = /"[^"\\\r\n]*"|true|false|null|-?(?:\d\d*\.|)\d+(?:[eE][\-+]?\d+|)/g,
 117 
 118     // Matches dashed string for camelizing
 119     rmsPrefix = /^-ms-/,
 120     rdashAlpha = /-([\da-z])/gi,
 121 
 122     // Used by jQuery.camelCase as callback to replace()
 123     fcamelCase = function( all, letter ) {
 124         return ( letter + "" ).toUpperCase();
 125     },
 126 
 127     // The ready event handler and self cleanup method
 128     // ready事件的处理器，自我清理函数
 129     DOMContentLoaded = function() {
 130         // 判断浏览器绑定事件回调的函数，决定调用相应的解绑函数
 131         // attachEvent/addEventListener 
 132         if ( document.addEventListener ) {
 133             document.removeEventListener( "DOMContentLoaded", DOMContentLoaded, false );
 134             jQuery.ready();
 135         } else if ( document.readyState === "complete" ) {
 136             // we're here because readyState === "complete" in oldIE
 137             // which is good enough for us to call the dom ready!
 138             // 在旧版本IE中使用readyState === "complete"可以正确判断dom ready事件
 139             document.detachEvent( "onreadystatechange", DOMContentLoaded );
 140             jQuery.ready();
 141         }
 142     },
 143 
 144     // [[Class]] -> type pairs
 145     class2type = {};
 146 
 147 /* 
 148  * 将jQuery的prototype赋给jQuery.fn，缓存jQuery.prototype属性，避免频繁访问带来的额外开销
 149  * jQuery的构造函数是原型上的init方法，而不是function jQuery 
 150  * 每次调用$()会用jQuery原型上的init创建一个实例 
 151  */
 152 jQuery.fn = jQuery.prototype = {
 153     constructor: jQuery,
 154     init: function( selector, context, rootjQuery ) {
 155         // context:待查找的 DOM 元素集、文档或 jQuery 对象
 156         var match, elem, ret, doc;
 157 
 158         // Handle $(""), $(null), $(undefined), $(false)
 159         // 处理 $(""), $(null), $(undefined), $(false)
 160         if ( !selector ) {
 161             return this;
 162         }
 163 
 164         // Handle $(DOMElement)
 165         // 处理直接传入dom对象的情况
 166         // 如果传入对象含有nodeType属性，则为dom对象，使用jQuery对象进行包装
 167         if ( selector.nodeType ) {
 168             this.context = this[0] = selector;
 169             this.length = 1;
 170             return this;
 171         }
 172 
 173         // Handle HTML strings
 174         // 处理HTML字符串，根据HTML生成dom
 175         if ( typeof selector === "string" ) {
 176             /* 
 177              * 如果传入的选择器是字符类型
 178              * 可能是选择器，比如$('p')，也可能是需要创建的dom对象$('<p>foo</p>')
 179              * 可以创建片段fragment
 180              */
 181             // 如果传入的字符串第一个和最后一个字符分别是<和>，并且字符串长度大于等于3，则认为需要创建dom对象
 182             if ( selector.charAt(0) === "<" && selector.charAt( selector.length - 1 ) === ">" && selector.length >= 3 ) {
 183                 // Assume that strings that start and end with <> are HTML and skip the regex check
 184                 // 确认字符串是html标签并且跳过正则检查
 185                 match = [ null, selector, null ];
 186 
 187             } else {
 188                 // 对选择器进行正则检查
 189                 match = rquickExpr.exec( selector );
 190             }
 191 
 192             // Match html or make sure no context is specified for #id
 193             // 选择器是html字符串并且没有传入待查找的上下文
 194             // match[1]即为匹配到的html字符串
 195             if ( match && (match[1] || !context) ) {
 196 
 197                 // HANDLE: $(html) -> $(array)
 198                 // match[1]不为空
 199                 if ( match[1] ) {
 200                     // match[1]不为空，则说明不是以#id开头的选择器，是要生成的html的代码
 201                     // 查找上下文context可以是jQuery对象，如果是jQuery对象，则拿到其包装的dom对象
 202                     // jQuery对象将其对应的dom对象放在0映射的value中
 203                     context = context instanceof jQuery ? context[0] : context;
 204                     // 问号表达式，当判断式为true的时候需要进行OR操作符的判断，OR操作符具体判断规则如下：
 205                     /*
 206                      * 如果一个运算数是对象，另一个是 Boolean 值，返回该对象。
 207                      * 如果两个运算数都是对象，返回第二个对象。
 208                      * 如果某个运算数是 null，返回 null。
 209                      * 如果某个运算数是 NaN，返回 NaN。
 210                      * 如果某个运算数是 undefined，发生错误。
 211                      */
 212                     // 为true时，context.ownerDocument || context返回非null的对象，如果两个对象都不是null，则返回context
 213                     doc = ( context && context.nodeType ? context.ownerDocument || context : document );
 214 
 215                     // scripts is true for back-compat
 216                     // 脚本向后兼容
 217                     selector = jQuery.parseHTML( match[1], doc, true );
 218                     if ( rsingleTag.test( match[1] ) && jQuery.isPlainObject( context ) ) {
 219                         this.attr.call( selector, context, true );
 220                     }
 221 
 222                     return jQuery.merge( this, selector );
 223 
 224                 // HANDLE: $(#id)
 225                 // 处理:$(#id)
 226                 // 使用rootjQuery.find进行查找
 227                 } else {
 228                     // match[1]为空，传入context，则要根据id获取元素
 229                     elem = document.getElementById( match[2] );
 230 
 231                     // Check parentNode to catch when Blackberry 4.6 returns
 232                     // nodes that are no longer in the document #6963
 233                     // 当黑莓4.6返回不存在于文档树的节点时，检查需要捕获的父节点
 234                     if ( elem && elem.parentNode ) {
 235                         // Handle the case where IE and Opera return items
 236                         // by name instead of ID
 237                         // 处理IE和Opera使用name替代id返回的情况
 238                         if ( elem.id !== match[2] ) {
 239                             // 查找节点
 240                             return rootjQuery.find( selector );
 241                         }
 242 
 243                         // Otherwise, we inject the element directly into the jQuery object
 244                         // 将找到的元素的原生dom元素直接注入到jQuery对象中，保存在0这个属性中
 245                         // 并设置jQuery对象的length属性值为1
 246                         this.length = 1;
 247                         this[0] = elem;
 248                     }
 249 
 250                     this.context = document;
 251                     this.selector = selector;
 252                     return this;
 253                 }
 254 
 255             // HANDLE: $(expr, $(...))
 256             // 处理$(expr, $(...))的情况，可以指定要查找的范围
 257             // match[1]为空，context不为空且为jQuery对象
 258             } else if ( !context || context.jquery ) {
 259                 return ( context || rootjQuery ).find( selector );
 260 
 261             // HANDLE: $(expr, context)
 262             // (which is just equivalent to: $(context).find(expr)
 263             // 处理$(expr, context),使用$(context).find(expr)进行查找
 264             // match[1]为空，context不为空且不为jQuery对象，先构造为jQuery对象，再进行查找
 265             } else {
 266                 return this.constructor( context ).find( selector );
 267             }
 268 
 269         // HANDLE: $(function)
 270         // Shortcut for document ready
 271         // 允许你绑定一个在 DOM 文档载入完成后执行的函数。
 272         // 该函数的作用如同 $(document).ready() 一样，只不过用这个函数时，需要把页面中所有需要在 DOM 加载完成时执行的其他 $() 操作符都包装到其中来
 273         // 尽管从技术上来说，这个函数是可链接的，但真正以这种方式链接的情况并不多。
 274 
 275         } else if ( jQuery.isFunction( selector ) ) {
 276             return rootjQuery.ready( selector );
 277         }
 278 
 279         if ( selector.selector !== undefined ) {
 280             // 将选择器和上下文对象保存到jQuery对象中
 281             this.selector = selector.selector;
 282             this.context = selector.context;
 283         }
 284 
 285         return jQuery.makeArray( selector, this );
 286     },
 287 
 288     // Start with an empty selector
 289     // 初始化空selector
 290     selector: "",
 291 
 292     // The current version of jQuery being used
 293     // 当前使用的jQuery的版本
 294     jquery: "1.8.1",
 295 
 296     // The default length of a jQuery object is 0
 297     // jQuery对象的默认length设置为0，设置该属性为了模拟数组
 298     length: 0,
 299 
 300     // The number of elements contained in the matched element set
 301     // 匹配元素集的元素个数
 302     size: function() {
 303         return this.length;
 304     },
 305 
 306     // 调用Array.prototype.slice
 307     toArray: function() {
 308         return core_slice.call( this );
 309     },
 310 
 311     // Get the Nth element in the matched element set OR
 312     // Get the whole matched element set as a clean array
 313     // 获取第n个匹配元素或者获取包含匹配元素的纯数组
 314     get: function( num ) {
 315         return num == null ?
 316 
 317             // Return a 'clean' array
 318             // 如果不传入序号，则返回包含匹配元素的纯数组
 319             this.toArray() :
 320 
 321             // Return just the object
 322             // 返回匹配元素的dom对象，如果传入负数，则按照倒序取
 323             ( num < 0 ? this[ this.length + num ] : this[ num ] );
 324     },
 325 
 326     // Take an array of elements and push it onto the stack
 327     // (returning the new matched element set)
 328     // 将一个DOM元素集合加入到jQuery栈
 329     pushStack: function( elems, name, selector ) {
 330 
 331         // Build a new jQuery matched element set
 332         // 调用jQuery的构造方法构造一个新对象，并将dom元素集合merge到新的对象中
 333         var ret = jQuery.merge( this.constructor(), elems );
 334 
 335         // Add the old object onto the stack (as a reference)
 336         // 持有就jQuery对象的引用
 337         ret.prevObject = this;
 338 
 339         // 传递上下文对象
 340         ret.context = this.context;
 341 
 342         if ( name === "find" ) {
 343             ret.selector = this.selector + ( this.selector ? " " : "" ) + selector;
 344         } else if ( name ) {
 345             ret.selector = this.selector + "." + name + "(" + selector + ")";
 346         }
 347 
 348         // Return the newly-formed element set
 349         // 返回新的包装过的元素集合
 350         return ret;
 351     },
 352 
 353     // Execute a callback for every element in the matched set.
 354     // 对集合中的所有元素调用回调函数
 355     // (You can seed the arguments with an array of args, but this is
 356     // only used internally.)
 357     // 你可以使用一个数组来传递参数，但是这种功能只是为内部使用而提供
 358     each: function( callback, args ) {
 359         return jQuery.each( this, callback, args );
 360     },
 361 
 362     ready: function( fn ) {
 363         // Add the callback
 364         // 增加回调，使用jQuery.ready.promise()返回的只读Deferred对象
 365         jQuery.ready.promise().done( fn );
 366 
 367         return this;
 368     },
 369 
 370     // 获取匹配集合中指定的元素
 371     // 使用pushStack构造新的jQuery对象
 372     eq: function( i ) {
 373         i = +i;
 374         return i === -1 ?
 375             /*
 376              * 当slice函数的第一个参数为负数时，是倒数计数，截取逻辑是向数组的末尾方向进行截取
 377              * 比如数组[a,b,c,d,e,f,g],slice(-4)即为从倒数第二个元素截取到数组末尾，为[d,e,f,g]
 378              * slice(-4,-2)为从倒数第四个元素截取到倒数第二个元素，为[d,e]
 379              * 并且slice第一个参数为负时，第二个参数不能为0，所以i===-1需要特殊处理
 380              */
 381             this.slice( i ) :
 382             this.slice( i, i + 1 );
 383     },
 384 
 385     // 第一个元素
 386     first: function() {
 387         return this.eq( 0 );
 388     },
 389 
 390     // 最后一个元素
 391     last: function() {
 392         return this.eq( -1 );
 393     },
 394 
 395     // 通过Array.prototype.slice实现数组的截取
 396     // 通过pushStack实现截取对象的包装
 397     slice: function() {
 398         return this.pushStack( core_slice.apply( this, arguments ),
 399             "slice", core_slice.call(arguments).join(",") );
 400     },
 401 
 402     // 遍历一个可遍历的类似数组的对象，对元素调用callback，将结果存到另一个数组中
 403     map: function( callback ) {
 404         return this.pushStack( jQuery.map(this, function( elem, i ) {
 405             return callback.call( elem, i, elem );
 406         }));
 407     },
 408 
 409     // 获取pushStack构造的对象中持有的原数据对象的引用
 410     end: function() {
 411         return this.prevObject || this.constructor(null);
 412     },
 413 
 414     // For internal use only.
 415     // 内部使用
 416     // Behaves like an Array's method, not like a jQuery method.
 417     // 模拟数组对象的行为
 418     push: core_push,
 419     // 调用数组的排序方法进行排序
 420     sort: [].sort,
 421     splice: [].splice
 422 };
 423 
 424 // Give the init function the jQuery prototype for later instantiation
 425 /*
 426  * 将jQuery的原型赋给jQuery.fn.init的原型，使init方法创建的对象包含jQuery原型中的方法
 427  * 解决如果使用init创建实例，这个对象继承的是init的prototype上的方法而不会继承jQuery prototype上的方法的问题 
 428  */
 429 jQuery.fn.init.prototype = jQuery.fn;
 430 
 431 jQuery.extend = jQuery.fn.extend = function() {
 432     var options, name, src, copy, copyIsArray, clone,
 433         target = arguments[0] || {},
 434         i = 1,
 435         length = arguments.length,
 436         deep = false;
 437 
 438     // Handle a deep copy situation
 439     if ( typeof target === "boolean" ) {
 440         deep = target;
 441         target = arguments[1] || {};
 442         // skip the boolean and the target
 443         i = 2;
 444     }
 445 
 446     // Handle case when target is a string or something (possible in deep copy)
 447     if ( typeof target !== "object" && !jQuery.isFunction(target) ) {
 448         target = {};
 449     }
 450 
 451     // extend jQuery itself if only one argument is passed
 452     if ( length === i ) {
 453         target = this;
 454         --i;
 455     }
 456 
 457     for ( ; i < length; i++ ) {
 458         // Only deal with non-null/undefined values
 459         if ( (options = arguments[ i ]) != null ) {
 460             // Extend the base object
 461             for ( name in options ) {
 462                 src = target[ name ];
 463                 copy = options[ name ];
 464 
 465                 // Prevent never-ending loop
 466                 if ( target === copy ) {
 467                     continue;
 468                 }
 469 
 470                 // Recurse if we're merging plain objects or arrays
 471                 if ( deep && copy && ( jQuery.isPlainObject(copy) || (copyIsArray = jQuery.isArray(copy)) ) ) {
 472                     if ( copyIsArray ) {
 473                         copyIsArray = false;
 474                         clone = src && jQuery.isArray(src) ? src : [];
 475 
 476                     } else {
 477                         clone = src && jQuery.isPlainObject(src) ? src : {};
 478                     }
 479 
 480                     // Never move original objects, clone them
 481                     target[ name ] = jQuery.extend( deep, clone, copy );
 482 
 483                 // Don't bring in undefined values
 484                 } else if ( copy !== undefined ) {
 485                     target[ name ] = copy;
 486                 }
 487             }
 488         }
 489     }
 490 
 491     // Return the modified object
 492     return target;
 493 };
 494 
 495 jQuery.extend({
 496     noConflict: function( deep ) {
 497         if ( window.$ === jQuery ) {
 498             window.$ = _$;
 499         }
 500 
 501         if ( deep && window.jQuery === jQuery ) {
 502             window.jQuery = _jQuery;
 503         }
 504 
 505         return jQuery;
 506     },
 507 
 508     // Is the DOM ready to be used? Set to true once it occurs.
 509     isReady: false,
 510 
 511     // A counter to track how many items to wait for before
 512     // the ready event fires. See #6781
 513     readyWait: 1,
 514 
 515     // Hold (or release) the ready event
 516     holdReady: function( hold ) {
 517         if ( hold ) {
 518             jQuery.readyWait++;
 519         } else {
 520             jQuery.ready( true );
 521         }
 522     },
 523 
 524     // Handle when the DOM is ready
 525     ready: function( wait ) {
 526 
 527         // Abort if there are pending holds or we're already ready
 528         if ( wait === true ? --jQuery.readyWait : jQuery.isReady ) {
 529             return;
 530         }
 531 
 532         // Make sure body exists, at least, in case IE gets a little overzealous (ticket #5443).
 533         if ( !document.body ) {
 534             return setTimeout( jQuery.ready, 1 );
 535         }
 536 
 537         // Remember that the DOM is ready
 538         jQuery.isReady = true;
 539 
 540         // If a normal DOM Ready event fired, decrement, and wait if need be
 541         if ( wait !== true && --jQuery.readyWait > 0 ) {
 542             return;
 543         }
 544 
 545         // If there are functions bound, to execute
 546         readyList.resolveWith( document, [ jQuery ] );
 547 
 548         // Trigger any bound ready events
 549         if ( jQuery.fn.trigger ) {
 550             jQuery( document ).trigger("ready").off("ready");
 551         }
 552     },
 553 
 554     // See test/unit/core.js for details concerning isFunction.
 555     // 涉及isFunction的详细信息参见test/unit/core.js
 556     // Since version 1.3, DOM methods and functions like alert
 557     // 从1.3版本以后，DOM方法和函数，比如alert不再被支持，他们在IE上返回false
 558     // aren't supported. They return false on IE (#2968).
 559     isFunction: function( obj ) {
 560         return jQuery.type(obj) === "function";
 561     },
 562 
 563     isArray: Array.isArray || function( obj ) {
 564         return jQuery.type(obj) === "array";
 565     },
 566 
 567     isWindow: function( obj ) {
 568         return obj != null && obj == obj.window;
 569     },
 570 
 571     isNumeric: function( obj ) {
 572         return !isNaN( parseFloat(obj) ) && isFinite( obj );
 573     },
 574 
 575     // 获取对象类型，core_toString即为Object.prototype.toString函数
 576     type: function( obj ) {
 577         return obj == null ?
 578             String( obj ) :
 579             class2type[ core_toString.call(obj) ] || "object";
 580     },
 581 
 582     isPlainObject: function( obj ) {
 583         // Must be an Object.
 584         // Because of IE, we also have to check the presence of the constructor property.
 585         // Make sure that DOM nodes and window objects don't pass through, as well
 586         if ( !obj || jQuery.type(obj) !== "object" || obj.nodeType || jQuery.isWindow( obj ) ) {
 587             return false;
 588         }
 589 
 590         try {
 591             // Not own constructor property must be Object
 592             if ( obj.constructor &&
 593                 !core_hasOwn.call(obj, "constructor") &&
 594                 !core_hasOwn.call(obj.constructor.prototype, "isPrototypeOf") ) {
 595                 return false;
 596             }
 597         } catch ( e ) {
 598             // IE8,9 Will throw exceptions on certain host objects #9897
 599             return false;
 600         }
 601 
 602         // Own properties are enumerated firstly, so to speed up,
 603         // if last one is own, then all properties are own.
 604 
 605         var key;
 606         for ( key in obj ) {}
 607 
 608         return key === undefined || core_hasOwn.call( obj, key );
 609     },
 610 
 611     isEmptyObject: function( obj ) {
 612         var name;
 613         for ( name in obj ) {
 614             return false;
 615         }
 616         return true;
 617     },
 618 
 619     error: function( msg ) {
 620         throw new Error( msg );
 621     },
 622 
 623     // 解析HTML字符串，生成相应的dom元素并返回
 624     // data: string of html
 625     // data: html字符串表示
 626     // context (optional): If specified, the fragment will be created in this context, defaults to document
 627     // context (可选的) : 如果指定，片段会被创建到该上下文上，默认是创建在document上
 628     // scripts (optional): If true, will include scripts passed in the html string
 629     // scripts (可选的) : 如果为true，会包含在html字符串中包含的脚本
 630     parseHTML: function( data, context, scripts ) {
 631         var parsed;
 632         if ( !data || typeof data !== "string" ) {
 633             return null;
 634         }
 635         if ( typeof context === "boolean" ) {
 636             // 如果context是布尔类型，则将context的值赋给scripts,并将context设置为0
 637             scripts = context;
 638             context = 0;
 639         }
 640         context = context || document;
 641 
 642         // Single tag
 643         // 判断是否是单一标签，创建该dom元素后返回
 644         if ( (parsed = rsingleTag.exec( data )) ) {
 645             return [ context.createElement( parsed[1] ) ];
 646         }
 647 
 648         // 多标签，生成片段
 649         parsed = jQuery.buildFragment( [ data ], context, scripts ? null : [] );
 650         return jQuery.merge( [],
 651             (parsed.cacheable ? jQuery.clone( parsed.fragment ) : parsed.fragment).childNodes );
 652     },
 653 
 654     parseJSON: function( data ) {
 655         if ( !data || typeof data !== "string") {
 656             return null;
 657         }
 658 
 659         // Make sure leading/trailing whitespace is removed (IE can't handle it)
 660         data = jQuery.trim( data );
 661 
 662         // Attempt to parse using the native JSON parser first
 663         if ( window.JSON && window.JSON.parse ) {
 664             return window.JSON.parse( data );
 665         }
 666 
 667         // Make sure the incoming data is actual JSON
 668         // Logic borrowed from http://json.org/json2.js
 669         if ( rvalidchars.test( data.replace( rvalidescape, "@" )
 670             .replace( rvalidtokens, "]" )
 671             .replace( rvalidbraces, "")) ) {
 672 
 673             return ( new Function( "return " + data ) )();
 674 
 675         }
 676         jQuery.error( "Invalid JSON: " + data );
 677     },
 678 
 679     // Cross-browser xml parsing
 680     parseXML: function( data ) {
 681         var xml, tmp;
 682         if ( !data || typeof data !== "string" ) {
 683             return null;
 684         }
 685         try {
 686             if ( window.DOMParser ) { // Standard
 687                 tmp = new DOMParser();
 688                 xml = tmp.parseFromString( data , "text/xml" );
 689             } else { // IE
 690                 xml = new ActiveXObject( "Microsoft.XMLDOM" );
 691                 xml.async = "false";
 692                 xml.loadXML( data );
 693             }
 694         } catch( e ) {
 695             xml = undefined;
 696         }
 697         if ( !xml || !xml.documentElement || xml.getElementsByTagName( "parsererror" ).length ) {
 698             jQuery.error( "Invalid XML: " + data );
 699         }
 700         return xml;
 701     },

 705     // Evaluates a script in a global context
 706     // Workarounds based on findings by Jim Driscoll
 707     // http://weblogs.java.net/blog/driscoll/archive/2009/09/08/eval-javascript-global-context
 708     globalEval: function( data ) {
 709         if ( data && core_rnotwhite.test( data ) ) {
 710             // We use execScript on Internet Explorer
 711             // We use an anonymous function so that context is window
 712             // rather than jQuery in Firefox
 713             ( window.execScript || function( data ) {
 714                 window[ "eval" ].call( window, data );
 715             } )( data );
 716         }
 717     },

 719     // Convert dashed to camelCase; used by the css and data modules
 720     // Microsoft forgot to hump their vendor prefix (#9572)
 721     camelCase: function( string ) {
 722         return string.replace( rmsPrefix, "ms-" ).replace( rdashAlpha, fcamelCase );

 725     // 判断dom元素的节点名称和name是否一样
 726     nodeName: function( elem, name ) {
 727         return elem.nodeName && elem.nodeName.toUpperCase() === name.toUpperCase();

 730     // args is for internal usage only
 731     each: function( obj, callback, args ) {
 732         var name,
 733             i = 0,
 734             length = obj.length,
 735             isObj = length === undefined || jQuery.isFunction( obj );
 736 
 737         if ( args ) {
 738             if ( isObj ) {
 739                 for ( name in obj ) {
 740                     if ( callback.apply( obj[ name ], args ) === false ) {
 741                         break;
 742                     }
 743                 }
 744             } else {
 745                 for ( ; i < length; ) {
 746                     if ( callback.apply( obj[ i++ ], args ) === false ) {
 747                         break;
 748                     }
 749                 }
 750             }
 751 
 752         // A special, fast, case for the most common use of each
 753         } else {
 754             if ( isObj ) {
 755                 for ( name in obj ) {
 756                     if ( callback.call( obj[ name ], name, obj[ name ] ) === false ) {
 757                         break;
 758                     }
 759                 }
 760             } else {
 761                 for ( ; i < length; ) {
 762                     if ( callback.call( obj[ i ], i, obj[ i++ ] ) === false ) {
 763                         break;
 764                     }
 765                 }
 766             }
 767         }
 768 
 769         return obj;
 770     },

 772     // Use native String.trim function wherever possible
 773     trim: core_trim && !core_trim.call("\uFEFF\xA0") ?
 774         function( text ) {
 775             return text == null ?
 776                 "" :
 777                 core_trim.call( text );
 778         } :
 779 
 780         // Otherwise use our own trimming functionality
 781         function( text ) {
 782             return text == null ?
 783                 "" :
 784                 text.toString().replace( rtrim, "" );
 785         },

 787     // results is for internal usage only
 788     makeArray: function( arr, results ) {
 789         var type,
 790             ret = results || [];
 791 
 792         if ( arr != null ) {
 793             // The window, strings (and functions) also have 'length'
 794             // Tweaked logic slightly to handle Blackberry 4.7 RegExp issues #6930
 795             type = jQuery.type( arr );
 796 
 797             if ( arr.length == null || type === "string" || type === "function" || type === "regexp" || jQuery.isWindow( arr ) ) {
 798                 core_push.call( ret, arr );
 799             } else {
 800                 jQuery.merge( ret, arr );
 801             }
 802         }
 803 
 804         return ret;
 805     },
 806 
 807     inArray: function( elem, arr, i ) {
 808         var len;
 809 
 810         if ( arr ) {
 811             if ( core_indexOf ) {
 812                 return core_indexOf.call( arr, elem, i );
 813             }
 814 
 815             len = arr.length;
 816             i = i ? i < 0 ? Math.max( 0, len + i ) : i : 0;
 817 
 818             for ( ; i < len; i++ ) {
 819                 // Skip accessing in sparse arrays
 820                 if ( i in arr && arr[ i ] === elem ) {
 821                     return i;
 822                 }
 823             }
 824         }
 825 
 826         return -1;
 827     },
 828 
 829     // 合并两个对象
 830     merge: function( first, second ) {
 831         var l = second.length,
 832             i = first.length,
 833             j = 0;
 834 
 835         // 如果要合并的两个对象的length属性为number，进行追加合并
 836         if ( typeof l === "number" ) {
 837             for ( ; j < l; j++ ) {
 838                 first[ i++ ] = second[ j ];
 839             }
 840 
 841         } else {
 842             // 如果要合并的两个对象的length属性不为number，则进行属性追加
 843             // foo{0:a,1:b,2:c},bar{0:d,1:e}合并后为foo{0:a,1:b,2:c,3:d,4:e}
 844             while ( second[j] !== undefined ) {
 845                 first[ i++ ] = second[ j++ ];
 846             }
 847         }
 848 
 849         // 设置length,合并过后的对象一定会有一个length属性
 850         first.length = i;
 851 
 852         return first;
 853     },
 854 
 855     /*
 856      * elems 要处理的数组
 857      * callback 在每个数组元素上调用的函数
 858      * inv 指示进行选取还是过滤
 859      * inv为false，保留调用callback返回true的元素
 860      * inv为true保留调用callback为false的元素
 861      */
 862     grep: function( elems, callback, inv ) {
 863         var retVal,
 864             ret = [],
 865             i = 0,
 866             length = elems.length;
 867         // 将inv转换由任何类型转换为布尔类型
 868         inv = !!inv;
 869 
 870         // Go through the array, only saving the items
 871         // that pass the validator function
 872         for ( ; i < length; i++ ) {
 873             // 在每个数组元素上调用回调
 874             retVal = !!callback( elems[ i ], i );
 875             if ( inv !== retVal ) {
 876                 ret.push( elems[ i ] );
 877             }
 878         }
 879 
 880         return ret;
 881     },
 882 
 883     // arg is for internal usage only
 884     map: function( elems, callback, arg ) {
 885         var value, key,
 886             ret = [],
 887             i = 0,
 888             length = elems.length,
 889             // jquery objects are treated as arrays
 890             isArray = elems instanceof jQuery || length !== undefined && typeof length === "number" && ( ( length > 0 && elems[ 0 ] && elems[ length -1 ] ) || length === 0 || jQuery.isArray( elems ) ) ;
 891 
 892         // Go through the array, translating each of the items to their
 893         if ( isArray ) {
 894             for ( ; i < length; i++ ) {
 895                 value = callback( elems[ i ], i, arg );
 896 
 897                 if ( value != null ) {
 898                     ret[ ret.length ] = value;
 899                 }
 900             }
 901 
 902         // Go through every key on the object,
 903         } else {
 904             for ( key in elems ) {
 905                 value = callback( elems[ key ], key, arg );
 906 
 907                 if ( value != null ) {
 908                     ret[ ret.length ] = value;
 909                 }
 910             }
 911         }
 912 
 913         // Flatten any nested arrays
 914         return ret.concat.apply( [], ret );
 915     },
 916 
 917     // A global GUID counter for objects
 918     guid: 1,
 919 
 920     // Bind a function to a context, optionally partially applying any
 921     // arguments.
 922     proxy: function( fn, context ) {
 923         var tmp, args, proxy;
 924 
 925         if ( typeof context === "string" ) {
 926             tmp = fn[ context ];
 927             context = fn;
 928             fn = tmp;
 929         }
 930 
 931         // Quick check to determine if target is callable, in the spec
 932         // this throws a TypeError, but we will just return undefined.
 933         if ( !jQuery.isFunction( fn ) ) {
 934             return undefined;
 935         }
 936 
 937         // Simulated bind
 938         args = core_slice.call( arguments, 2 );
 939         proxy = function() {
 940             return fn.apply( context, args.concat( core_slice.call( arguments ) ) );
 941         };
 942 
 943         // Set the guid of unique handler to the same of original handler, so it can be removed
 944         proxy.guid = fn.guid = fn.guid || proxy.guid || jQuery.guid++;
 945 
 946         return proxy;
 947     },
 948 
 949     // Multifunctional method to get and set values of a collection
 950     // The value/s can optionally be executed if it's a function
 951     access: function( elems, fn, key, value, chainable, emptyGet, pass ) {
 952         var exec,
 953             bulk = key == null,
 954             i = 0,
 955             length = elems.length;
 956 
 957         // Sets many values
 958         if ( key && typeof key === "object" ) {
 959             for ( i in key ) {
 960                 jQuery.access( elems, fn, i, key[i], 1, emptyGet, value );
 961             }
 962             chainable = 1;
 963 
 964         // Sets one value
 965         } else if ( value !== undefined ) {
 966             // Optionally, function values get executed if exec is true
 967             exec = pass === undefined && jQuery.isFunction( value );
 968 
 969             if ( bulk ) {
 970                 // Bulk operations only iterate when executing function values
 971                 if ( exec ) {
 972                     exec = fn;
 973                     fn = function( elem, key, value ) {
 974                         return exec.call( jQuery( elem ), value );
 975                     };
 976 
 977                 // Otherwise they run against the entire set
 978                 } else {
 979                     fn.call( elems, value );
 980                     fn = null;
 981                 }
 982             }
 983 
 984             if ( fn ) {
 985                 for (; i < length; i++ ) {
 986                     fn( elems[i], key, exec ? value.call( elems[i], i, fn( elems[i], key ) ) : value, pass );
 987                 }
 988             }
 989 
 990             chainable = 1;
 991         }
 992 
 993         return chainable ?
 994             elems :
 995 
 996             // Gets
 997             bulk ?
 998                 fn.call( elems ) :
 999                 length ? fn( elems[0], key ) : emptyGet;
1000     },
1001 
1002     now: function() {
1003         return ( new Date() ).getTime();
1004     }
1005 });

1007 /*
1008  * 在DOM加载完成调用事件的机制，通过Deferred对象实现
1009  */
1010 jQuery.ready.promise = function( obj ) {
1011     if ( !readyList ) {
1012 
1013         readyList = jQuery.Deferred();
1014 
1015         // Catch cases where $(document).ready() is called after the browser event has already occurred.
1016         // 处理$(document).ready()在浏览器事件已经出现后才调用的情况
1017         // we once tried to use readyState "interactive" here, but it caused issues like the one
1018         // 我们试过使用readyState "interactive"，但是发现一个问题，见url：
1019         // discovered by ChrisS here: http://bugs.jquery.com/ticket/12282#comment:15
1020         if ( document.readyState === "complete" ) {
1021             // Handle it asynchronously to allow scripts the opportunity to delay ready
1022             // 异步处理，给脚本提供延迟ready的机会
1023             setTimeout( jQuery.ready, 1 );
1024 
1025         // Standards-based browsers support DOMContentLoaded
1026         // 符合标准的浏览器支持DOMContentLoaded
1027         } else if ( document.addEventListener ) {
1028             // Use the handy event callback
1029             // 使用事件回调分发
1030             document.addEventListener( "DOMContentLoaded", DOMContentLoaded, false );
1031 
1032             // A fallback to window.onload, that will always work
1033             // 在window对象添加onload，肯定会起作用
1034             window.addEventListener( "load", jQuery.ready, false );
1035 
1036         // If IE event model is used
1037         // 如果使用IE事件模型
1038         } else {
1039             // Ensure firing before onload, maybe late but safe also for iframes
1040             // 确保在onload事件之前调用，或许会有延迟，但是对iframes也是安全的
1041             document.attachEvent( "onreadystatechange", DOMContentLoaded );
1042 
1043             // A fallback to window.onload, that will always work
1044             // 在window对象添加onload，肯定会起作用
1045             window.attachEvent( "onload", jQuery.ready );
1046 
1047             // If IE and not a frame
1048             // 如果是IE并且不是一个frame
1049             // continually check to see if the document is ready
1050             // 继续检查文档是否已经准备完成
1051             var top = false;
1052 
1053             try {
1054                 // 顶层的frame是否已经初始化完成，dom树是否构造完成
1055                 top = window.frameElement == null && document.documentElement;
1056             } catch(e) {}
1057 
1058             if ( top && top.doScroll ) {
1059                 (function doScrollCheck() {
1060                     if ( !jQuery.isReady ) {
1061 
1062                         try {
1063                             // Use the trick by Diego Perini
1064                             // http://javascript.nwbox.com/IEContentLoaded/
1065                             top.doScroll("left");
1066                         } catch(e) {
1067                             return setTimeout( doScrollCheck, 50 );
1068                         }
1069 
1070                         // and execute any waiting functions
1071                         // 执行任何等待的函数
1072                         jQuery.ready();
1073                     }
1074                 })();
1075             }
1076         }
1077     }
1078     return readyList.promise( obj );
1079 };

1081 // Populate the class2type map
1082 // 建立class2type的map，存放对象类型
1083 jQuery.each("Boolean Number String Function Array Date RegExp Object".split(" "), function(i, name) {
1084     class2type[ "[object " + name + "]" ] = name.toLowerCase();
1085 });
1086 
1087 // All jQuery objects should point back to these
1088 // 所有jQuery对象必须指向这个
1089 rootjQuery = jQuery(document);
1090 // String to Object options format cache
1091 var optionsCache = {};
1092 
1093 // Convert String-formatted options into Object-formatted ones and store in cache
1094 function createOptions( options ) {
1095     var object = optionsCache[ options ] = {};
1096     jQuery.each( options.split( core_rspace ), function( _, flag ) {
1097         object[ flag ] = true;
1098     });
1099     return object;
1100 }
1101 
1102 /*
1103  * Create a callback list using the following parameters:
1104  *
1105  *  options: an optional list of space-separated options that will change how
1106  *          the callback list behaves or a more traditional option object
1107  *
1108  * By default a callback list will act like an event callback list and can be
1109  * "fired" multiple times.
1110  *
1111  * Possible options:
1112  *
1113  *  once:           will ensure the callback list can only be fired once (like a Deferred)
1114  *
1115  *  memory:         will keep track of previous values and will call any callback added
1116  *                  after the list has been fired right away with the latest "memorized"
1117  *                  values (like a Deferred)
1118  *
1119  *  unique:         will ensure a callback can only be added once (no duplicate in the list)
1120  *
1121  *  stopOnFalse:    interrupt callings when a callback returns false
1122  *
1123  */
1124 jQuery.Callbacks = function( options ) {
1125 
1126     // Convert options from String-formatted to Object-formatted if needed
1127     // (we check in cache first)
1128     options = typeof options === "string" ?
1129         ( optionsCache[ options ] || createOptions( options ) ) :
1130         jQuery.extend( {}, options );
1131 
1132     var // Last fire value (for non-forgettable lists)
1133         memory,
1134         // Flag to know if list was already fired
1135         fired,
1136         // Flag to know if list is currently firing
1137         firing,
1138         // First callback to fire (used internally by add and fireWith)
1139         firingStart,
1140         // End of the loop when firing
1141         firingLength,
1142         // Index of currently firing callback (modified by remove if needed)
1143         firingIndex,
1144         // Actual callback list
1145         list = [],
1146         // Stack of fire calls for repeatable lists
1147         stack = !options.once && [],
1148         // Fire callbacks
1149         fire = function( data ) {
1150             memory = options.memory && data;
1151             fired = true;
1152             firingIndex = firingStart || 0;
1153             firingStart = 0;
1154             firingLength = list.length;
1155             firing = true;
1156             for ( ; list && firingIndex < firingLength; firingIndex++ ) {
1157                 if ( list[ firingIndex ].apply( data[ 0 ], data[ 1 ] ) === false && options.stopOnFalse ) {
1158                     memory = false; // To prevent further calls using add
1159                     break;
1160                 }
1161             }
1162             firing = false;
1163             if ( list ) {
1164                 if ( stack ) {
1165                     if ( stack.length ) {
1166                         fire( stack.shift() );
1167                     }
1168                 } else if ( memory ) {
1169                     list = [];
1170                 } else {
1171                     self.disable();
1172                 }
1173             }
1174         },
1175         // Actual Callbacks object
1176         self = {
1177             // Add a callback or a collection of callbacks to the list
1178             add: function() {
1179                 if ( list ) {
1180                     // First, we save the current length
1181                     var start = list.length;
1182                     (function add( args ) {
1183                         jQuery.each( args, function( _, arg ) {
1184                             var type = jQuery.type( arg );
1185                             if ( type === "function" && ( !options.unique || !self.has( arg ) ) ) {
1186                                 list.push( arg );
1187                             } else if ( arg && arg.length && type !== "string" ) {
1188                                 // Inspect recursively
1189                                 add( arg );
1190                             }
1191                         });
1192                     })( arguments );
1193                     // Do we need to add the callbacks to the
1194                     // current firing batch?
1195                     if ( firing ) {
1196                         firingLength = list.length;
1197                     // With memory, if we're not firing then
1198                     // we should call right away
1199                     } else if ( memory ) {
1200                         firingStart = start;
1201                         fire( memory );
1202                     }
1203                 }
1204                 return this;
1205             },
1206             // Remove a callback from the list
1207             remove: function() {
1208                 if ( list ) {
1209                     jQuery.each( arguments, function( _, arg ) {
1210                         var index;
1211                         while( ( index = jQuery.inArray( arg, list, index ) ) > -1 ) {
1212                             list.splice( index, 1 );
1213                             // Handle firing indexes
1214                             if ( firing ) {
1215                                 if ( index <= firingLength ) {
1216                                     firingLength--;
1217                                 }
1218                                 if ( index <= firingIndex ) {
1219                                     firingIndex--;
1220                                 }
1221                             }
1222                         }
1223                     });
1224                 }
1225                 return this;
1226             },
1227             // Control if a given callback is in the list
1228             has: function( fn ) {
1229                 return jQuery.inArray( fn, list ) > -1;
1230             },
1231             // Remove all callbacks from the list
1232             empty: function() {
1233                 list = [];
1234                 return this;
1235             },
1236             // Have the list do nothing anymore
1237             disable: function() {
1238                 list = stack = memory = undefined;
1239                 return this;
1240             },
1241             // Is it disabled?
1242             disabled: function() {
1243                 return !list;
1244             },
1245             // Lock the list in its current state
1246             lock: function() {
1247                 stack = undefined;
1248                 if ( !memory ) {
1249                     self.disable();
1250                 }
1251                 return this;
1252             },
1253             // Is it locked?
1254             locked: function() {
1255                 return !stack;
1256             },
1257             // Call all callbacks with the given context and arguments
1258             fireWith: function( context, args ) {
1259                 args = args || [];
1260                 args = [ context, args.slice ? args.slice() : args ];
1261                 if ( list && ( !fired || stack ) ) {
1262                     if ( firing ) {
1263                         stack.push( args );
1264                     } else {
1265                         fire( args );
1266                     }
1267                 }
1268                 return this;
1269             },
1270             // Call all the callbacks with the given arguments
1271             fire: function() {
1272                 self.fireWith( this, arguments );
1273                 return this;
1274             },
1275             // To know if the callbacks have already been called at least once
1276             fired: function() {
1277                 return !!fired;
1278             }
1279         };
1280 
1281     return self;
1282 };
1283 jQuery.extend({
1284 
1285     /*
1286      * 异步队列
1287      * 方法通过jQuery.Callbacks进行包装和维护
1288      */
1289     Deferred: function( func ) {
1290         var tuples = [
1291                 // action, add listener, listener list, final state
1292                 [ "resolve", "done", jQuery.Callbacks("once memory"), "resolved" ],
1293                 [ "reject", "fail", jQuery.Callbacks("once memory"), "rejected" ],
1294                 [ "notify", "progress", jQuery.Callbacks("memory") ]
1295             ],
1296             // 状态设置为“即将发生的”
1297             state = "pending",
1298             promise = {
1299                 // 返回状态
1300                 state: function() {
1301                     return state;
1302                 },
1303                 // 无论成功或者失败都调用
1304                 always: function() {
1305                     deferred.done( arguments ).fail( arguments );
1306                     return this;
1307                 },
1308                 // 便捷方法，同时传入成功、失败、通知的回调函数
1309                 then: function( /* fnDone, fnFail, fnProgress */ ) {
1310                     // 从arguments中获取状态对应的处理函数
1311                     var fns = arguments;
1312                     return jQuery.Deferred(function( newDefer ) {
1313                         // each() 方法用来让DOM循环结构更简单更不易出错。它会迭代jQuery对象中的每一个DOM元素。
1314                         // 每次回调函数执行时，会传递当前循环次数作为参数(从0开始计数)。
1315                         // 回调函数是在当前DOM元素为上下文的语境中触发的。因此关键字 this 总是指向这个元素。
1316                         // .each( function(index, Element) )
1317                         jQuery.each( tuples, function( i, tuple ) {
1318                             // i为遍历的索引号，tuple为遍历到的元素，tuple[ 0 ]为"resolve"、"reject"、"notify"。
1319                             var action = tuple[ 0 ],
1320                                 // fn为对应的处理函数
1321                                 fn = fns[ i ];
1322                             // deferred[ done | fail | progress ] for forwarding actions to newDefer
1323                             // 通过jQuery.Callbacks里的函数进行包装
1324                             deferred[ tuple[1] ]( jQuery.isFunction( fn ) ?
1325                                 function() {
1326                                     // returned为传入的函数的返回值，如果then中传入的函数的返回值也是deferred
1327                                     // 则继续通过promise()获取只读对象进行调用
1328                                     var returned = fn.apply( this, arguments );
1329                                     if ( returned && jQuery.isFunction( returned.promise ) ) {
1330                                         returned.promise()
1331                                             .done( newDefer.resolve )
1332                                             .fail( newDefer.reject )
1333                                             .progress( newDefer.notify );
1334                                     } else {
1335                                         newDefer[ action + "With" ]( this === deferred ? newDefer : this, [ returned ] );
1336                                     }
1337                                 } :
1338                                 newDefer[ action ]
1339                             );
1340                         });
1341                         fns = null;
1342                     }).promise();
1343                 },
1344                 // Get a promise for this deferred
1345                 // If obj is provided, the promise aspect is added to the object
1346                 // 获取deferred对象的只读版本
1347                 // 如果obj已经提供，promise被加到object中
1348                 promise: function( obj ) {
1349                     return typeof obj === "object" ? jQuery.extend( obj, promise ) : promise;
1350                 }
1351             },
1352             deferred = {};
1353 
1354         // Keep pipe for back-compat
1355         // 为pipe提供向后兼容性
1356         promise.pipe = promise.then;
1357 
1358         // Add list-specific methods
1359         // 添加指定的方法
1360         jQuery.each( tuples, function( i, tuple ) {
1361             // tuple[ 2 ]是jQuery.Callbacks里的队列
1362             var list = tuple[ 2 ],
1363                 stateString = tuple[ 3 ];
1364 
1365             // promise[ done | fail | progress ] = list.add
1366             promise[ tuple[1] ] = list.add;
1367 
1368             // Handle state
1369             // 处理状态
1370             if ( stateString ) {
1371                 list.add(function() {
1372                     // state = [ resolved | rejected ]
1373                     state = stateString;
1374 
1375                 /* 
1376                  * [ reject_list | resolve_list ].disable; progress_list.lock
1377                  * 位运算 XOR 由符号（^）表示，直接对二进制形式进行运算
1378                  * XOR 不同于 OR，当只有一个数位存放的是 1 时，它才返回 1。真值表如下：
1379                  *    --------------------+--------------------+-------
1380                  *     第一个数字中的数位 | 第二个数字中的数位 | 结果
1381                  *              1         |          1         |   0
1382                  *              1         |          0         |   1
1383                  *              0         |          1         |   1
1384                  *              0         |          0         |   0
1385                  *    --------------------+--------------------+-------
1386                  */
1387 
1388                 }, tuples[ i ^ 1 ][ 2 ].disable, tuples[ 2 ][ 2 ].lock );
1389             }
1390 
1391             // deferred[ resolve | reject | notify ] = list.fire
1392             deferred[ tuple[0] ] = list.fire;
1393             deferred[ tuple[0] + "With" ] = list.fireWith;
1394         });
1395 
1396         // Make the deferred a promise
1397         // 提供只读对象
1398         promise.promise( deferred );
1399 
1400         // Call given func if any
1401         // 调用提供的方法
1402         if ( func ) {
1403             func.call( deferred, deferred );
1404         }
1405 
1406         // All done!
1407         return deferred;
1408     },
1409 
1410     // Deferred helper
1411     when: function( subordinate /* , ..., subordinateN */ ) {
1412         var i = 0,
1413             resolveValues = core_slice.call( arguments ),
1414             length = resolveValues.length,
1415 
1416             // the count of uncompleted subordinates
1417             remaining = length !== 1 || ( subordinate && jQuery.isFunction( subordinate.promise ) ) ? length : 0,
1418 
1419             // the master Deferred. If resolveValues consist of only a single Deferred, just use that.
1420             deferred = remaining === 1 ? subordinate : jQuery.Deferred(),
1421 
1422             // Update function for both resolve and progress values
1423             updateFunc = function( i, contexts, values ) {
1424                 return function( value ) {
1425                     contexts[ i ] = this;
1426                     values[ i ] = arguments.length > 1 ? core_slice.call( arguments ) : value;
1427                     if( values === progressValues ) {
1428                         deferred.notifyWith( contexts, values );
1429                     } else if ( !( --remaining ) ) {
1430                         deferred.resolveWith( contexts, values );
1431                     }
1432                 };
1433             },
1434 
1435             progressValues, progressContexts, resolveContexts;
1436 
1437         // add listeners to Deferred subordinates; treat others as resolved
1438         if ( length > 1 ) {
1439             progressValues = new Array( length );
1440             progressContexts = new Array( length );
1441             resolveContexts = new Array( length );
1442             for ( ; i < length; i++ ) {
1443                 if ( resolveValues[ i ] && jQuery.isFunction( resolveValues[ i ].promise ) ) {
1444                     resolveValues[ i ].promise()
1445                         .done( updateFunc( i, resolveContexts, resolveValues ) )
1446                         .fail( deferred.reject )
1447                         .progress( updateFunc( i, progressContexts, progressValues ) );
1448                 } else {
1449                     --remaining;
1450                 }
1451             }
1452         }
1453 
1454         // if we're not waiting on anything, resolve the master
1455         if ( !remaining ) {
1456             deferred.resolveWith( resolveContexts, resolveValues );
1457         }
1458 
1459         return deferred.promise();
1460     }
1461 });

1729 var rbrace = /(?:\{[\s\S]*\}|\[[\s\S]*\])$/,
1730     rmultiDash = /([A-Z])/g;
1731 
1732 jQuery.extend({
1733     cache: {},
1734 
1735     deletedIds: [],
1736 
1737     // Please use with caution
1738     uuid: 0,
1739 
1740     // Unique for each copy of jQuery on the page
1741     // Non-digits removed to match rinlinejQuery
1742     expando: "jQuery" + ( jQuery.fn.jquery + Math.random() ).replace( /\D/g, "" ),
1743 
1744     // The following elements throw uncatchable exceptions if you
1745     // attempt to add expando properties to them.
1746     noData: {
1747         "embed": true,
1748         // Ban all objects except for Flash (which handle expandos)
1749         "object": "clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000",
1750         "applet": true
1751     },
1752 
1753     hasData: function( elem ) {
1754         elem = elem.nodeType ? jQuery.cache[ elem[jQuery.expando] ] : elem[ jQuery.expando ];
1755         return !!elem && !isEmptyDataObject( elem );
1756     },
1757 
1758     data: function( elem, name, data, pvt /* Internal Use Only */ ) {
1759         if ( !jQuery.acceptData( elem ) ) {
1760             return;
1761         }
1762 
1763         var thisCache, ret,
1764             internalKey = jQuery.expando,
1765             getByName = typeof name === "string",
1766 
1767             // We have to handle DOM nodes and JS objects differently because IE6-7
1768             // can't GC object references properly across the DOM-JS boundary
1769             isNode = elem.nodeType,
1770 
1771             // Only DOM nodes need the global jQuery cache; JS object data is
1772             // attached directly to the object so GC can occur automatically
1773             cache = isNode ? jQuery.cache : elem,
1774 
1775             // Only defining an ID for JS objects if its cache already exists allows
1776             // the code to shortcut on the same path as a DOM node with no cache
1777             id = isNode ? elem[ internalKey ] : elem[ internalKey ] && internalKey;
1778 
1779         // Avoid doing any more work than we need to when trying to get data on an
1780         // object that has no data at all
1781         if ( (!id || !cache[id] || (!pvt && !cache[id].data)) && getByName && data === undefined ) {
1782             return;
1783         }
1784 
1785         if ( !id ) {
1786             // Only DOM nodes need a new unique ID for each element since their data
1787             // ends up in the global cache
1788             if ( isNode ) {
1789                 elem[ internalKey ] = id = jQuery.deletedIds.pop() || ++jQuery.uuid;
1790             } else {
1791                 id = internalKey;
1792             }
1793         }
1794 
1795         if ( !cache[ id ] ) {
1796             cache[ id ] = {};
1797 
1798             // Avoids exposing jQuery metadata on plain JS objects when the object
1799             // is serialized using JSON.stringify
1800             if ( !isNode ) {
1801                 cache[ id ].toJSON = jQuery.noop;
1802             }
1803         }
1804 
1805         // An object can be passed to jQuery.data instead of a key/value pair; this gets
1806         // shallow copied over onto the existing cache
1807         if ( typeof name === "object" || typeof name === "function" ) {
1808             if ( pvt ) {
1809                 cache[ id ] = jQuery.extend( cache[ id ], name );
1810             } else {
1811                 cache[ id ].data = jQuery.extend( cache[ id ].data, name );
1812             }
1813         }
1814 
1815         thisCache = cache[ id ];
1816 
1817         // jQuery data() is stored in a separate object inside the object's internal data
1818         // cache in order to avoid key collisions between internal data and user-defined
1819         // data.
1820         if ( !pvt ) {
1821             if ( !thisCache.data ) {
1822                 thisCache.data = {};
1823             }
1824 
1825             thisCache = thisCache.data;
1826         }
1827 
1828         if ( data !== undefined ) {
1829             thisCache[ jQuery.camelCase( name ) ] = data;
1830         }
1831 
1832         // Check for both converted-to-camel and non-converted data property names
1833         // If a data property was specified
1834         if ( getByName ) {
1835 
1836             // First Try to find as-is property data
1837             ret = thisCache[ name ];
1838 
1839             // Test for null|undefined property data
1840             if ( ret == null ) {
1841 
1842                 // Try to find the camelCased property
1843                 ret = thisCache[ jQuery.camelCase( name ) ];
1844             }
1845         } else {
1846             ret = thisCache;
1847         }
1848 
1849         return ret;
1850     },
1851 
1852     removeData: function( elem, name, pvt /* Internal Use Only */ ) {
1853         if ( !jQuery.acceptData( elem ) ) {
1854             return;
1855         }
1856 
1857         var thisCache, i, l,
1858 
1859             isNode = elem.nodeType,
1860 
1861             // See jQuery.data for more information
1862             cache = isNode ? jQuery.cache : elem,
1863             id = isNode ? elem[ jQuery.expando ] : jQuery.expando;
1864 
1865         // If there is already no cache entry for this object, there is no
1866         // purpose in continuing
1867         if ( !cache[ id ] ) {
1868             return;
1869         }
1870 
1871         if ( name ) {
1872 
1873             thisCache = pvt ? cache[ id ] : cache[ id ].data;
1874 
1875             if ( thisCache ) {
1876 
1877                 // Support array or space separated string names for data keys
1878                 if ( !jQuery.isArray( name ) ) {
1879 
1880                     // try the string as a key before any manipulation
1881                     if ( name in thisCache ) {
1882                         name = [ name ];
1883                     } else {
1884 
1885                         // split the camel cased version by spaces unless a key with the spaces exists
1886                         name = jQuery.camelCase( name );
1887                         if ( name in thisCache ) {
1888                             name = [ name ];
1889                         } else {
1890                             name = name.split(" ");
1891                         }
1892                     }
1893                 }
1894 
1895                 for ( i = 0, l = name.length; i < l; i++ ) {
1896                     delete thisCache[ name[i] ];
1897                 }
1898 
1899                 // If there is no data left in the cache, we want to continue
1900                 // and let the cache object itself get destroyed
1901                 if ( !( pvt ? isEmptyDataObject : jQuery.isEmptyObject )( thisCache ) ) {
1902                     return;
1903                 }
1904             }
1905         }
1906 
1907         // See jQuery.data for more information
1908         if ( !pvt ) {
1909             delete cache[ id ].data;
1910 
1911             // Don't destroy the parent cache unless the internal data object
1912             // had been the only thing left in it
1913             if ( !isEmptyDataObject( cache[ id ] ) ) {
1914                 return;
1915             }
1916         }
1917 
1918         // Destroy the cache
1919         if ( isNode ) {
1920             jQuery.cleanData( [ elem ], true );
1921 
1922         // Use delete when supported for expandos or `cache` is not a window per isWindow (#10080)
1923         } else if ( jQuery.support.deleteExpando || cache != cache.window ) {
1924             delete cache[ id ];
1925 
1926         // When all else fails, null
1927         } else {
1928             cache[ id ] = null;
1929         }
1930     },
1931 
1932     // For internal use only.
1933     _data: function( elem, name, data ) {
1934         return jQuery.data( elem, name, data, true );
1935     },
1936 
1937     // A method for determining if a DOM node can handle the data expando
1938     acceptData: function( elem ) {
1939         var noData = elem.nodeName && jQuery.noData[ elem.nodeName.toLowerCase() ];
1940 
1941         // nodes accept data unless otherwise specified; rejection can be conditional
1942         return !noData || noData !== true && elem.getAttribute("classid") === noData;
1943     }
1944 });

1946 jQuery.fn.extend({
1947     data: function( key, value ) {
1948         var parts, part, attr, name, l,
1949             elem = this[0],
1950             i = 0,
1951             data = null;
1952 
1953         // Gets all values
1954         if ( key === undefined ) {
1955             if ( this.length ) {
1956                 data = jQuery.data( elem );
1957 
1958                 if ( elem.nodeType === 1 && !jQuery._data( elem, "parsedAttrs" ) ) {
1959                     attr = elem.attributes;
1960                     for ( l = attr.length; i < l; i++ ) {
1961                         name = attr[i].name;
1962 
1963                         if ( name.indexOf( "data-" ) === 0 ) {
1964                             name = jQuery.camelCase( name.substring(5) );
1965 
1966                             dataAttr( elem, name, data[ name ] );
1967                         }
1968                     }
1969                     jQuery._data( elem, "parsedAttrs", true );
1970                 }
1971             }
1972 
1973             return data;
1974         }
1975 
1976         // Sets multiple values
1977         if ( typeof key === "object" ) {
1978             return this.each(function() {
1979                 jQuery.data( this, key );
1980             });
1981         }
1982 
1983         parts = key.split( ".", 2 );
1984         parts[1] = parts[1] ? "." + parts[1] : "";
1985         part = parts[1] + "!";
1986 
1987         return jQuery.access( this, function( value ) {
1988 
1989             if ( value === undefined ) {
1990                 data = this.triggerHandler( "getData" + part, [ parts[0] ] );
1991 
1992                 // Try to fetch any internally stored data first
1993                 if ( data === undefined && elem ) {
1994                     data = jQuery.data( elem, key );
1995                     data = dataAttr( elem, key, data );
1996                 }
1997 
1998                 return data === undefined && parts[1] ?
1999                     this.data( parts[0] ) :
2000                     data;
2001             }
2002 
2003             parts[1] = value;
2004             this.each(function() {
2005                 var self = jQuery( this );
2006 
2007                 self.triggerHandler( "setData" + part, parts );
2008                 jQuery.data( this, key, value );
2009                 self.triggerHandler( "changeData" + part, parts );
2010             });
2011         }, null, value, arguments.length > 1, null, false );
2012     },
2013 
2014     removeData: function( key ) {
2015         return this.each(function() {
2016             jQuery.removeData( this, key );
2017         });
2018     }
2019 });
2020 
2021 function dataAttr( elem, key, data ) {
2022     // If nothing was found internally, try to fetch any
2023     // data from the HTML5 data-* attribute
2024     if ( data === undefined && elem.nodeType === 1 ) {
2025 
2026         var name = "data-" + key.replace( rmultiDash, "-$1" ).toLowerCase();
2027 
2028         data = elem.getAttribute( name );
2029 
2030         if ( typeof data === "string" ) {
2031             try {
2032                 data = data === "true" ? true :
2033                 data === "false" ? false :
2034                 data === "null" ? null :
2035                 // Only convert to a number if it doesn't change the string
2036                 +data + "" === data ? +data :
2037                 rbrace.test( data ) ? jQuery.parseJSON( data ) :
2038                     data;
2039             } catch( e ) {}
2040 
2041             // Make sure we set the data so it isn't changed later
2042             jQuery.data( elem, key, data );
2043 
2044         } else {
2045             data = undefined;
2046         }
2047     }
2048 
2049     return data;
2050 }
2051 
2052 // checks a cache object for emptiness
2053 function isEmptyDataObject( obj ) {
2054     var name;
2055     for ( name in obj ) {
2056 
2057         // if the public data object is empty, the private is still empty
2058         if ( name === "data" && jQuery.isEmptyObject( obj[name] ) ) {
2059             continue;
2060         }
2061         if ( name !== "toJSON" ) {
2062             return false;
2063         }
2064     }
2065 
2066     return true;
2067 }
2068 jQuery.extend({
2069     queue: function( elem, type, data ) {
2070         var queue;
2071 
2072         if ( elem ) {
2073             type = ( type || "fx" ) + "queue";
2074             queue = jQuery._data( elem, type );
2075 
2076             // Speed up dequeue by getting out quickly if this is just a lookup
2077             if ( data ) {
2078                 if ( !queue || jQuery.isArray(data) ) {
2079                     queue = jQuery._data( elem, type, jQuery.makeArray(data) );
2080                 } else {
2081                     queue.push( data );
2082                 }
2083             }
2084             return queue || [];
2085         }
2086     },
2087 
2088     dequeue: function( elem, type ) {
2089         type = type || "fx";
2090 
2091         var queue = jQuery.queue( elem, type ),
2092             startLength = queue.length,
2093             fn = queue.shift(),
2094             hooks = jQuery._queueHooks( elem, type ),
2095             next = function() {
2096                 jQuery.dequeue( elem, type );
2097             };
2098 
2099         // If the fx queue is dequeued, always remove the progress sentinel
2100         if ( fn === "inprogress" ) {
2101             fn = queue.shift();
2102             startLength--;
2103         }
2104 
2105         if ( fn ) {
2106 
2107             // Add a progress sentinel to prevent the fx queue from being
2108             // automatically dequeued
2109             if ( type === "fx" ) {
2110                 queue.unshift( "inprogress" );
2111             }
2112 
2113             // clear up the last queue stop function
2114             delete hooks.stop;
2115             fn.call( elem, next, hooks );
2116         }
2117 
2118         if ( !startLength && hooks ) {
2119             hooks.empty.fire();
2120         }
2121     },
2122 
2123     // not intended for public consumption - generates a queueHooks object, or returns the current one
2124     _queueHooks: function( elem, type ) {
2125         var key = type + "queueHooks";
2126         return jQuery._data( elem, key ) || jQuery._data( elem, key, {
2127             empty: jQuery.Callbacks("once memory").add(function() {
2128                 jQuery.removeData( elem, type + "queue", true );
2129                 jQuery.removeData( elem, key, true );
2130             })
2131         });
2132     }
2133 });

2135 jQuery.fn.extend({
2136     queue: function( type, data ) {
2137         var setter = 2;
2138 
2139         if ( typeof type !== "string" ) {
2140             data = type;
2141             type = "fx";
2142             setter--;
2143         }
2144 
2145         if ( arguments.length < setter ) {
2146             return jQuery.queue( this[0], type );
2147         }
2148 
2149         return data === undefined ?
2150             this :
2151             this.each(function() {
2152                 var queue = jQuery.queue( this, type, data );
2153 
2154                 // ensure a hooks for this queue
2155                 jQuery._queueHooks( this, type );
2156 
2157                 if ( type === "fx" && queue[0] !== "inprogress" ) {
2158                     jQuery.dequeue( this, type );
2159                 }
2160             });
2161     },
2162     dequeue: function( type ) {

2167     // Based off of the plugin by Clint Helfers, with permission.
2168     // http://blindsignals.com/index.php/2009/07/jquery-delay/
2169     delay: function( time, type ) {
2170         time = jQuery.fx ? jQuery.fx.speeds[ time ] || time : time;
2171         type = type || "fx";
2172 
2173         return this.queue( type, function( next, hooks ) {
2174             var timeout = setTimeout( next, time );
2175             hooks.stop = function() {
2176                 clearTimeout( timeout );
2177             };
2178         });
2179     },
2180     clearQueue: function( type ) {
2181         return this.queue( type || "fx", [] );
2182     },
2183     // Get a promise resolved when queues of a certain type
2184     // are emptied (fx is the type by default)
2185     promise: function( type, obj ) {
2186         var tmp,
2187             count = 1,
2188             defer = jQuery.Deferred(),
2189             elements = this,
2190             i = this.length,
2191             resolve = function() {
2192                 if ( !( --count ) ) {
2193                     defer.resolveWith( elements, [ elements ] );
2194                 }
2195             };
2196 
2197         if ( typeof type !== "string" ) {
2198             obj = type;
2199             type = undefined;
2200         }
2201         type = type || "fx";
2202 
2203         while( i-- ) {
2204             tmp = jQuery._data( elements[ i ], type + "queueHooks" );
2205             if ( tmp && tmp.empty ) {
2206                 count++;
2207                 tmp.empty.add( resolve );
2208             }
2209         }
2210         resolve();
2211         return defer.promise( obj );
2212     }

2254             return this.each(function( j ) {
2255                 jQuery( this ).addClass( value.call(this, j, this.className) );
2256             });
2257         }
2258 
2259         if ( value && typeof value === "string" ) {
2260             classNames = value.split( core_rspace );
2261

2263                 elem = this[ i ];

2266                     if ( !elem.className && classNames.length === 1 ) {
2267                         elem.className = value;
2268

2271

2273                             if ( !~setClass.indexOf( " " + classNames[ c ] + " " ) ) {
2274                                 setClass += classNames[ c ] + " ";

2278                     }

2287         var removes, className, elem, c, cl, i, l;
2288 
2289         if ( jQuery.isFunction( value ) ) {
2290             return this.each(function( j ) {
2291                 jQuery( this ).removeClass( value.call(this, j, this.className) );
2292             });
2293         }
2294         if ( (value && typeof value === "string") || value === undefined ) {
2295             removes = ( value || "" ).split( core_rspace );
2296 
2297             for ( i = 0, l = this.length; i < l; i++ ) {
2298                 elem = this[ i ];
2299                 if ( elem.nodeType === 1 && elem.className ) {
2300 
2301                     className = (" " + elem.className + " ").replace( rclass, " " );
2302 
2303                     // loop over each item in the removal list
2304                     for ( c = 0, cl = removes.length; c < cl; c++ ) {
2305                         // Remove until there is nothing to remove,
2306                         while ( className.indexOf(" " + removes[ c ] + " ") > -1 ) {
2307                             className = className.replace( " " + removes[ c ] + " " , " " );
2308                         }
2309                     }
2310                     elem.className = value ? jQuery.trim( className ) : "";
2311                 }
2312             }

2318     toggleClass: function( value, stateVal ) {
2319         var type = typeof value,
2320             isBool = typeof stateVal === "boolean";
2321 
2322         if ( jQuery.isFunction( value ) ) {
2323             return this.each(function( i ) {
2324                 jQuery( this ).toggleClass( value.call(this, i, this.className, stateVal), stateVal );
2325             });
2326         }
2327 
2328         return this.each(function() {
2329             if ( type === "string" ) {
2330                 // toggle individual class names
2331                 var className,
2332                     i = 0,
2333                     self = jQuery( this ),
2334                     state = stateVal,
2335                     classNames = value.split( core_rspace );
2336 
2337                 while ( (className = classNames[ i++ ]) ) {
2338                     // check each className given, space separated list
2339                     state = isBool ? state : !self.hasClass( className );
2340                     self[ state ? "addClass" : "removeClass" ]( className );
2341                 }
2342 
2343             } else if ( type === "undefined" || type === "boolean" ) {
2344                 if ( this.className ) {
2345                     // store className if set
2346                     jQuery._data( this, "__className__", this.className );
2347                 }
2348

2350                 this.className = this.className || value === false ? "" : jQuery._data( this, "__className__" ) || "";
2351             }

2355     hasClass: function( selector ) {
2356         var className = " " + selector + " ",
2357             i = 0,
2358             l = this.length;
2359         for ( ; i < l; i++ ) {
2360             if ( this[i].nodeType === 1 && (" " + this[i].className + " ").replace(rclass, " ").indexOf( className ) > -1 ) {
2361                 return true;
2362             }
2363         }
