2368     val: function( value ) {
2369         var hooks, ret, isFunction,
2370             elem = this[0];
2371 
2372         if ( !arguments.length ) {
2373             if ( elem ) {
2374                 hooks = jQuery.valHooks[ elem.type ] || jQuery.valHooks[ elem.nodeName.toLowerCase() ];
2375 
2376                 if ( hooks && "get" in hooks && (ret = hooks.get( elem, "value" )) !== undefined ) {
2377                     return ret;
2378                 }
2379 
2380                 ret = elem.value;
2381 
2382                 return typeof ret === "string" ?
2383                     // handle most common string cases
2384                     ret.replace(rreturn, "") :
2385                     // handle cases where value is null/undef or number
2386                     ret == null ? "" : ret;
2387             }
2388 
2389             return;
2390         }
2391 
2392         isFunction = jQuery.isFunction( value );
2393 
2394         return this.each(function( i ) {
2395             var val,
2396                 self = jQuery(this);
2397 
2398             if ( this.nodeType !== 1 ) {
2399                 return;
2400             }
2401 
2402             if ( isFunction ) {
2403                 val = value.call( this, i, self.val() );
2404             } else {
2405                 val = value;
2406             }
2407 
2408             // Treat null/undefined as ""; convert numbers to string
2409             if ( val == null ) {
2410                 val = "";
2411             } else if ( typeof val === "number" ) {
2412                 val += "";
2413             } else if ( jQuery.isArray( val ) ) {
2414                 val = jQuery.map(val, function ( value ) {
2415                     return value == null ? "" : value + "";
2416                 });
2417             }
2418 
2419             hooks = jQuery.valHooks[ this.type ] || jQuery.valHooks[ this.nodeName.toLowerCase() ];
2420 
2421             // If set returns undefined, fall back to normal setting
2422             if ( !hooks || !("set" in hooks) || hooks.set( this, val, "value" ) === undefined ) {
2423                 this.value = val;
2424             }
2425         });
2426     }

2429 jQuery.extend({
2430     valHooks: {
2431         option: {
2432             get: function( elem ) {
2433                 // attributes.value is undefined in Blackberry 4.7 but
2434                 // uses .value. See #6932
2435                 var val = elem.attributes.value;
2436                 return !val || val.specified ? elem.value : elem.text;
2437             }
2438         },
2439         select: {
2440             get: function( elem ) {
2441                 var value, i, max, option,
2442                     index = elem.selectedIndex,
2443                     values = [],
2444                     options = elem.options,
2445                     one = elem.type === "select-one";
2446 
2447                 // Nothing was selected
2448                 if ( index < 0 ) {
2449                     return null;
2450                 }
2451 
2452                 // Loop through all the selected options
2453                 i = one ? index : 0;
2454                 max = one ? index + 1 : options.length;
2455                 for ( ; i < max; i++ ) {
2456                     option = options[ i ];
2457 
2458                     // Don't return options that are disabled or in a disabled optgroup
2459                     if ( option.selected && (jQuery.support.optDisabled ? !option.disabled : option.getAttribute("disabled") === null) &&
2460                             (!option.parentNode.disabled || !jQuery.nodeName( option.parentNode, "optgroup" )) ) {
2461 
2462                         // Get the specific value for the option
2463                         value = jQuery( option ).val();
2464 
2465                         // We don't need an array for one selects
2466                         if ( one ) {
2467                             return value;
2468                         }
2469 
2470                         // Multi-Selects return an array
2471                         values.push( value );
2472                     }
2473                 }
2474 
2475                 // Fixes Bug #2551 -- select.val() broken in IE after form.reset()
2476                 if ( one && !values.length && options.length ) {
2477                     return jQuery( options[ index ] ).val();
2478                 }
2479 
2480                 return values;
2481             },
2482 
2483             set: function( elem, value ) {
2484                 var values = jQuery.makeArray( value );
2485 
2486                 jQuery(elem).find("option").each(function() {
2487                     this.selected = jQuery.inArray( jQuery(this).val(), values ) >= 0;
2488                 });
2489 
2490                 if ( !values.length ) {
2491                     elem.selectedIndex = -1;
2492                 }
2493                 return values;
2494             }
2495         }
2496     },

2498     // Unused in 1.8, left in so attrFn-stabbers won't die; remove in 1.9
2499     attrFn: {},
2500 
2501     attr: function( elem, name, value, pass ) {
2502         var ret, hooks, notxml,
2503             nType = elem.nodeType;
2504 
2505         // don't get/set attributes on text, comment and attribute nodes
2506         if ( !elem || nType === 3 || nType === 8 || nType === 2 ) {
2507             return;
2508         }
2509 
2510         if ( pass && jQuery.isFunction( jQuery.fn[ name ] ) ) {
2511             return jQuery( elem )[ name ]( value );
2512         }
2513 
2514         // Fallback to prop when attributes are not supported
2515         if ( typeof elem.getAttribute === "undefined" ) {
2516             return jQuery.prop( elem, name, value );
2517         }
2518 
2519         notxml = nType !== 1 || !jQuery.isXMLDoc( elem );
2520 
2521         // All attributes are lowercase
2522         // Grab necessary hook if one is defined
2523         if ( notxml ) {
2524             name = name.toLowerCase();
2525             hooks = jQuery.attrHooks[ name ] || ( rboolean.test( name ) ? boolHook : nodeHook );
2526         }
2527 
2528         if ( value !== undefined ) {
2529 
2530             if ( value === null ) {
2531                 jQuery.removeAttr( elem, name );
2532                 return;
2533 
2534             } else if ( hooks && "set" in hooks && notxml && (ret = hooks.set( elem, value, name )) !== undefined ) {
2535                 return ret;
2536 
2537             } else {
2538                 elem.setAttribute( name, "" + value );
2539                 return value;
2540             }
2541 
2542         } else if ( hooks && "get" in hooks && notxml && (ret = hooks.get( elem, name )) !== null ) {
2543             return ret;
2544 
2545         } else {
2546 
2547             ret = elem.getAttribute( name );
2548 
2549             // Non-existent attributes return null, we normalize to undefined
2550             return ret === null ?
2551                 undefined :
2552                 ret;
2553         }
2554     },

2556     removeAttr: function( elem, value ) {
2557         var propName, attrNames, name, isBool,
2558             i = 0;
2559 
2560         if ( value && elem.nodeType === 1 ) {
2561 
2562             attrNames = value.split( core_rspace );
2563 
2564             for ( ; i < attrNames.length; i++ ) {
2565                 name = attrNames[ i ];
2566 
2567                 if ( name ) {
2568                     propName = jQuery.propFix[ name ] || name;
2569                     isBool = rboolean.test( name );
2570 
2571                     // See #9699 for explanation of this approach (setting first, then removal)
2572                     // Do not do this for boolean attributes (see #10870)
2573                     if ( !isBool ) {
2574                         jQuery.attr( elem, name, "" );
2575                     }
2576                     elem.removeAttribute( getSetAttribute ? name : propName );
2577 
2578                     // Set corresponding property to false for boolean attributes
2579                     if ( isBool && propName in elem ) {
2580                         elem[ propName ] = false;
2581                     }
2582                 }
2583             }
2584         }

2587     attrHooks: {
2588         type: {
2589             set: function( elem, value ) {
2590                 // We can't allow the type property to be changed (since it causes problems in IE)
2591                 if ( rtype.test( elem.nodeName ) && elem.parentNode ) {
2592                     jQuery.error( "type property can't be changed" );
2593                 } else if ( !jQuery.support.radioValue && value === "radio" && jQuery.nodeName(elem, "input") ) {
2594                     // Setting the type on a radio button after the value resets the value in IE6-9
2595                     // Reset value to it's default in case type is set after value
2596                     // This is for element creation
2597                     var val = elem.value;
2598                     elem.setAttribute( "type", value );
2599                     if ( val ) {
2600                         elem.value = val;
2601                     }
2602                     return value;
2603                 }
2604             }
2605         },
2606         // Use the value property for back compat
2607         // Use the nodeHook for button elements in IE6/7 (#1954)
2608         value: {
2609             get: function( elem, name ) {
2610                 if ( nodeHook && jQuery.nodeName( elem, "button" ) ) {
2611                     return nodeHook.get( elem, name );
2612                 }
2613                 return name in elem ?
2614                     elem.value :
2615                     null;
2616             },
2617             set: function( elem, value, name ) {
2618                 if ( nodeHook && jQuery.nodeName( elem, "button" ) ) {
2619                     return nodeHook.set( elem, value, name );
2620                 }
2621                 // Does not return so that setAttribute is also used
2622                 elem.value = value;
2623             }
2624         }
2625     },

2628         tabindex: "tabIndex",
2629         readonly: "readOnly",

2633         cellspacing: "cellSpacing",

2642     prop: function( elem, name, value ) {
2643         var ret, hooks, notxml,
2644             nType = elem.nodeType;
2645 
2646         // don't get/set properties on text, comment and attribute nodes
2647         if ( !elem || nType === 3 || nType === 8 || nType === 2 ) {
2648             return;
2649         }
2650 
2651         notxml = nType !== 1 || !jQuery.isXMLDoc( elem );
2652 
2653         if ( notxml ) {
2654             // Fix name and attach hooks
2655             name = jQuery.propFix[ name ] || name;
2656             hooks = jQuery.propHooks[ name ];
2657         }
2658 
2659         if ( value !== undefined ) {
2660             if ( hooks && "set" in hooks && (ret = hooks.set( elem, value, name )) !== undefined ) {
2661                 return ret;
2662 
2663             } else {
2664                 return ( elem[ name ] = value );
2665             }
2666 
2667         } else {
2668             if ( hooks && "get" in hooks && (ret = hooks.get( elem, name )) !== null ) {
2669                 return ret;
2670 
2671             } else {
2672                 return elem[ name ];
2673             }
2674         }
2675     },

2677     propHooks: {
2678         tabIndex: {
2679             get: function( elem ) {

2681                 // http://fluidproject.org/blog/2008/01/09/getting-setting-and-removing-tabindex-values-with-javascript/
2682                 var attributeNode = elem.getAttributeNode("tabindex");
2683 
2684                 return attributeNode && attributeNode.specified ?
2685                     parseInt( attributeNode.value, 10 ) :
2686                     rfocusable.test( elem.nodeName ) || rclickable.test( elem.nodeName ) && elem.href ?
2687                         0 :
2688                         undefined;
2689             }
2690         }

2694 // Hook for boolean attributes

2696     get: function( elem, name ) {

2698         // Fall back to attribute presence where some booleans are not supported
2699         var attrNode,
2700             property = jQuery.prop( elem, name );
2701         return property === true || typeof property !== "boolean" && ( attrNode = elem.getAttributeNode(name) ) && attrNode.nodeValue !== false ?
2702             name.toLowerCase() :
2703             undefined;
2704     },
2705     set: function( elem, value, name ) {
2706         var propName;
2707         if ( value === false ) {
2708             // Remove boolean attributes when set to false
2709             jQuery.removeAttr( elem, name );
2710         } else {
2711             // value is true since we know at this point it's type boolean and not false
2712             // Set boolean attributes to the same name and set the DOM property
2713             propName = jQuery.propFix[ name ] || name;
2714             if ( propName in elem ) {
2715                 // Only set the IDL specifically if it already exists on the element
2716                 elem[ propName ] = true;
2717             }
2718 
2719             elem.setAttribute( name, name.toLowerCase() );
2720         }
2721         return name;
2722     }

2852 var rformElems = /^(?:textarea|input|select)$/i,
2853     rtypenamespace = /^([^\.]*|)(?:\.(.+)|)$/,
2854     rhoverHack = /(?:^|\s)hover(\.\S+|)\b/,
2855     rkeyEvent = /^key/,
2856     rmouseEvent = /^(?:mouse|contextmenu)|click/,
2857     rfocusMorph = /^(?:focusinfocus|focusoutblur)$/,
2858     hoverHack = function( events ) {
2859         return jQuery.event.special.hover ? events : events.replace( rhoverHack, "mouseenter$1 mouseleave$1" );
2860     };

2862 /*
2863  * Helper functions for managing events -- not part of the public interface.
2864  * Props to Dean Edwards' addEvent library for many of the ideas.
2865  */
2866 jQuery.event = {
2867 
2868     add: function( elem, types, handler, data, selector ) {
2869 
2870         var elemData, eventHandle, events,
2871             t, tns, type, namespaces, handleObj,
2872             handleObjIn, handlers, special;
2873 
2874         // Don't attach events to noData or text/comment nodes (allow plain objects tho)
2875         if ( elem.nodeType === 3 || elem.nodeType === 8 || !types || !handler || !(elemData = jQuery._data( elem )) ) {
2876             return;
2877         }
2878 
2879         // Caller can pass in an object of custom data in lieu of the handler
2880         if ( handler.handler ) {
2881             handleObjIn = handler;
2882             handler = handleObjIn.handler;
2883             selector = handleObjIn.selector;
2884         }
2885 
2886         // Make sure that the handler has a unique ID, used to find/remove it later
2887         if ( !handler.guid ) {
2888             handler.guid = jQuery.guid++;
2889         }
2890 
2891         // Init the element's event structure and main handler, if this is the first
2892         events = elemData.events;
2893         if ( !events ) {
2894             elemData.events = events = {};
2895         }
2896         eventHandle = elemData.handle;
2897         if ( !eventHandle ) {
2898             elemData.handle = eventHandle = function( e ) {
2899                 // Discard the second event of a jQuery.event.trigger() and
2900                 // when an event is called after a page has unloaded
2901                 return typeof jQuery !== "undefined" && (!e || jQuery.event.triggered !== e.type) ?
2902                     jQuery.event.dispatch.apply( eventHandle.elem, arguments ) :
2903                     undefined;
2904             };
2905             // Add elem as a property of the handle fn to prevent a memory leak with IE non-native events
2906             eventHandle.elem = elem;
2907         }
2908 
2909         // Handle multiple events separated by a space
2910         // jQuery(...).bind("mouseover mouseout", fn);
2911         types = jQuery.trim( hoverHack(types) ).split( " " );
2912         for ( t = 0; t < types.length; t++ ) {
2913 
2914             tns = rtypenamespace.exec( types[t] ) || [];
2915             type = tns[1];
2916             namespaces = ( tns[2] || "" ).split( "." ).sort();
2917 
2918             // If event changes its type, use the special event handlers for the changed type
2919             special = jQuery.event.special[ type ] || {};
2920 
2921             // If selector defined, determine special event api type, otherwise given type
2922             type = ( selector ? special.delegateType : special.bindType ) || type;
2923 
2924             // Update special based on newly reset type
2925             special = jQuery.event.special[ type ] || {};
2926 
2927             // handleObj is passed to all event handlers
2928             handleObj = jQuery.extend({
2929                 type: type,
2930                 origType: tns[1],
2931                 data: data,
2932                 handler: handler,
2933                 guid: handler.guid,
2934                 selector: selector,
2935                 namespace: namespaces.join(".")
2936             }, handleObjIn );
2937 
2938             // Init the event handler queue if we're the first
2939             handlers = events[ type ];
2940             if ( !handlers ) {
2941                 handlers = events[ type ] = [];
2942                 handlers.delegateCount = 0;
2943 
2944                 // Only use addEventListener/attachEvent if the special events handler returns false
2945                 if ( !special.setup || special.setup.call( elem, data, namespaces, eventHandle ) === false ) {
2946                     // Bind the global event handler to the element
2947                     if ( elem.addEventListener ) {
2948                         elem.addEventListener( type, eventHandle, false );
2949 
2950                     } else if ( elem.attachEvent ) {
2951                         elem.attachEvent( "on" + type, eventHandle );
2952                     }
2953                 }
2954             }
2955 
2956             if ( special.add ) {
2957                 special.add.call( elem, handleObj );
2958 
2959                 if ( !handleObj.handler.guid ) {
2960                     handleObj.handler.guid = handler.guid;
2961                 }
2962             }
2963 
2964             // Add to the element's handler list, delegates in front
2965             if ( selector ) {
2966                 handlers.splice( handlers.delegateCount++, 0, handleObj );
2967             } else {
2968                 handlers.push( handleObj );
2969             }
2970 
2971             // Keep track of which events have ever been used, for event optimization
2972             jQuery.event.global[ type ] = true;
2973         }
2974 
2975         // Nullify elem to prevent memory leaks in IE
2976         elem = null;
2977     },
2978 
2979     global: {},
2980 
2981     // Detach an event or set of events from an element
2982     remove: function( elem, types, handler, selector, mappedTypes ) {
2983 
2984         var t, tns, type, origType, namespaces, origCount,
2985             j, events, special, eventType, handleObj,
2986             elemData = jQuery.hasData( elem ) && jQuery._data( elem );
2987 
2988         if ( !elemData || !(events = elemData.events) ) {
2989             return;
2990         }
2991 
2992         // Once for each type.namespace in types; type may be omitted
2993         types = jQuery.trim( hoverHack( types || "" ) ).split(" ");
2994         for ( t = 0; t < types.length; t++ ) {
2995             tns = rtypenamespace.exec( types[t] ) || [];
2996             type = origType = tns[1];
2997             namespaces = tns[2];
2998 
2999             // Unbind all events (on this namespace, if provided) for the element
3000             if ( !type ) {
3001                 for ( type in events ) {
3002                     jQuery.event.remove( elem, type + types[ t ], handler, selector, true );
3003                 }
3004                 continue;
3005             }
3006 
3007             special = jQuery.event.special[ type ] || {};
3008             type = ( selector? special.delegateType : special.bindType ) || type;
3009             eventType = events[ type ] || [];
3010             origCount = eventType.length;
3011             namespaces = namespaces ? new RegExp("(^|\\.)" + namespaces.split(".").sort().join("\\.(?:.*\\.|)") + "(\\.|$)") : null;
3012 
3013             // Remove matching events
3014             for ( j = 0; j < eventType.length; j++ ) {
3015                 handleObj = eventType[ j ];
3016 
3017                 if ( ( mappedTypes || origType === handleObj.origType ) &&
3018                      ( !handler || handler.guid === handleObj.guid ) &&
3019                      ( !namespaces || namespaces.test( handleObj.namespace ) ) &&
3020                      ( !selector || selector === handleObj.selector || selector === "**" && handleObj.selector ) ) {
3021                     eventType.splice( j--, 1 );
3022 
3023                     if ( handleObj.selector ) {
3024                         eventType.delegateCount--;
3025                     }
3026                     if ( special.remove ) {
3027                         special.remove.call( elem, handleObj );
3028                     }
3029                 }
3030             }
3031 
3032             // Remove generic event handler if we removed something and no more handlers exist
3033             // (avoids potential for endless recursion during removal of special event handlers)
3034             if ( eventType.length === 0 && origCount !== eventType.length ) {
3035                 if ( !special.teardown || special.teardown.call( elem, namespaces, elemData.handle ) === false ) {
3036                     jQuery.removeEvent( elem, type, elemData.handle );
3037                 }
3038 
3039                 delete events[ type ];
3040             }
3041         }
3042 
3043         // Remove the expando if it's no longer used
3044         if ( jQuery.isEmptyObject( events ) ) {
3045             delete elemData.handle;
3046 
3047             // removeData also checks for emptiness and clears the expando if empty
3048             // so use it instead of delete
3049             jQuery.removeData( elem, "events", true );
3050         }
3051     },
3052 
3053     // Events that are safe to short-circuit if no handlers are attached.
3054     // Native DOM events should not be added, they may have inline handlers.
3055     customEvent: {
3056         "getData": true,
3057         "setData": true,
3058         "changeData": true
3059     },
3060 
3061     trigger: function( event, data, elem, onlyHandlers ) {
3062         // Don't do events on text and comment nodes
3063         if ( elem && (elem.nodeType === 3 || elem.nodeType === 8) ) {
3064             return;
3065         }
3066 
3067         // Event object or event type
3068         var cache, exclusive, i, cur, old, ontype, special, handle, eventPath, bubbleType,
3069             type = event.type || event,
3070             namespaces = [];
3071 
3072         // focus/blur morphs to focusin/out; ensure we're not firing them right now
3073         if ( rfocusMorph.test( type + jQuery.event.triggered ) ) {
3074             return;
3075         }
3076 
3077         if ( type.indexOf( "!" ) >= 0 ) {
3078             // Exclusive events trigger only for the exact event (no namespaces)
3079             type = type.slice(0, -1);
3080             exclusive = true;
3081         }
3082 
3083         if ( type.indexOf( "." ) >= 0 ) {
3084             // Namespaced trigger; create a regexp to match event type in handle()
3085             namespaces = type.split(".");
3086             type = namespaces.shift();
3087             namespaces.sort();
3088         }
3089 
3090         if ( (!elem || jQuery.event.customEvent[ type ]) && !jQuery.event.global[ type ] ) {
3091             // No jQuery handlers for this event type, and it can't have inline handlers
3092             return;
3093         }
3094 
3095         // Caller can pass in an Event, Object, or just an event type string
3096         event = typeof event === "object" ?
3097             // jQuery.Event object
3098             event[ jQuery.expando ] ? event :
3099             // Object literal
3100             new jQuery.Event( type, event ) :
3101             // Just the event type (string)
3102             new jQuery.Event( type );
3103 
3104         event.type = type;
3105         event.isTrigger = true;
3106         event.exclusive = exclusive;
3107         event.namespace = namespaces.join( "." );
3108         event.namespace_re = event.namespace? new RegExp("(^|\\.)" + namespaces.join("\\.(?:.*\\.|)") + "(\\.|$)") : null;
3109         ontype = type.indexOf( ":" ) < 0 ? "on" + type : "";
3110 
3111         // Handle a global trigger
3112         if ( !elem ) {
3113 
3114             // TODO: Stop taunting the data cache; remove global events and always attach to document
3115             cache = jQuery.cache;
3116             for ( i in cache ) {
3117                 if ( cache[ i ].events && cache[ i ].events[ type ] ) {
3118                     jQuery.event.trigger( event, data, cache[ i ].handle.elem, true );
3119                 }
3120             }
3121             return;
3122         }
3123 
3124         // Clean up the event in case it is being reused
3125         event.result = undefined;
3126         if ( !event.target ) {
3127             event.target = elem;
3128         }
3129 
3130         // Clone any incoming data and prepend the event, creating the handler arg list
3131         data = data != null ? jQuery.makeArray( data ) : [];
3132         data.unshift( event );
3133 
3134         // Allow special events to draw outside the lines
3135         special = jQuery.event.special[ type ] || {};
3136         if ( special.trigger && special.trigger.apply( elem, data ) === false ) {
3137             return;
3138         }
3139 
3140         // Determine event propagation path in advance, per W3C events spec (#9951)
3141         // Bubble up to document, then to window; watch for a global ownerDocument var (#9724)
3142         eventPath = [[ elem, special.bindType || type ]];
3143         if ( !onlyHandlers && !special.noBubble && !jQuery.isWindow( elem ) ) {
3144 
3145             bubbleType = special.delegateType || type;
3146             cur = rfocusMorph.test( bubbleType + type ) ? elem : elem.parentNode;
3147             for ( old = elem; cur; cur = cur.parentNode ) {
3148                 eventPath.push([ cur, bubbleType ]);
3149                 old = cur;
3150             }
3151 
3152             // Only add window if we got to document (e.g., not plain obj or detached DOM)
3153             if ( old === (elem.ownerDocument || document) ) {
3154                 eventPath.push([ old.defaultView || old.parentWindow || window, bubbleType ]);
3155             }
3156         }
3157 
3158         // Fire handlers on the event path
3159         for ( i = 0; i < eventPath.length && !event.isPropagationStopped(); i++ ) {
3160 
3161             cur = eventPath[i][0];
3162             event.type = eventPath[i][1];
3163 
3164             handle = ( jQuery._data( cur, "events" ) || {} )[ event.type ] && jQuery._data( cur, "handle" );
3165             if ( handle ) {
3166                 handle.apply( cur, data );
3167             }
3168             // Note that this is a bare JS function and not a jQuery handler
3169             handle = ontype && cur[ ontype ];
3170             if ( handle && jQuery.acceptData( cur ) && handle.apply( cur, data ) === false ) {
3171                 event.preventDefault();
3172             }
3173         }
3174         event.type = type;
3175 
3176         // If nobody prevented the default action, do it now
3177         if ( !onlyHandlers && !event.isDefaultPrevented() ) {
3178 
3179             if ( (!special._default || special._default.apply( elem.ownerDocument, data ) === false) &&
3180                 !(type === "click" && jQuery.nodeName( elem, "a" )) && jQuery.acceptData( elem ) ) {
3181 
3182                 // Call a native DOM method on the target with the same name name as the event.
3183                 // Can't use an .isFunction() check here because IE6/7 fails that test.
3184                 // Don't do default actions on window, that's where global variables be (#6170)
3185                 // IE<9 dies on focus/blur to hidden element (#1486)
3186                 if ( ontype && elem[ type ] && ((type !== "focus" && type !== "blur") || event.target.offsetWidth !== 0) && !jQuery.isWindow( elem ) ) {
3187 
3188                     // Don't re-trigger an onFOO event when we call its FOO() method
3189                     old = elem[ ontype ];
3190 
3191                     if ( old ) {
3192                         elem[ ontype ] = null;
3193                     }
3194 
3195                     // Prevent re-triggering of the same event, since we already bubbled it above
3196                     jQuery.event.triggered = type;
3197                     elem[ type ]();
3198                     jQuery.event.triggered = undefined;
3199 
3200                     if ( old ) {
3201                         elem[ ontype ] = old;
3202                     }
3203                 }
3204             }
3205         }
3206 
3207         return event.result;
3208     },
3209 
3210     dispatch: function( event ) {
3211 
3212         // Make a writable jQuery.Event from the native event object
3213         event = jQuery.event.fix( event || window.event );
3214 
3215         var i, j, cur, ret, selMatch, matched, matches, handleObj, sel, related,
3216             handlers = ( (jQuery._data( this, "events" ) || {} )[ event.type ] || []),
3217             delegateCount = handlers.delegateCount,
3218             args = [].slice.call( arguments ),
3219             run_all = !event.exclusive && !event.namespace,
3220             special = jQuery.event.special[ event.type ] || {},
3221             handlerQueue = [];
3222 
3223         // Use the fix-ed jQuery.Event rather than the (read-only) native event
3224         args[0] = event;
3225         event.delegateTarget = this;
3226 
3227         // Call the preDispatch hook for the mapped type, and let it bail if desired
3228         if ( special.preDispatch && special.preDispatch.call( this, event ) === false ) {
3229             return;
3230         }
3231 
3232         // Determine handlers that should run if there are delegated events
3233         // Avoid non-left-click bubbling in Firefox (#3861)
3234         if ( delegateCount && !(event.button && event.type === "click") ) {
3235 
3236             for ( cur = event.target; cur != this; cur = cur.parentNode || this ) {
3237 
3238                 // Don't process clicks (ONLY) on disabled elements (#6911, #8165, #11382, #11764)
3239                 if ( cur.disabled !== true || event.type !== "click" ) {
3240                     selMatch = {};
3241                     matches = [];
3242                     for ( i = 0; i < delegateCount; i++ ) {
3243                         handleObj = handlers[ i ];
3244                         sel = handleObj.selector;
3245 
3246                         if ( selMatch[ sel ] === undefined ) {
3247                             selMatch[ sel ] = jQuery( sel, this ).index( cur ) >= 0;
3248                         }
3249                         if ( selMatch[ sel ] ) {
3250                             matches.push( handleObj );
3251                         }
3252                     }
3253                     if ( matches.length ) {
3254                         handlerQueue.push({ elem: cur, matches: matches });
3255                     }
3256                 }
3257             }
3258         }
3259 
3260         // Add the remaining (directly-bound) handlers
3261         if ( handlers.length > delegateCount ) {
3262             handlerQueue.push({ elem: this, matches: handlers.slice( delegateCount ) });
3263         }
3264 
3265         // Run delegates first; they may want to stop propagation beneath us
3266         for ( i = 0; i < handlerQueue.length && !event.isPropagationStopped(); i++ ) {
3267             matched = handlerQueue[ i ];
3268             event.currentTarget = matched.elem;
3269 
3270             for ( j = 0; j < matched.matches.length && !event.isImmediatePropagationStopped(); j++ ) {
3271                 handleObj = matched.matches[ j ];
3272 
3273                 // Triggered event must either 1) be non-exclusive and have no namespace, or
3274                 // 2) have namespace(s) a subset or equal to those in the bound event (both can have no namespace).
3275                 if ( run_all || (!event.namespace && !handleObj.namespace) || event.namespace_re && event.namespace_re.test( handleObj.namespace ) ) {
3276 
3277                     event.data = handleObj.data;
3278                     event.handleObj = handleObj;
3279 
3280                     ret = ( (jQuery.event.special[ handleObj.origType ] || {}).handle || handleObj.handler )
3281                             .apply( matched.elem, args );
3282 
3283                     if ( ret !== undefined ) {
3284                         event.result = ret;
3285                         if ( ret === false ) {
3286                             event.preventDefault();
3287                             event.stopPropagation();
3288                         }
3289                     }
3290                 }
3291             }
3292         }
3293 
3294         // Call the postDispatch hook for the mapped type
3295         if ( special.postDispatch ) {
3296             special.postDispatch.call( this, event );
3297         }
3298 
3299         return event.result;
3300     },
3301 
3302     // Includes some event props shared by KeyEvent and MouseEvent
3303     // *** attrChange attrName relatedNode srcElement  are not normalized, non-W3C, deprecated, will be removed in 1.8 ***
3304     props: "attrChange attrName relatedNode srcElement altKey bubbles cancelable ctrlKey currentTarget eventPhase metaKey relatedTarget shiftKey target timeStamp view which".split(" "),
3305 
3306     fixHooks: {},
3307 
3308     keyHooks: {
3309         props: "char charCode key keyCode".split(" "),
3310         filter: function( event, original ) {
3311 
3312             // Add which for key events
3313             if ( event.which == null ) {
3314                 event.which = original.charCode != null ? original.charCode : original.keyCode;
3315             }
3316 
3317             return event;
3318         }
3319     },
3320 
3321     mouseHooks: {
3322         props: "button buttons clientX clientY fromElement offsetX offsetY pageX pageY screenX screenY toElement".split(" "),
3323         filter: function( event, original ) {
3324             var eventDoc, doc, body,
3325                 button = original.button,
3326                 fromElement = original.fromElement;
3327 
3328             // Calculate pageX/Y if missing and clientX/Y available
3329             if ( event.pageX == null && original.clientX != null ) {
3330                 eventDoc = event.target.ownerDocument || document;
3331                 doc = eventDoc.documentElement;
3332                 body = eventDoc.body;
3333 
3334                 event.pageX = original.clientX + ( doc && doc.scrollLeft || body && body.scrollLeft || 0 ) - ( doc && doc.clientLeft || body && body.clientLeft || 0 );
3335                 event.pageY = original.clientY + ( doc && doc.scrollTop  || body && body.scrollTop  || 0 ) - ( doc && doc.clientTop  || body && body.clientTop  || 0 );
3336             }
3337 
3338             // Add relatedTarget, if necessary
3339             if ( !event.relatedTarget && fromElement ) {
3340                 event.relatedTarget = fromElement === event.target ? original.toElement : fromElement;
3341             }
3342 
3343             // Add which for click: 1 === left; 2 === middle; 3 === right
3344             // Note: button is not normalized, so don't use it
3345             if ( !event.which && button !== undefined ) {
3346                 event.which = ( button & 1 ? 1 : ( button & 2 ? 3 : ( button & 4 ? 2 : 0 ) ) );
3347             }
3348 
3349             return event;
3350         }
3351     },
3352 
3353     fix: function( event ) {
3354         if ( event[ jQuery.expando ] ) {
3355             return event;
3356         }
3357 
3358         // Create a writable copy of the event object and normalize some properties
3359         var i, prop,
3360             originalEvent = event,
3361             fixHook = jQuery.event.fixHooks[ event.type ] || {},
3362             copy = fixHook.props ? this.props.concat( fixHook.props ) : this.props;
3363 
3364         event = jQuery.Event( originalEvent );
3365 
3366         for ( i = copy.length; i; ) {
3367             prop = copy[ --i ];
3368             event[ prop ] = originalEvent[ prop ];
3369         }
3370 
3371         // Fix target property, if necessary (#1925, IE 6/7/8 & Safari2)
3372         if ( !event.target ) {
3373             event.target = originalEvent.srcElement || document;
3374         }
3375 
3376         // Target should not be a text node (#504, Safari)
3377         if ( event.target.nodeType === 3 ) {
3378             event.target = event.target.parentNode;
3379         }
3380 
3381         // For mouse/key events, metaKey==false if it's undefined (#3368, #11328; IE6/7/8)
3382         event.metaKey = !!event.metaKey;
3383 
3384         return fixHook.filter? fixHook.filter( event, originalEvent ) : event;
3385     },
3386 
3387     special: {
3388         load: {
3389             // Prevent triggered image.load events from bubbling to window.load
3390             noBubble: true
3391         },
3392 
3393         focus: {
3394             delegateType: "focusin"
3395         },
3396         blur: {
3397             delegateType: "focusout"
3398         },
3399 
3400         beforeunload: {
3401             setup: function( data, namespaces, eventHandle ) {
3402                 // We only want to do this special case on windows
3403                 if ( jQuery.isWindow( this ) ) {
3404                     this.onbeforeunload = eventHandle;
3405                 }
3406             },
3407 
3408             teardown: function( namespaces, eventHandle ) {
3409                 if ( this.onbeforeunload === eventHandle ) {
3410                     this.onbeforeunload = null;
3411                 }
3412             }
3413         }
3414     },
3415 
3416     simulate: function( type, elem, event, bubble ) {
3417         // Piggyback on a donor event to simulate a different one.
3418         // Fake originalEvent to avoid donor's stopPropagation, but if the
3419         // simulated event prevents default then we do the same on the donor.
3420         var e = jQuery.extend(
3421             new jQuery.Event(),
3422             event,
3423             { type: type,
3424                 isSimulated: true,
3425                 originalEvent: {}
3426             }
3427         );
3428         if ( bubble ) {
3429             jQuery.event.trigger( e, null, elem );
3430         } else {
3431             jQuery.event.dispatch.call( elem, e );
3432         }
3433         if ( e.isDefaultPrevented() ) {
3434             event.preventDefault();
3435         }
3436     }
3437 };

3439 // Some plugins are using, but it's undocumented/deprecated and will be removed.
3440 // The 1.7 special event interface should provide all the hooks needed now.
3441 jQuery.event.handle = jQuery.event.dispatch;

3443 jQuery.removeEvent = document.removeEventListener ?
3444     function( elem, type, handle ) {
3445         if ( elem.removeEventListener ) {
3446             elem.removeEventListener( type, handle, false );
3447         }
3448     } :
3449     function( elem, type, handle ) {
3450         var name = "on" + type;
3451 
3452         if ( elem.detachEvent ) {
3453 
3454             // #8545, #7054, preventing memory leaks for custom events in IE6-8 –
3455             // detachEvent needed property on element, by name of that event, to properly expose it to GC
3456             if ( typeof elem[ name ] === "undefined" ) {
3457                 elem[ name ] = null;
3458             }
3459 
3460             elem.detachEvent( name, handle );
3461         }
3462     };

3464 jQuery.Event = function( src, props ) {
3465     // Allow instantiation without the 'new' keyword
3466     if ( !(this instanceof jQuery.Event) ) {
3467         return new jQuery.Event( src, props );
3468     }
3469 
3470     // Event object
3471     if ( src && src.type ) {
3472         this.originalEvent = src;
3473         this.type = src.type;
3474 
3475         // Events bubbling up the document may have been marked as prevented
3476         // by a handler lower down the tree; reflect the correct value.
3477         this.isDefaultPrevented = ( src.defaultPrevented || src.returnValue === false ||
3478             src.getPreventDefault && src.getPreventDefault() ) ? returnTrue : returnFalse;
3479 
3480     // Event type
3481     } else {
3482         this.type = src;
3483     }
3484 
3485     // Put explicitly provided properties onto the event object
3486     if ( props ) {
3487         jQuery.extend( this, props );
3488     }
3489 
3490     // Create a timestamp if incoming event doesn't have one
3491     this.timeStamp = src && src.timeStamp || jQuery.now();
3492 
3493     // Mark it as fixed
3494     this[ jQuery.expando ] = true;
3495 };
3496 
3497 function returnFalse() {
3498     return false;
3499 }
3500 function returnTrue() {
3501     return true;
3502 }
3503 
3504 // jQuery.Event is based on DOM3 Events as specified by the ECMAScript Language Binding
3505 // http://www.w3.org/TR/2003/WD-DOM-Level-3-Events-20030331/ecma-script-binding.html
3506 jQuery.Event.prototype = {
3507     preventDefault: function() {
3508         this.isDefaultPrevented = returnTrue;
3509 
3510         var e = this.originalEvent;
3511         if ( !e ) {
3512             return;
3513         }
3514 
3515         // if preventDefault exists run it on the original event
3516         if ( e.preventDefault ) {
3517             e.preventDefault();
3518 
3519         // otherwise set the returnValue property of the original event to false (IE)
3520         } else {
3521             e.returnValue = false;
3522         }
3523     },
3524     stopPropagation: function() {
3525         this.isPropagationStopped = returnTrue;
3526 
3527         var e = this.originalEvent;
3528         if ( !e ) {
3529             return;
3530         }
3531         // if stopPropagation exists run it on the original event
3532         if ( e.stopPropagation ) {
3533             e.stopPropagation();
3534         }
3535         // otherwise set the cancelBubble property of the original event to true (IE)
3536         e.cancelBubble = true;
3537     },
3538     stopImmediatePropagation: function() {
3539         this.isImmediatePropagationStopped = returnTrue;
3540         this.stopPropagation();
3541     },
3542     isDefaultPrevented: returnFalse,
3543     isPropagationStopped: returnFalse,
3544     isImmediatePropagationStopped: returnFalse
3545 };

3547 // Create mouseenter/leave events using mouseover/out and event-time checks
3548 jQuery.each({
3549     mouseenter: "mouseover",
3550     mouseleave: "mouseout"
3551 }, function( orig, fix ) {
3552     jQuery.event.special[ orig ] = {
3553         delegateType: fix,
3554         bindType: fix,
3555 
3556         handle: function( event ) {
3557             var ret,
3558                 target = this,
3559                 related = event.relatedTarget,
3560                 handleObj = event.handleObj,
3561                 selector = handleObj.selector;
3562 
3563             // For mousenter/leave call the handler if related is outside the target.
3564             // NB: No relatedTarget if the mouse left/entered the browser window
3565             if ( !related || (related !== target && !jQuery.contains( target, related )) ) {
3566                 event.type = handleObj.origType;
3567                 ret = handleObj.handler.apply( this, arguments );
3568                 event.type = fix;
3569             }
3570             return ret;
3571         }
3572     };

3575 // IE submit delegation
3576 if ( !jQuery.support.submitBubbles ) {
3577 
3578     jQuery.event.special.submit = {
3579         setup: function() {
3580             // Only need this for delegated form submit events
3581             if ( jQuery.nodeName( this, "form" ) ) {
3582                 return false;
3583             }
3584 
3585             // Lazy-add a submit handler when a descendant form may potentially be submitted
3586             jQuery.event.add( this, "click._submit keypress._submit", function( e ) {
3587                 // Node name check avoids a VML-related crash in IE (#9807)
3588                 var elem = e.target,
3589                     form = jQuery.nodeName( elem, "input" ) || jQuery.nodeName( elem, "button" ) ? elem.form : undefined;
3590                 if ( form && !jQuery._data( form, "_submit_attached" ) ) {
3591                     jQuery.event.add( form, "submit._submit", function( event ) {
3592                         event._submit_bubble = true;
3593                     });
3594                     jQuery._data( form, "_submit_attached", true );
3595                 }
3596             });
3597             // return undefined since we don't need an event listener
3598         },
3599 
3600         postDispatch: function( event ) {
3601             // If form was submitted by the user, bubble the event up the tree
3602             if ( event._submit_bubble ) {
3603                 delete event._submit_bubble;
3604                 if ( this.parentNode && !event.isTrigger ) {
3605                     jQuery.event.simulate( "submit", this.parentNode, event, true );
3606                 }
3607             }
3608         },
3609 
3610         teardown: function() {
3611             // Only need this for delegated form submit events
3612             if ( jQuery.nodeName( this, "form" ) ) {
3613                 return false;
3614             }
3615 
3616             // Remove delegated handlers; cleanData eventually reaps submit handlers attached above
3617             jQuery.event.remove( this, "._submit" );
3618         }
3619     };
3620 }

3622 // IE change delegation and checkbox/radio fix
3623 if ( !jQuery.support.changeBubbles ) {
3624 
3625     jQuery.event.special.change = {
3626 
3627         setup: function() {
3628 
3629             if ( rformElems.test( this.nodeName ) ) {
3630                 // IE doesn't fire change on a check/radio until blur; trigger it on click
3631                 // after a propertychange. Eat the blur-change in special.change.handle.
3632                 // This still fires onchange a second time for check/radio after blur.
3633                 if ( this.type === "checkbox" || this.type === "radio" ) {
3634                     jQuery.event.add( this, "propertychange._change", function( event ) {
3635                         if ( event.originalEvent.propertyName === "checked" ) {
3636                             this._just_changed = true;
3637                         }
3638                     });
3639                     jQuery.event.add( this, "click._change", function( event ) {
3640                         if ( this._just_changed && !event.isTrigger ) {
3641                             this._just_changed = false;
3642                         }
3643                         // Allow triggered, simulated change events (#11500)
3644                         jQuery.event.simulate( "change", this, event, true );
3645                     });
3646                 }
3647                 return false;
3648             }
3649             // Delegated event; lazy-add a change handler on descendant inputs
3650             jQuery.event.add( this, "beforeactivate._change", function( e ) {
3651                 var elem = e.target;
3652 
3653                 if ( rformElems.test( elem.nodeName ) && !jQuery._data( elem, "_change_attached" ) ) {
3654                     jQuery.event.add( elem, "change._change", function( event ) {
3655                         if ( this.parentNode && !event.isSimulated && !event.isTrigger ) {
3656                             jQuery.event.simulate( "change", this.parentNode, event, true );
3657                         }
3658                     });
3659                     jQuery._data( elem, "_change_attached", true );
3660                 }
3661             });
3662         },
3663 
3664         handle: function( event ) {
3665             var elem = event.target;
3666 
3667             // Swallow native change events from checkbox/radio, we already triggered them above
3668             if ( this !== elem || event.isSimulated || event.isTrigger || (elem.type !== "radio" && elem.type !== "checkbox") ) {
3669                 return event.handleObj.handler.apply( this, arguments );
3670             }
3671         },
3672 
3673         teardown: function() {
3674             jQuery.event.remove( this, "._change" );
3675 
3676             return !rformElems.test( this.nodeName );
3677         }
3678     };
3679 }

3681 // Create "bubbling" focus and blur events
3682 if ( !jQuery.support.focusinBubbles ) {
3683     jQuery.each({ focus: "focusin", blur: "focusout" }, function( orig, fix ) {
3684 
3685         // Attach a single capturing handler while someone wants focusin/focusout
3686         var attaches = 0,
3687             handler = function( event ) {
3688                 jQuery.event.simulate( fix, event.target, jQuery.event.fix( event ), true );
3689             };
3690 
3691         jQuery.event.special[ fix ] = {
3692             setup: function() {
3693                 if ( attaches++ === 0 ) {
3694                     document.addEventListener( orig, handler, true );
3695                 }
3696             },
3697             teardown: function() {
3698                 if ( --attaches === 0 ) {
3699                     document.removeEventListener( orig, handler, true );
3700                 }
3701             }
3702         };
3703     });

3706 jQuery.fn.extend({
3707 
3708     on: function( types, selector, data, fn, /*INTERNAL*/ one ) {
3709         var origFn, type;
3710 
3711         // Types can be a map of types/handlers
3712         if ( typeof types === "object" ) {
3713             // ( types-Object, selector, data )
3714             if ( typeof selector !== "string" ) { // && selector != null
3715                 // ( types-Object, data )
3716                 data = data || selector;
3717                 selector = undefined;
3718             }
3719             for ( type in types ) {
3720                 this.on( type, selector, data, types[ type ], one );
3721             }
3722             return this;
3723         }
3724 
3725         if ( data == null && fn == null ) {
3726             // ( types, fn )
3727             fn = selector;
3728             data = selector = undefined;
3729         } else if ( fn == null ) {
3730             if ( typeof selector === "string" ) {
3731                 // ( types, selector, fn )
3732                 fn = data;
3733                 data = undefined;
3734             } else {
3735                 // ( types, data, fn )
3736                 fn = data;
3737                 data = selector;
3738                 selector = undefined;
3739             }
3740         }
3741         if ( fn === false ) {
3742             fn = returnFalse;
3743         } else if ( !fn ) {
3744             return this;
3745         }
3746 
3747         if ( one === 1 ) {
3748             origFn = fn;
3749             fn = function( event ) {
3750                 // Can use an empty set, since event contains the info
3751                 jQuery().off( event );
3752                 return origFn.apply( this, arguments );
3753             };
3754             // Use same guid so caller can remove using origFn
3755             fn.guid = origFn.guid || ( origFn.guid = jQuery.guid++ );
3756         }
3757         return this.each( function() {
3758             jQuery.event.add( this, types, fn, data, selector );
3759         });
3760     },
3761     one: function( types, selector, data, fn ) {
3762         return this.on( types, selector, data, fn, 1 );
3763     },
3764     off: function( types, selector, fn ) {
3765         var handleObj, type;
3766         if ( types && types.preventDefault && types.handleObj ) {
3767             // ( event )  dispatched jQuery.Event
3768             handleObj = types.handleObj;
3769             jQuery( types.delegateTarget ).off(
3770                 handleObj.namespace ? handleObj.origType + "." + handleObj.namespace : handleObj.origType,
3771                 handleObj.selector,
3772                 handleObj.handler
3773             );
3774             return this;
3775         }
3776         if ( typeof types === "object" ) {
3777             // ( types-object [, selector] )
3778             for ( type in types ) {
3779                 this.off( type, selector, types[ type ] );
3780             }
3781             return this;
3782         }
3783         if ( selector === false || typeof selector === "function" ) {
3784             // ( types [, fn] )
3785             fn = selector;
3786             selector = undefined;
3787         }
3788         if ( fn === false ) {
3789             fn = returnFalse;
3790         }
3791         return this.each(function() {
3792             jQuery.event.remove( this, types, fn, selector );
3793         });
3794     },
3795 
3796     bind: function( types, data, fn ) {
3797         return this.on( types, null, data, fn );
3798     },
3799     unbind: function( types, fn ) {
3800         return this.off( types, null, fn );
3801     },
3802 
3803     live: function( types, data, fn ) {
3804         jQuery( this.context ).on( types, this.selector, data, fn );
3805         return this;
3806     },
3807     die: function( types, fn ) {
3808         jQuery( this.context ).off( types, this.selector || "**", fn );
3809         return this;
3810     },
3811 
3812     delegate: function( selector, types, data, fn ) {
3813         return this.on( types, selector, data, fn );
3814     },
3815     undelegate: function( selector, types, fn ) {
3816         // ( namespace ) or ( selector, types [, fn] )
3817         return arguments.length == 1? this.off( selector, "**" ) : this.off( types, selector || "**", fn );
3818     },
3819 
3820     trigger: function( type, data ) {
3821         return this.each(function() {
3822             jQuery.event.trigger( type, data, this );
3823         });
3824     },
3825     triggerHandler: function( type, data ) {
3826         if ( this[0] ) {
3827             return jQuery.event.trigger( type, data, this[0], true );
3828         }
3829     },
3830 
3831     toggle: function( fn ) {
3832         // Save reference to arguments for access in closure
3833         var args = arguments,
3834             guid = fn.guid || jQuery.guid++,
3835             i = 0,
3836             toggler = function( event ) {
3837                 // Figure out which function to execute
3838                 var lastToggle = ( jQuery._data( this, "lastToggle" + fn.guid ) || 0 ) % i;
3839                 jQuery._data( this, "lastToggle" + fn.guid, lastToggle + 1 );
3840 
3841                 // Make sure that clicks stop
3842                 event.preventDefault();
3843 
3844                 // and execute the function
3845                 return args[ lastToggle ].apply( this, arguments ) || false;
3846             };
3847 
3848         // link all the functions, so any of them can unbind this click handler
3849         toggler.guid = guid;
3850         while ( i < args.length ) {
3851             args[ i++ ].guid = guid;
3852         }
3853 
3854         return this.click( toggler );
3855     },
3856 
3857     hover: function( fnOver, fnOut ) {
3858         return this.mouseenter( fnOver ).mouseleave( fnOut || fnOver );
3859     }
3860 });

3862 jQuery.each( ("blur focus focusin focusout load resize scroll unload click dblclick " +
3863     "mousedown mouseup mousemove mouseover mouseout mouseenter mouseleave " +
3864     "change select submit keydown keypress keyup error contextmenu").split(" "), function( i, name ) {
3865 
3866     // Handle event binding
3867     jQuery.fn[ name ] = function( data, fn ) {
3868         if ( fn == null ) {
3869             fn = data;
3870             data = null;
3871         }
3872 
3873         return arguments.length > 0 ?
3874             this.on( name, null, data, fn ) :
3875             this.trigger( name );
3876     };
3877 
3878     if ( rkeyEvent.test( name ) ) {
3879         jQuery.event.fixHooks[ name ] = jQuery.event.keyHooks;
3880     }
3881 
3882     if ( rmouseEvent.test( name ) ) {
3883         jQuery.event.fixHooks[ name ] = jQuery.event.mouseHooks;
3884     }
3885 });

3916     // Augment a function for special use by Sizzle
3917     markFunction = function( fn, value ) {
3918         fn[ expando ] = value || true;
3919         return fn;

3922     createCache = function() {
3923         var cache = {},
3924             keys = [];
3925 
3926         return markFunction(function( key, value ) {
3927             // Only keep the most recent entries
3928             if ( keys.push( key ) > Expr.cacheLength ) {
3929                 delete cache[ keys.shift() ];
3930             }
3931 
3932             return (cache[ key ] = value);
3933         }, cache );
3934     },

3940     // Regex
3941 
3942     // Whitespace characters http://www.w3.org/TR/css3-selectors/#whitespace
3943     whitespace = "[\\x20\\t\\r\\n\\f]",
3944     // http://www.w3.org/TR/css3-syntax/#characters
3945     characterEncoding = "(?:\\\\.|[-\\w]|[^\\x00-\\xa0])+",
3946 
3947     // Loosely modeled on CSS identifier characters
3948     // An unquoted value should be a CSS identifier (http://www.w3.org/TR/css3-selectors/#attribute-selectors)
3949     // Proper syntax: http://www.w3.org/TR/CSS21/syndata.html#value-def-identifier
3950     identifier = characterEncoding.replace( "w", "w#" ),
3951 
3952     // Acceptable operators http://www.w3.org/TR/selectors/#attribute-selectors
3953     operators = "([*^$|!~]?=)",
3954     attributes = "\\[" + whitespace + "*(" + characterEncoding + ")" + whitespace +
3955         "*(?:" + operators + whitespace + "*(?:(['\"])((?:\\\\.|[^\\\\])*?)\\3|(" + identifier + ")|)|)" + whitespace + "*\\]",
3956 
3957     // Prefer arguments not in parens/brackets,
3958     //   then attribute selectors and non-pseudos (denoted by :),
3959     //   then anything else
3960     // These preferences are here to reduce the number of selectors
3961     //   needing tokenize in the PSEUDO preFilter
3962     pseudos = ":(" + characterEncoding + ")(?:\\((?:(['\"])((?:\\\\.|[^\\\\])*?)\\2|([^()[\\]]*|(?:(?:" + attributes + ")|[^:]|\\\\.)*|.*))\\)|)",
3963 
3964     // For matchExpr.POS and matchExpr.needsContext
3965     pos = ":(nth|eq|gt|lt|first|last|even|odd)(?:\\(((?:-\\d)?\\d*)\\)|)(?=[^-]|$)",
3966 
3967     // Leading and non-escaped trailing whitespace, capturing some non-whitespace characters preceding the latter
3968     rtrim = new RegExp( "^" + whitespace + "+|((?:^|[^\\\\])(?:\\\\.)*)" + whitespace + "+$", "g" ),
3969 
3970     rcomma = new RegExp( "^" + whitespace + "*," + whitespace + "*" ),
3971     rcombinators = new RegExp( "^" + whitespace + "*([\\x20\\t\\r\\n\\f>+~])" + whitespace + "*" ),
3972     rpseudo = new RegExp( pseudos ),
3973 
3974     // Easily-parseable/retrievable ID or TAG or CLASS selectors
3975     rquickExpr = /^(?:#([\w\-]+)|(\w+)|\.([\w\-]+))$/,
3976 
3977     rnot = /^:not/,
3978     rsibling = /[\x20\t\r\n\f]*[+~]/,
3979     rendsWithNot = /:not\($/,
3980 
3981     rheader = /h\d/i,
3982     rinputs = /input|select|textarea|button/i,
3983 
3984     rbackslash = /\\(?!\\)/g,
3985 
3986     matchExpr = {
3987         "ID": new RegExp( "^#(" + characterEncoding + ")" ),
3988         "CLASS": new RegExp( "^\\.(" + characterEncoding + ")" ),
3989         "NAME": new RegExp( "^\\[name=['\"]?(" + characterEncoding + ")['\"]?\\]" ),
3990         "TAG": new RegExp( "^(" + characterEncoding.replace( "w", "w*" ) + ")" ),
3991         "ATTR": new RegExp( "^" + attributes ),
3992         "PSEUDO": new RegExp( "^" + pseudos ),
3993         "CHILD": new RegExp( "^:(only|nth|last|first)-child(?:\\(" + whitespace +
3994             "*(even|odd|(([+-]|)(\\d*)n|)" + whitespace + "*(?:([+-]|)" + whitespace +
3995             "*(\\d+)|))" + whitespace + "*\\)|)", "i" ),
3996         "POS": new RegExp( pos, "ig" ),
3997         // For use in libraries implementing .is()
3998         "needsContext": new RegExp( "^" + whitespace + "*[>+~]|" + pos, "i" )
3999     },

4003     // Used for testing something on an element
4004     assert = function( fn ) {
4005         var div = document.createElement("div");
4006 
4007         try {
4008             return fn( div );
4009         } catch (e) {
4010             return false;
4011         } finally {
4012             // release memory in IE
4013             div = null;
4014         }
4015     },

4017     // Check if getElementsByTagName("*") returns only elements
4018     assertTagNameNoComments = assert(function( div ) {
4019         div.appendChild( document.createComment("") );
4020         return !div.getElementsByTagName("*").length;
4021     }),
4022 
4023     // Check if getAttribute returns normalized href attributes
4024     assertHrefNotNormalized = assert(function( div ) {
4025         div.innerHTML = "<a href='#'></a>";
4026         return div.firstChild && typeof div.firstChild.getAttribute !== strundefined &&
4027             div.firstChild.getAttribute("href") === "#";
4028     }),
4029 
4030     // Check if attributes should be retrieved by attribute nodes
4031     assertAttributes = assert(function( div ) {
4032         div.innerHTML = "<select></select>";
4033         var type = typeof div.lastChild.getAttribute("multiple");
4034         // IE8 returns a string for some attributes even when not present
4035         return type !== "boolean" && type !== "string";
4036     }),
4037 
4038     // Check if getElementsByClassName can be trusted
4039     assertUsableClassName = assert(function( div ) {
4040         // Opera can't find a second classname (in 9.6)
4041         div.innerHTML = "<div class='hidden e'></div><div class='hidden'></div>";
4042         if ( !div.getElementsByClassName || !div.getElementsByClassName("e").length ) {
4043             return false;
4044         }
4045 
4046         // Safari 3.2 caches class attributes and doesn't catch changes
4047         div.lastChild.className = "e";
4048         return div.getElementsByClassName("e").length === 2;
4049     }),
4050 
4051     // Check if getElementById returns elements by name
4052     // Check if getElementsByName privileges form controls or returns elements by ID
4053     assertUsableName = assert(function( div ) {
4054         // Inject content
4055         div.id = expando + 0;
4056         div.innerHTML = "<a name='" + expando + "'></a><div name='" + expando + "'></div>";
4057         docElem.insertBefore( div, docElem.firstChild );
4058 
4059         // Test
4060         var pass = document.getElementsByName &&
4061             // buggy browsers will return fewer than the correct 2
4062             document.getElementsByName( expando ).length === 2 +
4063             // buggy browsers will return more than the correct 0
4064             document.getElementsByName( expando + 0 ).length;
4065         assertGetIdNotName = !document.getElementById( expando );
4066 
4067         // Cleanup
4068         docElem.removeChild( div );
4069 
4070         return pass;
4071     });
4072 
4073 // If slice is not available, provide a backup
4074 try {
4075     slice.call( docElem.childNodes, 0 )[0].nodeType;
4076 } catch ( e ) {
4077     slice = function( i ) {
4078         var elem, results = [];
4079         for ( ; (elem = this[i]); i++ ) {
4080             results.push( elem );
4081         }
4082         return results;
4083     };

4085 
4086 function Sizzle( selector, context, results, seed ) {
4087     results = results || [];
4088     context = context || document;
4089     var match, elem, xml, m,
4090         nodeType = context.nodeType;
4091 
4092     if ( nodeType !== 1 && nodeType !== 9 ) {
4093         return [];
4094     }
4095 
4096     if ( !selector || typeof selector !== "string" ) {
4097         return results;
4098     }
4099 
4100     xml = isXML( context );
4101 
4102     if ( !xml && !seed ) {
4103         if ( (match = rquickExpr.exec( selector )) ) {
4104             // Speed-up: Sizzle("#ID")
4105             if ( (m = match[1]) ) {
4106                 if ( nodeType === 9 ) {
4107                     elem = context.getElementById( m );
4108                     // Check parentNode to catch when Blackberry 4.6 returns
4109                     // nodes that are no longer in the document #6963
4110                     if ( elem && elem.parentNode ) {
4111                         // Handle the case where IE, Opera, and Webkit return items
4112                         // by name instead of ID
4113                         if ( elem.id === m ) {
4114                             results.push( elem );
4115                             return results;
4116                         }
4117                     } else {
4118                         return results;
4119                     }
4120                 } else {
4121                     // Context is not a document
4122                     if ( context.ownerDocument && (elem = context.ownerDocument.getElementById( m )) &&
4123                         contains( context, elem ) && elem.id === m ) {
4124                         results.push( elem );
4125                         return results;
4126                     }
4127                 }
4128 
4129             // Speed-up: Sizzle("TAG")
4130             } else if ( match[2] ) {
4131                 push.apply( results, slice.call(context.getElementsByTagName( selector ), 0) );
4132                 return results;
4133 
4134             // Speed-up: Sizzle(".CLASS")
4135             } else if ( (m = match[3]) && assertUsableClassName && context.getElementsByClassName ) {
4136                 push.apply( results, slice.call(context.getElementsByClassName( m ), 0) );
4137                 return results;
4138             }
4139         }
4140     }
4141 
4142     // All others
4143     return select( selector, context, results, seed, xml );
4144 }
4145 
4146 Sizzle.matches = function( expr, elements ) {
4147     return Sizzle( expr, null, null, elements );
4148 };
4149 
4150 Sizzle.matchesSelector = function( elem, expr ) {
4151     return Sizzle( expr, null, null, [ elem ] ).length > 0;
4152 };

4154 // Returns a function to use in pseudos for input types
4155 function createInputPseudo( type ) {
4156     return function( elem ) {
4157         var name = elem.nodeName.toLowerCase();
4158         return name === "input" && elem.type === type;
4159     };
4160 }

4162 // Returns a function to use in pseudos for buttons
4163 function createButtonPseudo( type ) {
4164     return function( elem ) {
4165         var name = elem.nodeName.toLowerCase();
4166         return (name === "input" || name === "button") && elem.type === type;
4167     };
4168 }

4170 /**
4171  * Utility function for retrieving the text value of an array of DOM nodes
4172  * @param {Array|Element} elem
4173  */
4174 getText = Sizzle.getText = function( elem ) {
4175     var node,
4176         ret = "",
4177         i = 0,
4178         nodeType = elem.nodeType;
4179 
4180     if ( nodeType ) {
4181         if ( nodeType === 1 || nodeType === 9 || nodeType === 11 ) {
4182             // Use textContent for elements
4183             // innerText usage removed for consistency of new lines (see #11153)
4184             if ( typeof elem.textContent === "string" ) {
4185                 return elem.textContent;
4186             } else {
4187                 // Traverse its children
4188                 for ( elem = elem.firstChild; elem; elem = elem.nextSibling ) {
4189                     ret += getText( elem );
4190                 }
4191             }
4192         } else if ( nodeType === 3 || nodeType === 4 ) {
4193             return elem.nodeValue;
4194         }
4195         // Do not include comment or processing instruction nodes
4196     } else {
4197 
4198         // If no nodeType, this is expected to be an array
4199         for ( ; (node = elem[i]); i++ ) {
4200             // Do not traverse comment nodes
4201             ret += getText( node );
4202         }
4203     }
4204     return ret;
4205 };

4207 isXML = Sizzle.isXML = function isXML( elem ) {
4208     // documentElement is verified for cases where it doesn't yet exist
4209     // (such as loading iframes in IE - #4833)
4210     var documentElement = elem && (elem.ownerDocument || elem).documentElement;
4211     return documentElement ? documentElement.nodeName !== "HTML" : false;
4212 };
4213 
4214 // Element contains another
4215 contains = Sizzle.contains = docElem.contains ?
4216     function( a, b ) {
4217         var adown = a.nodeType === 9 ? a.documentElement : a,
4218             bup = b && b.parentNode;
4219         return a === bup || !!( bup && bup.nodeType === 1 && adown.contains && adown.contains(bup) );
4220     } :
4221     docElem.compareDocumentPosition ?
4222     function( a, b ) {
4223         return b && !!( a.compareDocumentPosition( b ) & 16 );
4224     } :
4225     function( a, b ) {
4226         while ( (b = b.parentNode) ) {
4227             if ( b === a ) {
4228                 return true;
4229             }
4230         }
4231         return false;
4232     };

4234 Sizzle.attr = function( elem, name ) {
4235     var attr,
4236         xml = isXML( elem );
4237 
4238     if ( !xml ) {
4239         name = name.toLowerCase();
4240     }
4241     if ( Expr.attrHandle[ name ] ) {
4242         return Expr.attrHandle[ name ]( elem );
4243     }
4244     if ( assertAttributes || xml ) {
4245         return elem.getAttribute( name );
4246     }
4247     attr = elem.getAttributeNode( name );
4248     return attr ?
4249         typeof elem[ name ] === "boolean" ?
4250             elem[ name ] ? name : null :
4251             attr.specified ? attr.value : null :
4252         null;
4253 };

4281     find: {
4282         "ID": assertGetIdNotName ?
4283             function( id, context, xml ) {
4284                 if ( typeof context.getElementById !== strundefined && !xml ) {
4285                     var m = context.getElementById( id );
4286                     // Check parentNode to catch when Blackberry 4.6 returns
4287                     // nodes that are no longer in the document #6963
4288                     return m && m.parentNode ? [m] : [];
4289                 }
4290             } :
4291             function( id, context, xml ) {
4292                 if ( typeof context.getElementById !== strundefined && !xml ) {
4293                     var m = context.getElementById( id );
4294 
4295                     return m ?
4296                         m.id === id || typeof m.getAttributeNode !== strundefined && m.getAttributeNode("id").value === id ?
4297                             [m] :
4298                             undefined :
4299                         [];
4300                 }
4301             },
4302 
4303         "TAG": assertTagNameNoComments ?
4304             function( tag, context ) {
4305                 if ( typeof context.getElementsByTagName !== strundefined ) {
4306                     return context.getElementsByTagName( tag );
4307                 }
4308             } :
4309             function( tag, context ) {
4310                 var results = context.getElementsByTagName( tag );
4311

4313                 if ( tag === "*" ) {

4317

4319                         if ( elem.nodeType === 1 ) {
4320                             tmp.push( elem );
4321                         }
4322                     }
4323

4326                 return results;
4327             },

4330             if ( typeof context.getElementsByName !== strundefined ) {
4331                 return context.getElementsByName( name );
4332             }

4342     relative: {
4343         ">": { dir: "parentNode", first: true },
4344         " ": { dir: "parentNode" },
4345         "+": { dir: "previousSibling", first: true },
4346         "~": { dir: "previousSibling" }
