4349     preFilter: {
4350         "ATTR": function( match ) {
4351             match[1] = match[1].replace( rbackslash, "" );
4352 
4353             // Move the given value to match[3] whether quoted or unquoted
4354             match[3] = ( match[4] || match[5] || "" ).replace( rbackslash, "" );
4355 
4356             if ( match[2] === "~=" ) {
4357                 match[3] = " " + match[3] + " ";
4358             }
4359 
4360             return match.slice( 0, 4 );
4361         },
4362 
4363         "CHILD": function( match ) {
4364             /* matches from matchExpr.CHILD
4365                 1 type (only|nth|...)
4366                 2 argument (even|odd|\d*|\d*n([+-]\d+)?|...)
4367                 3 xn-component of xn+y argument ([+-]?\d*n|)
4368                 4 sign of xn-component
4369                 5 x of xn-component
4370                 6 sign of y-component
4371                 7 y of y-component
4372             */
4373             match[1] = match[1].toLowerCase();
4374 
4375             if ( match[1] === "nth" ) {
4376                 // nth-child requires argument
4377                 if ( !match[2] ) {
4378                     Sizzle.error( match[0] );
4379                 }
4380 
4381                 // numeric x and y parameters for Expr.filter.CHILD
4382                 // remember that false/true cast respectively to 0/1
4383                 match[3] = +( match[3] ? match[4] + (match[5] || 1) : 2 * ( match[2] === "even" || match[2] === "odd" ) );
4384                 match[4] = +( ( match[6] + match[7] ) || match[2] === "odd" );
4385 
4386             // other types prohibit arguments
4387             } else if ( match[2] ) {
4388                 Sizzle.error( match[0] );
4389             }
4390 
4391             return match;
4392         },
4393 
4394         "PSEUDO": function( match, context, xml ) {
4395             var unquoted, excess;
4396             if ( matchExpr["CHILD"].test( match[0] ) ) {
4397                 return null;
4398             }
4399 
4400             if ( match[3] ) {
4401                 match[2] = match[3];
4402             } else if ( (unquoted = match[4]) ) {
4403                 // Only check arguments that contain a pseudo
4404                 if ( rpseudo.test(unquoted) &&
4405                     // Get excess from tokenize (recursively)
4406                     (excess = tokenize( unquoted, context, xml, true )) &&
4407                     // advance to the next closing parenthesis
4408                     (excess = unquoted.indexOf( ")", unquoted.length - excess ) - unquoted.length) ) {
4409 
4410                     // excess is a negative index
4411                     unquoted = unquoted.slice( 0, excess );
4412                     match[0] = match[0].slice( 0, excess );
4413                 }
4414                 match[2] = unquoted;
4415             }
4416 
4417             // Return only captures needed by the pseudo filter method (type and argument)
4418             return match.slice( 0, 3 );
4419         }
4420     },
4421 
4422     filter: {
4423         "ID": assertGetIdNotName ?
4424             function( id ) {
4425                 id = id.replace( rbackslash, "" );
4426                 return function( elem ) {
4427                     return elem.getAttribute("id") === id;
4428                 };
4429             } :
4430             function( id ) {
4431                 id = id.replace( rbackslash, "" );
4432                 return function( elem ) {
4433                     var node = typeof elem.getAttributeNode !== strundefined && elem.getAttributeNode("id");
4434                     return node && node.value === id;
4435                 };
4436             },
4437 
4438         "TAG": function( nodeName ) {
4439             if ( nodeName === "*" ) {
4440                 return function() { return true; };
4441             }
4442             nodeName = nodeName.replace( rbackslash, "" ).toLowerCase();
4443 
4444             return function( elem ) {
4445                 return elem.nodeName && elem.nodeName.toLowerCase() === nodeName;
4446             };
4447         },
4448 
4449         "CLASS": function( className ) {
4450             var pattern = classCache[ expando ][ className ];
4451             if ( !pattern ) {
4452                 pattern = classCache( className, new RegExp("(^|" + whitespace + ")" + className + "(" + whitespace + "|$)") );
4453             }
4454             return function( elem ) {
4455                 return pattern.test( elem.className || (typeof elem.getAttribute !== strundefined && elem.getAttribute("class")) || "" );
4456             };
4457         },
4458 
4459         "ATTR": function( name, operator, check ) {
4460             if ( !operator ) {
4461                 return function( elem ) {
4462                     return Sizzle.attr( elem, name ) != null;
4463                 };
4464             }
4465 
4466             return function( elem ) {
4467                 var result = Sizzle.attr( elem, name ),
4468                     value = result + "";
4469 
4470                 if ( result == null ) {
4471                     return operator === "!=";
4472                 }
4473 
4474                 switch ( operator ) {
4475                     case "=":
4476                         return value === check;
4477                     case "!=":
4478                         return value !== check;
4479                     case "^=":
4480                         return check && value.indexOf( check ) === 0;
4481                     case "*=":
4482                         return check && value.indexOf( check ) > -1;
4483                     case "$=":
4484                         return check && value.substr( value.length - check.length ) === check;
4485                     case "~=":
4486                         return ( " " + value + " " ).indexOf( check ) > -1;
4487                     case "|=":
4488                         return value === check || value.substr( 0, check.length + 1 ) === check + "-";
4489                 }
4490             };
4491         },
4492 
4493         "CHILD": function( type, argument, first, last ) {
4494 
4495             if ( type === "nth" ) {
4496                 var doneName = done++;
4497 
4498                 return function( elem ) {
4499                     var parent, diff,
4500                         count = 0,
4501                         node = elem;
4502 
4503                     if ( first === 1 && last === 0 ) {
4504                         return true;
4505                     }
4506 
4507                     parent = elem.parentNode;
4508 
4509                     if ( parent && (parent[ expando ] !== doneName || !elem.sizset) ) {
4510                         for ( node = parent.firstChild; node; node = node.nextSibling ) {
4511                             if ( node.nodeType === 1 ) {
4512                                 node.sizset = ++count;
4513                                 if ( node === elem ) {
4514                                     break;
4515                                 }
4516                             }
4517                         }
4518 
4519                         parent[ expando ] = doneName;
4520                     }
4521 
4522                     diff = elem.sizset - last;
4523 
4524                     if ( first === 0 ) {
4525                         return diff === 0;
4526 
4527                     } else {
4528                         return ( diff % first === 0 && diff / first >= 0 );
4529                     }
4530                 };
4531             }
4532 
4533             return function( elem ) {
4534                 var node = elem;
4535 
4536                 switch ( type ) {
4537                     case "only":
4538                     case "first":
4539                         while ( (node = node.previousSibling) ) {
4540                             if ( node.nodeType === 1 ) {
4541                                 return false;
4542                             }
4543                         }
4544 
4545                         if ( type === "first" ) {
4546                             return true;
4547                         }
4548 
4549                         node = elem;
4550 
4551                         /* falls through */
4552                     case "last":
4553                         while ( (node = node.nextSibling) ) {
4554                             if ( node.nodeType === 1 ) {
4555                                 return false;
4556                             }
4557                         }
4558 
4559                         return true;
4560                 }
4561             };
4562         },
4563 
4564         "PSEUDO": function( pseudo, argument, context, xml ) {
4565             // pseudo-class names are case-insensitive
4566             // http://www.w3.org/TR/selectors/#pseudo-classes
4567             // Prioritize by case sensitivity in case custom pseudos are added with uppercase letters
4568             var args,
4569                 fn = Expr.pseudos[ pseudo ] || Expr.pseudos[ pseudo.toLowerCase() ];
4570 
4571             if ( !fn ) {
4572                 Sizzle.error( "unsupported pseudo: " + pseudo );
4573             }
4574 
4575             // The user may use createPseudo to indicate that
4576             // arguments are needed to create the filter function
4577             // just as Sizzle does
4578             if ( !fn[ expando ] ) {
4579                 if ( fn.length > 1 ) {
4580                     args = [ pseudo, pseudo, "", argument ];
4581                     return function( elem ) {
4582                         return fn( elem, 0, args );
4583                     };
4584                 }
4585                 return fn;
4586             }
4587 
4588             return fn( argument, context, xml );
4589         }
4590     },
4591 
4592     pseudos: {
4593         "not": markFunction(function( selector, context, xml ) {
4594             // Trim the selector passed to compile
4595             // to avoid treating leading and trailing
4596             // spaces as combinators
4597             var matcher = compile( selector.replace( rtrim, "$1" ), context, xml );
4598             return function( elem ) {
4599                 return !matcher( elem );
4600             };
4601         }),
4602 
4603         "enabled": function( elem ) {
4604             return elem.disabled === false;
4605         },
4606 
4607         "disabled": function( elem ) {
4608             return elem.disabled === true;
4609         },
4610 
4611         "checked": function( elem ) {
4612             // In CSS3, :checked should return both checked and selected elements
4613             // http://www.w3.org/TR/2011/REC-css3-selectors-20110929/#checked
4614             var nodeName = elem.nodeName.toLowerCase();
4615             return (nodeName === "input" && !!elem.checked) || (nodeName === "option" && !!elem.selected);
4616         },
4617 
4618         "selected": function( elem ) {
4619             // Accessing this property makes selected-by-default
4620             // options in Safari work properly
4621             if ( elem.parentNode ) {
4622                 elem.parentNode.selectedIndex;
4623             }
4624 
4625             return elem.selected === true;
4626         },
4627 
4628         "parent": function( elem ) {
4629             return !Expr.pseudos["empty"]( elem );
4630         },
4631 
4632         "empty": function( elem ) {
4633             // http://www.w3.org/TR/selectors/#empty-pseudo
4634             // :empty is only affected by element nodes and content nodes(including text(3), cdata(4)),
4635             //   not comment, processing instructions, or others
4636             // Thanks to Diego Perini for the nodeName shortcut
4637             //   Greater than "@" means alpha characters (specifically not starting with "#" or "?")
4638             var nodeType;
4639             elem = elem.firstChild;
4640             while ( elem ) {
4641                 if ( elem.nodeName > "@" || (nodeType = elem.nodeType) === 3 || nodeType === 4 ) {
4642                     return false;
4643                 }
4644                 elem = elem.nextSibling;
4645             }
4646             return true;
4647         },
4648 
4649         "contains": markFunction(function( text ) {
4650             return function( elem ) {
4651                 return ( elem.textContent || elem.innerText || getText( elem ) ).indexOf( text ) > -1;
4652             };
4653         }),
4654 
4655         "has": markFunction(function( selector ) {
4656             return function( elem ) {
4657                 return Sizzle( selector, elem ).length > 0;
4658             };
4659         }),
4660 
4661         "header": function( elem ) {
4662             return rheader.test( elem.nodeName );
4663         },
4664 
4665         "text": function( elem ) {
4666             var type, attr;
4667             // IE6 and 7 will map elem.type to 'text' for new HTML5 types (search, etc)
4668             // use getAttribute instead to test this case
4669             return elem.nodeName.toLowerCase() === "input" &&
4670                 (type = elem.type) === "text" &&
4671                 ( (attr = elem.getAttribute("type")) == null || attr.toLowerCase() === type );
4672         },
4673 
4674         // Input types
4675         "radio": createInputPseudo("radio"),
4676         "checkbox": createInputPseudo("checkbox"),
4677         "file": createInputPseudo("file"),
4678         "password": createInputPseudo("password"),
4679         "image": createInputPseudo("image"),
4680 
4681         "submit": createButtonPseudo("submit"),
4682         "reset": createButtonPseudo("reset"),
4683 
4684         "button": function( elem ) {
4685             var name = elem.nodeName.toLowerCase();
4686             return name === "input" && elem.type === "button" || name === "button";
4687         },
4688 
4689         "input": function( elem ) {
4690             return rinputs.test( elem.nodeName );
4691         },
4692 
4693         "focus": function( elem ) {
4694             var doc = elem.ownerDocument;
4695             return elem === doc.activeElement && (!doc.hasFocus || doc.hasFocus()) && !!(elem.type || elem.href);
4696         },
4697 
4698         "active": function( elem ) {
4699             return elem === elem.ownerDocument.activeElement;
4700         }
4701     },
4702 
4703     setFilters: {
4704         "first": function( elements, argument, not ) {
4705             return not ? elements.slice( 1 ) : [ elements[0] ];
4706         },
4707 
4708         "last": function( elements, argument, not ) {
4709             var elem = elements.pop();
4710             return not ? elements : [ elem ];
4711         },
4712 
4713         "even": function( elements, argument, not ) {
4714             var results = [],
4715                 i = not ? 1 : 0,
4716                 len = elements.length;
4717             for ( ; i < len; i = i + 2 ) {
4718                 results.push( elements[i] );
4719             }
4720             return results;
4721         },
4722 
4723         "odd": function( elements, argument, not ) {
4724             var results = [],
4725                 i = not ? 0 : 1,
4726                 len = elements.length;
4727             for ( ; i < len; i = i + 2 ) {
4728                 results.push( elements[i] );
4729             }
4730             return results;
4731         },
4732 
4733         "lt": function( elements, argument, not ) {
4734             return not ? elements.slice( +argument ) : elements.slice( 0, +argument );
4735         },
4736 
4737         "gt": function( elements, argument, not ) {
4738             return not ? elements.slice( 0, +argument + 1 ) : elements.slice( +argument + 1 );
4739         },
4740 
4741         "eq": function( elements, argument, not ) {
4742             var elem = elements.splice( +argument, 1 );
4743             return not ? elements : elem;
4744         }
4745     }
4746 };
4747 
4748 function siblingCheck( a, b, ret ) {
4749     if ( a === b ) {
4750         return ret;
4751     }
4752 
4753     var cur = a.nextSibling;
4754 
4755     while ( cur ) {
4756         if ( cur === b ) {
4757             return -1;
4758         }
4759 
4760         cur = cur.nextSibling;
4761     }
4762 
4763     return 1;
4764 }
4765 
4766 sortOrder = docElem.compareDocumentPosition ?
4767     function( a, b ) {
4768         if ( a === b ) {
4769             hasDuplicate = true;
4770             return 0;
4771         }
4772 
4773         return ( !a.compareDocumentPosition || !b.compareDocumentPosition ?
4774             a.compareDocumentPosition :
4775             a.compareDocumentPosition(b) & 4
4776         ) ? -1 : 1;
4777     } :
4778     function( a, b ) {
4779         // The nodes are identical, we can exit early
4780         if ( a === b ) {
4781             hasDuplicate = true;
4782             return 0;
4783 
4784         // Fallback to using sourceIndex (in IE) if it's available on both nodes
4785         } else if ( a.sourceIndex && b.sourceIndex ) {
4786             return a.sourceIndex - b.sourceIndex;
4787         }
4788 
4789         var al, bl,
4790             ap = [],
4791             bp = [],
4792             aup = a.parentNode,
4793             bup = b.parentNode,
4794             cur = aup;
4795 
4796         // If the nodes are siblings (or identical) we can do a quick check
4797         if ( aup === bup ) {
4798             return siblingCheck( a, b );
4799 
4800         // If no parents were found then the nodes are disconnected
4801         } else if ( !aup ) {
4802             return -1;
4803 
4804         } else if ( !bup ) {
4805             return 1;
4806         }
4807 
4808         // Otherwise they're somewhere else in the tree so we need
4809         // to build up a full list of the parentNodes for comparison
4810         while ( cur ) {
4811             ap.unshift( cur );
4812             cur = cur.parentNode;
4813         }
4814 
4815         cur = bup;
4816 
4817         while ( cur ) {
4818             bp.unshift( cur );
4819             cur = cur.parentNode;
4820         }
4821 
4822         al = ap.length;
4823         bl = bp.length;
4824 
4825         // Start walking down the tree looking for a discrepancy
4826         for ( var i = 0; i < al && i < bl; i++ ) {
4827             if ( ap[i] !== bp[i] ) {
4828                 return siblingCheck( ap[i], bp[i] );
4829             }
4830         }
4831 
4832         // We ended someplace up the tree so do a sibling check
4833         return i === al ?
4834             siblingCheck( a, bp[i], -1 ) :
4835             siblingCheck( ap[i], b, 1 );
4836     };
4837 
4838 // Always assume the presence of duplicates if sort doesn't
4839 // pass them to our comparison function (as in Google Chrome).
4840 [0, 0].sort( sortOrder );
4841 baseHasDuplicate = !hasDuplicate;
4842 
4843 // Document sorting and removing duplicates
4844 Sizzle.uniqueSort = function( results ) {
4845     var elem,
4846         i = 1;
4847 
4848     hasDuplicate = baseHasDuplicate;
4849     results.sort( sortOrder );
4850 
4851     if ( hasDuplicate ) {
4852         for ( ; (elem = results[i]); i++ ) {
4853             if ( elem === results[ i - 1 ] ) {
4854                 results.splice( i--, 1 );
4855             }
4856         }
4857     }
4858 
4859     return results;
4860 };
4861 
4862 Sizzle.error = function( msg ) {
4863     throw new Error( "Syntax error, unrecognized expression: " + msg );
4864 };
4865 
4866 function tokenize( selector, context, xml, parseOnly ) {
4867     var matched, match, tokens, type,
4868         soFar, groups, group, i,
4869         preFilters, filters,
4870         checkContext = !xml && context !== document,
4871         // Token cache should maintain spaces
4872         key = ( checkContext ? "<s>" : "" ) + selector.replace( rtrim, "$1<s>" ),
4873         cached = tokenCache[ expando ][ key ];
4874 
4875     if ( cached ) {
4876         return parseOnly ? 0 : slice.call( cached, 0 );
4877     }
4878 
4879     soFar = selector;
4880     groups = [];
4881     i = 0;
4882     preFilters = Expr.preFilter;
4883     filters = Expr.filter;
4884 
4885     while ( soFar ) {
4886 
4887         // Comma and first run
4888         if ( !matched || (match = rcomma.exec( soFar )) ) {
4889             if ( match ) {
4890                 soFar = soFar.slice( match[0].length );
4891                 tokens.selector = group;
4892             }
4893             groups.push( tokens = [] );
4894             group = "";
4895 
4896             // Need to make sure we're within a narrower context if necessary
4897             // Adding a descendant combinator will generate what is needed
4898             if ( checkContext ) {
4899                 soFar = " " + soFar;
4900             }
4901         }
4902 
4903         matched = false;
4904 
4905         // Combinators
4906         if ( (match = rcombinators.exec( soFar )) ) {
4907             group += match[0];
4908             soFar = soFar.slice( match[0].length );
4909 
4910             // Cast descendant combinators to space
4911             matched = tokens.push({
4912                 part: match.pop().replace( rtrim, " " ),
4913                 string: match[0],
4914                 captures: match
4915             });
4916         }
4917 
4918         // Filters
4919         for ( type in filters ) {
4920             if ( (match = matchExpr[ type ].exec( soFar )) && (!preFilters[ type ] ||
4921                 ( match = preFilters[ type ](match, context, xml) )) ) {
4922 
4923                 group += match[0];
4924                 soFar = soFar.slice( match[0].length );
4925                 matched = tokens.push({
4926                     part: type,
4927                     string: match.shift(),
4928                     captures: match
4929                 });
4930             }
4931         }
4932 
4933         if ( !matched ) {
4934             break;
4935         }
4936     }
4937 
4938     // Attach the full group as a selector
4939     if ( group ) {
4940         tokens.selector = group;
4941     }
4942 
4943     // Return the length of the invalid excess
4944     // if we're just parsing
4945     // Otherwise, throw an error or return tokens
4946     return parseOnly ?
4947         soFar.length :
4948         soFar ?
4949             Sizzle.error( selector ) :
4950             // Cache the tokens
4951             slice.call( tokenCache(key, groups), 0 );
4952 }
4953 
4954 function addCombinator( matcher, combinator, context, xml ) {
4955     var dir = combinator.dir,
4956         doneName = done++;
4957 
4958     if ( !matcher ) {
4959         // If there is no matcher to check, check against the context
4960         matcher = function( elem ) {
4961             return elem === context;
4962         };
4963     }
4964     return combinator.first ?
4965         function( elem ) {
4966             while ( (elem = elem[ dir ]) ) {
4967                 if ( elem.nodeType === 1 ) {
4968                     return matcher( elem ) && elem;
4969                 }
4970             }
4971         } :
4972         xml ?
4973             function( elem ) {
4974                 while ( (elem = elem[ dir ]) ) {
4975                     if ( elem.nodeType === 1 ) {
4976                         if ( matcher( elem ) ) {
4977                             return elem;
4978                         }
4979                     }
4980                 }
4981             } :
4982             function( elem ) {
4983                 var cache,
4984                     dirkey = doneName + "." + dirruns,
4985                     cachedkey = dirkey + "." + cachedruns;
4986                 while ( (elem = elem[ dir ]) ) {
4987                     if ( elem.nodeType === 1 ) {
4988                         if ( (cache = elem[ expando ]) === cachedkey ) {
4989                             return elem.sizset;
4990                         } else if ( typeof cache === "string" && cache.indexOf(dirkey) === 0 ) {
4991                             if ( elem.sizset ) {
4992                                 return elem;
4993                             }
4994                         } else {
4995                             elem[ expando ] = cachedkey;
4996                             if ( matcher( elem ) ) {
4997                                 elem.sizset = true;
4998                                 return elem;
4999                             }
5000                             elem.sizset = false;
5001                         }
5002                     }
5003                 }
5004             };
5005 }
5006 
5007 function addMatcher( higher, deeper ) {
5008     return higher ?
5009         function( elem ) {
5010             var result = deeper( elem );
5011             return result && higher( result === true ? elem : result );
5012         } :
5013         deeper;
5014 }
5015 
5016 // ["TAG", ">", "ID", " ", "CLASS"]
5017 function matcherFromTokens( tokens, context, xml ) {
5018     var token, matcher,
5019         i = 0;
5020 
5021     for ( ; (token = tokens[i]); i++ ) {
5022         if ( Expr.relative[ token.part ] ) {
5023             matcher = addCombinator( matcher, Expr.relative[ token.part ], context, xml );
5024         } else {
5025             matcher = addMatcher( matcher, Expr.filter[ token.part ].apply(null, token.captures.concat( context, xml )) );
5026         }
5027     }
5028 
5029     return matcher;
5030 }
5031 
5032 function matcherFromGroupMatchers( matchers ) {
5033     return function( elem ) {
5034         var matcher,
5035             j = 0;
5036         for ( ; (matcher = matchers[j]); j++ ) {
5037             if ( matcher(elem) ) {
5038                 return true;
5039             }
5040         }
5041         return false;
5042     };
5043 }
5044 
5045 compile = Sizzle.compile = function( selector, context, xml ) {
5046     var group, i, len,
5047         cached = compilerCache[ expando ][ selector ];
5048 
5049     // Return a cached group function if already generated (context dependent)
5050     if ( cached && cached.context === context ) {
5051         return cached;
5052     }
5053 
5054     // Generate a function of recursive functions that can be used to check each element
5055     group = tokenize( selector, context, xml );
5056     for ( i = 0, len = group.length; i < len; i++ ) {
5057         group[i] = matcherFromTokens(group[i], context, xml);
5058     }
5059 
5060     // Cache the compiled function
5061     cached = compilerCache( selector, matcherFromGroupMatchers(group) );
5062     cached.context = context;
5063     cached.runs = cached.dirruns = 0;
5064     return cached;
5065 };
5066 
5067 function multipleContexts( selector, contexts, results, seed ) {
5068     var i = 0,
5069         len = contexts.length;
5070     for ( ; i < len; i++ ) {
5071         Sizzle( selector, contexts[i], results, seed );
5072     }
5073 }
5074 
5075 function handlePOSGroup( selector, posfilter, argument, contexts, seed, not ) {
5076     var results,
5077         fn = Expr.setFilters[ posfilter.toLowerCase() ];
5078 
5079     if ( !fn ) {
5080         Sizzle.error( posfilter );
5081     }
5082 
5083     if ( selector || !(results = seed) ) {
5084         multipleContexts( selector || "*", contexts, (results = []), seed );
5085     }
5086 
5087     return results.length > 0 ? fn( results, argument, not ) : [];
5088 }
5089 
5090 function handlePOS( groups, context, results, seed ) {
5091     var group, part, j, groupLen, token, selector,
5092         anchor, elements, match, matched,
5093         lastIndex, currentContexts, not,
5094         i = 0,
5095         len = groups.length,
5096         rpos = matchExpr["POS"],
5097         // This is generated here in case matchExpr["POS"] is extended
5098         rposgroups = new RegExp( "^" + rpos.source + "(?!" + whitespace + ")", "i" ),
5099         // This is for making sure non-participating
5100         // matching groups are represented cross-browser (IE6-8)
5101         setUndefined = function() {
5102             var i = 1,
5103                 len = arguments.length - 2;
5104             for ( ; i < len; i++ ) {
5105                 if ( arguments[i] === undefined ) {
5106                     match[i] = undefined;
5107                 }
5108             }
5109         };
5110 
5111     for ( ; i < len; i++ ) {
5112         group = groups[i];
5113         part = "";
5114         elements = seed;
5115         for ( j = 0, groupLen = group.length; j < groupLen; j++ ) {
5116             token = group[j];
5117             selector = token.string;
5118             if ( token.part === "PSEUDO" ) {
5119                 // Reset regex index to 0
5120                 rpos.exec("");
5121                 anchor = 0;
5122                 while ( (match = rpos.exec( selector )) ) {
5123                     matched = true;
5124                     lastIndex = rpos.lastIndex = match.index + match[0].length;
5125                     if ( lastIndex > anchor ) {
5126                         part += selector.slice( anchor, match.index );
5127                         anchor = lastIndex;
5128                         currentContexts = [ context ];
5129 
5130                         if ( rcombinators.test(part) ) {
5131                             if ( elements ) {
5132                                 currentContexts = elements;
5133                             }
5134                             elements = seed;
5135                         }
5136 
5137                         if ( (not = rendsWithNot.test( part )) ) {
5138                             part = part.slice( 0, -5 ).replace( rcombinators, "$&*" );
5139                             anchor++;
5140                         }
5141 
5142                         if ( match.length > 1 ) {
5143                             match[0].replace( rposgroups, setUndefined );
5144                         }
5145                         elements = handlePOSGroup( part, match[1], match[2], currentContexts, elements, not );
5146                     }
5147                     part = "";
5148                 }
5149 
5150             }
5151 
5152             if ( !matched ) {
5153                 part += selector;
5154             }
5155             matched = false;
5156         }
5157 
5158         if ( part ) {
5159             if ( rcombinators.test(part) ) {
5160                 multipleContexts( part, elements || [ context ], results, seed );
5161             } else {
5162                 Sizzle( part, context, results, seed ? seed.concat(elements) : elements );
5163             }
5164         } else {
5165             push.apply( results, elements );
5166         }
5167     }
5168 
5169     // Do not sort if this is a single filter
5170     return len === 1 ? results : Sizzle.uniqueSort( results );
5171 }
5172 
5173 function select( selector, context, results, seed, xml ) {
5174     // Remove excessive whitespace
5175     selector = selector.replace( rtrim, "$1" );
5176     var elements, matcher, cached, elem,
5177         i, tokens, token, lastToken, findContext, type,
5178         match = tokenize( selector, context, xml ),
5179         contextNodeType = context.nodeType;
5180 
5181     // POS handling
5182     if ( matchExpr["POS"].test(selector) ) {
5183         return handlePOS( match, context, results, seed );
5184     }
5185 
5186     if ( seed ) {
5187         elements = slice.call( seed, 0 );
5188 
5189     // To maintain document order, only narrow the
5190     // set if there is one group
5191     } else if ( match.length === 1 ) {
5192 
5193         // Take a shortcut and set the context if the root selector is an ID
5194         if ( (tokens = slice.call( match[0], 0 )).length > 2 &&
5195                 (token = tokens[0]).part === "ID" &&
5196                 contextNodeType === 9 && !xml &&
5197                 Expr.relative[ tokens[1].part ] ) {
5198 
5199             context = Expr.find["ID"]( token.captures[0].replace( rbackslash, "" ), context, xml )[0];
5200             if ( !context ) {
5201                 return results;
5202             }
5203 
5204             selector = selector.slice( tokens.shift().string.length );
5205         }
5206 
5207         findContext = ( (match = rsibling.exec( tokens[0].string )) && !match.index && context.parentNode ) || context;
5208 
5209         // Reduce the set if possible
5210         lastToken = "";
5211         for ( i = tokens.length - 1; i >= 0; i-- ) {
5212             token = tokens[i];
5213             type = token.part;
5214             lastToken = token.string + lastToken;
5215             if ( Expr.relative[ type ] ) {
5216                 break;
5217             }
5218             if ( Expr.order.test(type) ) {
5219                 elements = Expr.find[ type ]( token.captures[0].replace( rbackslash, "" ), findContext, xml );
5220                 if ( elements == null ) {
5221                     continue;
5222                 } else {
5223                     selector = selector.slice( 0, selector.length - lastToken.length ) +
5224                         lastToken.replace( matchExpr[ type ], "" );
5225 
5226                     if ( !selector ) {
5227                         push.apply( results, slice.call(elements, 0) );
5228                     }
5229 
5230                     break;
5231                 }
5232             }
5233         }
5234     }
5235 
5236     // Only loop over the given elements once
5237     if ( selector ) {
5238         matcher = compile( selector, context, xml );
5239         dirruns = matcher.dirruns++;
5240         if ( elements == null ) {
5241             elements = Expr.find["TAG"]( "*", (rsibling.test( selector ) && context.parentNode) || context );
5242         }
5243 
5244         for ( i = 0; (elem = elements[i]); i++ ) {
5245             cachedruns = matcher.runs++;
5246             if ( matcher(elem) ) {
5247                 results.push( elem );
5248             }
5249         }
5250     }
5251 
5252     return results;
5253 }
5254 
5255 if ( document.querySelectorAll ) {
5256     (function() {
5257         var disconnectedMatch,
5258             oldSelect = select,
5259             rescape = /'|\\/g,
5260             rattributeQuotes = /\=[\x20\t\r\n\f]*([^'"\]]*)[\x20\t\r\n\f]*\]/g,
5261             rbuggyQSA = [],
5262             // matchesSelector(:active) reports false when true (IE9/Opera 11.5)
5263             // A support test would require too much code (would include document ready)
5264             // just skip matchesSelector for :active
5265             rbuggyMatches = [":active"],
5266             matches = docElem.matchesSelector ||
5267                 docElem.mozMatchesSelector ||
5268                 docElem.webkitMatchesSelector ||
5269                 docElem.oMatchesSelector ||
5270                 docElem.msMatchesSelector;
5271 
5272         // Build QSA regex
5273         // Regex strategy adopted from Diego Perini
5274         assert(function( div ) {
5275             // Select is set to empty string on purpose
5276             // This is to test IE's treatment of not explictly
5277             // setting a boolean content attribute,
5278             // since its presence should be enough
5279             // http://bugs.jquery.com/ticket/12359
5280             div.innerHTML = "<select><option selected=''></option></select>";
5281 
5282             // IE8 - Some boolean attributes are not treated correctly
5283             if ( !div.querySelectorAll("[selected]").length ) {
5284                 rbuggyQSA.push( "\\[" + whitespace + "*(?:checked|disabled|ismap|multiple|readonly|selected|value)" );
5285             }
5286 
5287             // Webkit/Opera - :checked should return selected option elements
5288             // http://www.w3.org/TR/2011/REC-css3-selectors-20110929/#checked
5289             // IE8 throws error here (do not put tests after this one)
5290             if ( !div.querySelectorAll(":checked").length ) {
5291                 rbuggyQSA.push(":checked");
5292             }
5293         });
5294 
5295         assert(function( div ) {
5296 
5297             // Opera 10-12/IE9 - ^= $= *= and empty values
5298             // Should not select anything
5299             div.innerHTML = "<p test=''></p>";
5300             if ( div.querySelectorAll("[test^='']").length ) {
5301                 rbuggyQSA.push( "[*^$]=" + whitespace + "*(?:\"\"|'')" );
5302             }
5303 
5304             // FF 3.5 - :enabled/:disabled and hidden elements (hidden elements are still enabled)
5305             // IE8 throws error here (do not put tests after this one)
5306             div.innerHTML = "<input type='hidden'/>";
5307             if ( !div.querySelectorAll(":enabled").length ) {
5308                 rbuggyQSA.push(":enabled", ":disabled");
5309             }
5310         });
5311 
5312         rbuggyQSA = rbuggyQSA.length && new RegExp( rbuggyQSA.join("|") );
5313 
5314         select = function( selector, context, results, seed, xml ) {
5315             // Only use querySelectorAll when not filtering,
5316             // when this is not xml,
5317             // and when no QSA bugs apply
5318             if ( !seed && !xml && (!rbuggyQSA || !rbuggyQSA.test( selector )) ) {
5319                 if ( context.nodeType === 9 ) {
5320                     try {
5321                         push.apply( results, slice.call(context.querySelectorAll( selector ), 0) );
5322                         return results;
5323                     } catch(qsaError) {}
5324                 // qSA works strangely on Element-rooted queries
5325                 // We can work around this by specifying an extra ID on the root
5326                 // and working up from there (Thanks to Andrew Dupont for the technique)
5327                 // IE 8 doesn't work on object elements
5328                 } else if ( context.nodeType === 1 && context.nodeName.toLowerCase() !== "object" ) {
5329                     var groups, i, len,
5330                         old = context.getAttribute("id"),
5331                         nid = old || expando,
5332                         newContext = rsibling.test( selector ) && context.parentNode || context;
5333 
5334                     if ( old ) {
5335                         nid = nid.replace( rescape, "\\$&" );
5336                     } else {
5337                         context.setAttribute( "id", nid );
5338                     }
5339 
5340                     groups = tokenize(selector, context, xml);
5341                     // Trailing space is unnecessary
5342                     // There is always a context check
5343                     nid = "[id='" + nid + "']";
5344                     for ( i = 0, len = groups.length; i < len; i++ ) {
5345                         groups[i] = nid + groups[i].selector;
5346                     }
5347                     try {
5348                         push.apply( results, slice.call( newContext.querySelectorAll(
5349                             groups.join(",")
5350                         ), 0 ) );
5351                         return results;
5352                     } catch(qsaError) {
5353                     } finally {
5354                         if ( !old ) {
5355                             context.removeAttribute("id");
5356                         }
5357                     }
5358                 }
5359             }
5360 
5361             return oldSelect( selector, context, results, seed, xml );
5362         };
5363 
5364         if ( matches ) {
5365             assert(function( div ) {
5366                 // Check to see if it's possible to do matchesSelector
5367                 // on a disconnected node (IE 9)
5368                 disconnectedMatch = matches.call( div, "div" );
5369 
5370                 // This should fail with an exception
5371                 // Gecko does not error, returns false instead
5372                 try {
5373                     matches.call( div, "[test!='']:sizzle" );
5374                     rbuggyMatches.push( matchExpr["PSEUDO"].source, matchExpr["POS"].source, "!=" );
5375                 } catch ( e ) {}
5376             });
5377 
5378             // rbuggyMatches always contains :active, so no need for a length check
5379             rbuggyMatches = /* rbuggyMatches.length && */ new RegExp( rbuggyMatches.join("|") );
5380 
5381             Sizzle.matchesSelector = function( elem, expr ) {
5382                 // Make sure that attribute selectors are quoted
5383                 expr = expr.replace( rattributeQuotes, "='$1']" );
5384 
5385                 // rbuggyMatches always contains :active, so no need for an existence check
5386                 if ( !isXML( elem ) && !rbuggyMatches.test( expr ) && (!rbuggyQSA || !rbuggyQSA.test( expr )) ) {
5387                     try {
5388                         var ret = matches.call( elem, expr );
5389 
5390                         // IE 9's matchesSelector returns false on disconnected nodes
5391                         if ( ret || disconnectedMatch ||
5392                                 // As well, disconnected nodes are said to be in a document
5393                                 // fragment in IE 9
5394                                 elem.document && elem.document.nodeType !== 11 ) {
5395                             return ret;
5396                         }
5397                     } catch(e) {}
5398                 }
5399 
5400                 return Sizzle( expr, null, null, [ elem ] ).length > 0;
5401             };
5402         }
5403     })();

5436 jQuery.fn.extend({
5437     find: function( selector ) {
5438         var i, l, length, n, r, ret,
5439             self = this;
5440 
5441         if ( typeof selector !== "string" ) {
5442             return jQuery( selector ).filter(function() {
5443                 for ( i = 0, l = self.length; i < l; i++ ) {
5444                     if ( jQuery.contains( self[ i ], this ) ) {
5445                         return true;
5446                     }
5447                 }
5448             });
5449         }
5450 
5451         ret = this.pushStack( "", "find", selector );
5452 
5453         for ( i = 0, l = this.length; i < l; i++ ) {
5454             length = ret.length;
5455             jQuery.find( selector, this[i], ret );
5456 
5457             if ( i > 0 ) {
5458                 // Make sure that the results are unique
5459                 for ( n = length; n < ret.length; n++ ) {
5460                     for ( r = 0; r < length; r++ ) {
5461                         if ( ret[r] === ret[n] ) {
5462                             ret.splice(n--, 1);
5463                             break;
5464                         }
5465                     }
5466                 }
5467             }
5468         }
5469

5495     is: function( selector ) {
5496         return !!selector && (
5497             typeof selector === "string" ?
5498                 // If this is a positional/relative selector, check membership in the returned set
5499                 // so $("p:first").is("p:last") won't return true for a doc with two "p".
5500                 rneedsContext.test( selector ) ?
5501                     jQuery( selector, this.context ).index( this[0] ) >= 0 :
5502                     jQuery.filter( selector, this ).length > 0 :

5506     closest: function( selectors, context ) {
5507         var cur,
5508             i = 0,
5509             l = this.length,
5510             ret = [],

5512                 jQuery( selectors, context || this.context ) :

5520                     ret.push( cur );

5547         return jQuery.inArray(

5549             elem.jquery ? elem[0] : elem, this );

5685 // Implement the identical functionality for filter and not
5686 function winnow( elements, qualifier, keep ) {
5687 
5688     // Can't pass null or undefined to indexOf in Firefox 4
5689     // Set to 0 to skip string check
5690     qualifier = qualifier || 0;
5691 
5692     if ( jQuery.isFunction( qualifier ) ) {
5693         return jQuery.grep(elements, function( elem, i ) {
5694             var retVal = !!qualifier.call( elem, i, elem );
5695             return retVal === keep;
5696         });
5697 
5698     } else if ( qualifier.nodeType ) {
5699         return jQuery.grep(elements, function( elem, i ) {
5700             return ( elem === qualifier ) === keep;
5701         });
5702 
5703     } else if ( typeof qualifier === "string" ) {
5704         var filtered = jQuery.grep(elements, function( elem ) {
5705             return elem.nodeType === 1;
5706         });
5707 
5708         if ( isSimple.test( qualifier ) ) {
5709             return jQuery.filter(qualifier, filtered, !keep);
5710         } else {
5711             qualifier = jQuery.filter( qualifier, filtered );
5712         }
5713     }
5714 
5715     return jQuery.grep(elements, function( elem, i ) {
5716         return ( jQuery.inArray( elem, qualifier ) >= 0 ) === keep;
5717     });
5718 }

5720 // 生成安全fragment
5721 function createSafeFragment( document ) {
5722     var list = nodeNames.split( "|" ),
5723     safeFrag = document.createDocumentFragment();
5724 
5725     if ( safeFrag.createElement ) {
5726         // 使用pop()弹出数组元素，数组元素变为0时被转换为false，循环结束
5727         while ( list.length ) {
5728             safeFrag.createElement(
5729                 list.pop()
5730             );
5731         }
5732     }
5733     return safeFrag;
5734 }

5940     html: function( value ) {
5941         return jQuery.access( this, function( value ) {
5942             var elem = this[0] || {},
5943                 i = 0,
5944                 l = this.length;
5945 
5946             if ( value === undefined ) {
5947                 return elem.nodeType === 1 ?
5948                     elem.innerHTML.replace( rinlinejQuery, "" ) :
5949                     undefined;
5950             }
5951 
5952             // See if we can take a shortcut and just use innerHTML
5953             if ( typeof value === "string" && !rnoInnerhtml.test( value ) &&
5954                 ( jQuery.support.htmlSerialize || !rnoshimcache.test( value )  ) &&
5955                 ( jQuery.support.leadingWhitespace || !rleadingWhitespace.test( value ) ) &&
5956                 !wrapMap[ ( rtagName.exec( value ) || ["", ""] )[1].toLowerCase() ] ) {
5957 
5958                 value = value.replace( rxhtmlTag, "<$1></$2>" );
5959 
5960                 try {
5961                     for (; i < l; i++ ) {
5962                         // Remove element nodes and prevent memory leaks
5963                         elem = this[i] || {};
5964                         if ( elem.nodeType === 1 ) {
5965                             jQuery.cleanData( elem.getElementsByTagName( "*" ) );
5966                             elem.innerHTML = value;
5967                         }
5968                     }
5969 
5970                     elem = 0;
5971 
5972                 // If using innerHTML throws an exception, use the fallback method
5973                 } catch(e) {}
5974             }
5975 
5976             if ( elem ) {
5977                 this.empty().append( value );
5978             }
5979         }, null, value, arguments.length );
5980     },
5981 
5982     replaceWith: function( value ) {
5983         if ( !isDisconnected( this[0] ) ) {
5984             // Make sure that the elements are removed from the DOM before they are inserted
5985             // this can help fix replacing a parent with child elements
5986             if ( jQuery.isFunction( value ) ) {
5987                 return this.each(function(i) {
5988                     var self = jQuery(this), old = self.html();
5989                     self.replaceWith( value.call( this, i, old ) );
5990                 });
5991             }
5992 
5993             if ( typeof value !== "string" ) {
5994                 value = jQuery( value ).detach();
5995             }
5996 
5997             return this.each(function() {
5998                 var next = this.nextSibling,
5999                     parent = this.parentNode;
6000 
6001                 jQuery( this ).remove();
6002 
6003                 if ( next ) {
6004                     jQuery(next).before( value );
6005                 } else {
6006                     jQuery(parent).append( value );
6007                 }
6008             });
6009         }
6010 
6011         return this.length ?
6012             this.pushStack( jQuery(jQuery.isFunction(value) ? value() : value), "replaceWith", value ) :
6013             this;
6014     },
6015 
6016     detach: function( selector ) {
6017         return this.remove( selector, true );
6018     },
6019 
6020     domManip: function( args, table, callback ) {
6021 
6022         // Flatten any nested arrays
6023         args = [].concat.apply( [], args );
6024 
6025         var results, first, fragment, iNoClone,
6026             i = 0,
6027             value = args[0],
6028             scripts = [],
6029             l = this.length;
6030 
6031         // We can't cloneNode fragments that contain checked, in WebKit
6032         if ( !jQuery.support.checkClone && l > 1 && typeof value === "string" && rchecked.test( value ) ) {
6033             return this.each(function() {
6034                 jQuery(this).domManip( args, table, callback );
6035             });
6036         }
6037 
6038         if ( jQuery.isFunction(value) ) {
6039             return this.each(function(i) {
6040                 var self = jQuery(this);
6041                 args[0] = value.call( this, i, table ? self.html() : undefined );
6042                 self.domManip( args, table, callback );
6043             });
6044         }
6045 
6046         if ( this[0] ) {
6047             results = jQuery.buildFragment( args, this, scripts );
6048             fragment = results.fragment;
6049             first = fragment.firstChild;
6050 
6051             if ( fragment.childNodes.length === 1 ) {
6052                 fragment = first;
6053             }
6054 
6055             if ( first ) {
6056                 table = table && jQuery.nodeName( first, "tr" );
6057 
6058                 // Use the original fragment for the last item instead of the first because it can end up
6059                 // being emptied incorrectly in certain situations (#8070).
6060                 // Fragments from the fragment cache must always be cloned and never used in place.
6061                 for ( iNoClone = results.cacheable || l - 1; i < l; i++ ) {
6062                     callback.call(
6063                         table && jQuery.nodeName( this[i], "table" ) ?
6064                             findOrAppend( this[i], "tbody" ) :
6065                             this[i],
6066                         i === iNoClone ?
6067                             fragment :
6068                             jQuery.clone( fragment, true, true )
6069                     );
6070                 }
6071             }
6072 
6073             // Fix #11809: Avoid leaking memory
6074             fragment = first = null;
6075 
6076             if ( scripts.length ) {
6077                 jQuery.each( scripts, function( i, elem ) {
6078                     if ( elem.src ) {
6079                         if ( jQuery.ajax ) {
6080                             jQuery.ajax({
6081                                 url: elem.src,
6082                                 type: "GET",
6083                                 dataType: "script",
6084                                 async: false,
6085                                 global: false,
6086                                 "throws": true
6087                             });
6088                         } else {
6089                             jQuery.error("no ajax");
6090                         }
6091                     } else {
6092                         jQuery.globalEval( ( elem.text || elem.textContent || elem.innerHTML || "" ).replace( rcleanScript, "" ) );
6093                     }
6094 
6095                     if ( elem.parentNode ) {
6096                         elem.parentNode.removeChild( elem );
6097                     }
6098                 });
6099             }
6100         }
6101 
6102         return this;
6103     }
6104 });
6105 
6106 function findOrAppend( elem, tag ) {
6107     return elem.getElementsByTagName( tag )[0] || elem.appendChild( elem.ownerDocument.createElement( tag ) );
6108 }
6109 
6110 function cloneCopyEvent( src, dest ) {
6111 
6112     if ( dest.nodeType !== 1 || !jQuery.hasData( src ) ) {
6113         return;
6114     }
6115 
6116     var type, i, l,
6117         oldData = jQuery._data( src ),
6118         curData = jQuery._data( dest, oldData ),
6119         events = oldData.events;
6120 
6121     if ( events ) {
6122         delete curData.handle;
6123         curData.events = {};
6124 
6125         for ( type in events ) {
6126             for ( i = 0, l = events[ type ].length; i < l; i++ ) {
6127                 jQuery.event.add( dest, type, events[ type ][ i ] );
6128             }
6129         }
6130     }
6131 
6132     // make the cloned public data object a copy from the original
6133     if ( curData.data ) {
6134         curData.data = jQuery.extend( {}, curData.data );
6135     }
6136 }
6137 
6138 function cloneFixAttributes( src, dest ) {
6139     var nodeName;
6140 
6141     // We do not need to do anything for non-Elements
6142     if ( dest.nodeType !== 1 ) {
6143         return;
6144     }
6145 
6146     // clearAttributes removes the attributes, which we don't want,
6147     // but also removes the attachEvent events, which we *do* want
6148     if ( dest.clearAttributes ) {
6149         dest.clearAttributes();
6150     }
6151 
6152     // mergeAttributes, in contrast, only merges back on the
6153     // original attributes, not the events
6154     if ( dest.mergeAttributes ) {
6155         dest.mergeAttributes( src );
6156     }
6157 
6158     nodeName = dest.nodeName.toLowerCase();
6159 
6160     if ( nodeName === "object" ) {
6161         // IE6-10 improperly clones children of object elements using classid.
6162         // IE10 throws NoModificationAllowedError if parent is null, #12132.
6163         if ( dest.parentNode ) {
6164             dest.outerHTML = src.outerHTML;
6165         }
6166 
6167         // This path appears unavoidable for IE9. When cloning an object
6168         // element in IE9, the outerHTML strategy above is not sufficient.
6169         // If the src has innerHTML and the destination does not,
6170         // copy the src.innerHTML into the dest.innerHTML. #10324
6171         if ( jQuery.support.html5Clone && (src.innerHTML && !jQuery.trim(dest.innerHTML)) ) {
6172             dest.innerHTML = src.innerHTML;
6173         }
6174 
6175     } else if ( nodeName === "input" && rcheckableType.test( src.type ) ) {
6176         // IE6-8 fails to persist the checked state of a cloned checkbox
6177         // or radio button. Worse, IE6-7 fail to give the cloned element
6178         // a checked appearance if the defaultChecked value isn't also set
6179 
6180         dest.defaultChecked = dest.checked = src.checked;
6181 
6182         // IE6-7 get confused and end up setting the value of a cloned
6183         // checkbox/radio button to an empty string instead of "on"
6184         if ( dest.value !== src.value ) {
6185             dest.value = src.value;
6186         }
6187 
6188     // IE6-8 fails to return the selected option to the default selected
6189     // state when cloning options
6190     } else if ( nodeName === "option" ) {
6191         dest.selected = src.defaultSelected;
6192 
6193     // IE6-8 fails to set the defaultValue to the correct value when
6194     // cloning other types of input fields
6195     } else if ( nodeName === "input" || nodeName === "textarea" ) {
6196         dest.defaultValue = src.defaultValue;
6197 
6198     // IE blanks contents when cloning scripts
6199     } else if ( nodeName === "script" && dest.text !== src.text ) {
6200         dest.text = src.text;
6201     }
6202 
6203     // Event data gets referenced instead of copied if the expando
6204     // gets copied too
6205     dest.removeAttribute( jQuery.expando );
6206 }
6207 
6208 jQuery.buildFragment = function( args, context, scripts ) {
6209     var fragment, cacheable, cachehit,
6210         first = args[ 0 ];
6211 
6212     // Set context from what may come in as undefined or a jQuery collection or a node
6213     // Updated to fix #12266 where accessing context[0] could throw an exception in IE9/10 &
6214     // also doubles as fix for #8950 where plain objects caused createDocumentFragment exception
6215     // 处理传入undefined的情况
6216     context = context || document;
6217     // 处理传入jQuery对象的情况
6218     context = !context.nodeType && context[0] || context;
6219     // 处理传入平凡对象的情况
6220     context = context.ownerDocument || context;
6221 
6222     // Only cache "small" (1/2 KB) HTML strings that are associated with the main document
6223     // 只缓存和主文档关联的“小”(0.5KB)的HTML字符串
6224     // Cloning options loses the selected state, so don't cache them
6225     // 复制option标签将丢失选择的状态，不进行缓存
6226     // IE 6 doesn't like it when you put <object> or <embed> elements in a fragment
6227     // IE 6不支持fragment中包含<object> 或 <embed> 
6228     // Also, WebKit does not clone 'checked' attributes on cloneNode, so don't cache
6229     // WebKit不克隆节点的'checked',所以不缓存
6230     // Lastly, IE6,7,8 will not correctly reuse cached fragments that were created from unknown elems #10501
6231     // IE6,7,8不能正确重用从未知元素创建的缓存fragments
6232     if ( args.length === 1 && typeof first === "string" && first.length < 512 && context === document &&
6233         first.charAt(0) === "<" && !rnocache.test( first ) &&
6234         (jQuery.support.checkClone || !rchecked.test( first )) &&
6235         (jQuery.support.html5Clone || !rnoshimcache.test( first )) ) {
6236 
6237         // Mark cacheable and look for a hit
6238         // 从缓存中查找
6239         cacheable = true;
6240         fragment = jQuery.fragments[ first ];
6241         cachehit = fragment !== undefined;
6242     }
6243 
6244     // 未找到缓存的fragment
6245     if ( !fragment ) {
6246         // 在context上创建一个fragment,在jQuery.clean中向其中添加dom元素
6247         fragment = context.createDocumentFragment();
6248         jQuery.clean( args, context, fragment, scripts );
6249 
6250         // Update the cache, but only store false
6251         // unless this is a second parsing of the same content
6252         // 更新缓存，如果fragment为null或者false，则缓存为false，否则返回fragment
6253         if ( cacheable ) {
6254             jQuery.fragments[ first ] = cachehit && fragment;
6255         }
6256     }
6257 
6258     return { fragment: fragment, cacheable: cacheable };
6259 };
6260 
6261 jQuery.fragments = {};
6262 
6263 jQuery.each({
6264     appendTo: "append",
6265     prependTo: "prepend",
6266     insertBefore: "before",
6267     insertAfter: "after",
6268     replaceAll: "replaceWith"
6269 }, function( name, original ) {
6270     jQuery.fn[ name ] = function( selector ) {
6271         var elems,
6272             i = 0,
6273             ret = [],
6274             insert = jQuery( selector ),
6275             l = insert.length,
6276             parent = this.length === 1 && this[0].parentNode;
6277 
6278         if ( (parent == null || parent && parent.nodeType === 11 && parent.childNodes.length === 1) && l === 1 ) {
6279             insert[ original ]( this[0] );
6280             return this;
6281         } else {
6282             for ( ; i < l; i++ ) {
6283                 elems = ( i > 0 ? this.clone(true) : this ).get();
6284                 jQuery( insert[i] )[ original ]( elems );
6285                 ret = ret.concat( elems );
6286             }
6287 
6288             return this.pushStack( ret, name, insert.selector );
6289         }
6290     };
6291 });

6293 function getAll( elem ) {
6294     if ( typeof elem.getElementsByTagName !== "undefined" ) {
6295         return elem.getElementsByTagName( "*" );
6296 
6297     } else if ( typeof elem.querySelectorAll !== "undefined" ) {
6298         return elem.querySelectorAll( "*" );
6299 
6300     } else {
6301         return [];
6302     }
6303 }

6305 // Used in clean, fixes the defaultChecked property
6306 // 在clean中使用，修复checkbox/radio的默认选中属性
6307 function fixDefaultChecked( elem ) {
6308     if ( rcheckableType.test( elem.type ) ) {
6309         elem.defaultChecked = elem.checked;
6310     }

6313 jQuery.extend({
6314     clone: function( elem, dataAndEvents, deepDataAndEvents ) {
6315         var srcElements,
6316             destElements,
6317             i,
6318             clone;
6319 
6320         if ( jQuery.support.html5Clone || jQuery.isXMLDoc(elem) || !rnoshimcache.test( "<" + elem.nodeName + ">" ) ) {
6321             clone = elem.cloneNode( true );
6322 
6323         // IE<=8 does not properly clone detached, unknown element nodes
6324         } else {
6325             fragmentDiv.innerHTML = elem.outerHTML;
6326             fragmentDiv.removeChild( clone = fragmentDiv.firstChild );
6327         }
6328 
6329         if ( (!jQuery.support.noCloneEvent || !jQuery.support.noCloneChecked) &&
6330                 (elem.nodeType === 1 || elem.nodeType === 11) && !jQuery.isXMLDoc(elem) ) {
6331             // IE copies events bound via attachEvent when using cloneNode.
6332             // Calling detachEvent on the clone will also remove the events
6333             // from the original. In order to get around this, we use some
6334             // proprietary methods to clear the events. Thanks to MooTools
6335             // guys for this hotness.
6336 
6337             cloneFixAttributes( elem, clone );
6338 
6339             // Using Sizzle here is crazy slow, so we use getElementsByTagName instead
6340             srcElements = getAll( elem );
6341             destElements = getAll( clone );
6342 
6343             // Weird iteration because IE will replace the length property
6344             // with an element if you are cloning the body and one of the
6345             // elements on the page has a name or id of "length"
6346             for ( i = 0; srcElements[i]; ++i ) {
6347                 // Ensure that the destination node is not null; Fixes #9587
6348                 if ( destElements[i] ) {
6349                     cloneFixAttributes( srcElements[i], destElements[i] );
6350                 }
6351             }
6352         }
6353 
6354         // Copy the events from the original to the clone
6355         if ( dataAndEvents ) {
6356             cloneCopyEvent( elem, clone );
6357 
6358             if ( deepDataAndEvents ) {
6359                 srcElements = getAll( elem );
6360                 destElements = getAll( clone );
6361 
6362                 for ( i = 0; srcElements[i]; ++i ) {
6363                     cloneCopyEvent( srcElements[i], destElements[i] );
6364                 }
6365             }
6366         }
6367 
6368         srcElements = destElements = null;
6369 
6370         // Return the cloned set
6371         return clone;
6372     },
6373 
6374     /*
6375      * 把HTML代码转换为DOM元素
6376      * elems: 待转换HTML代码数组
6377      * context: 文档对象，会调用context的createTextNode方法和createElement方法
6378      * fragment: 文档碎片，在其上插入div，在div上设置innerHTML
6379      * scripts: 脚本数组
6380      */
6381     clean: function( elems, context, fragment, scripts ) {
6382         var i, j, elem, tag, wrap, depth, div, hasBody, tbody, len, handleScript, jsTags,
6383         /*
6384          * AND运算的逻辑如下：
6385          * 如果一个运算数是对象，另一个是 Boolean 值，返回该对象。
6386          * 如果两个运算数都是对象，返回第二个对象。
6387          * 如果某个运算数是 null，返回 null。
6388          * 如果某个运算数是 NaN，返回 NaN。
6389          * 如果某个运算数是 undefined，发生错误。
6390          */
6391             safe = context === document && safeFragment,
6392             ret = [];
6393 
6394         // Ensure that context is a document
6395         // 保证context是document
6396         if ( !context || typeof context.createDocumentFragment === "undefined" ) {
6397             context = document;
6398         }
6399 
6400         // Use the already-created safe fragment if context permits
6401         // 如果context允许，使用已经创建的安全fragment
6402         for ( i = 0; (elem = elems[i]) != null; i++ ) {
6403             if ( typeof elem === "number" ) {
6404                 elem += "";
6405             }
6406 
6407             if ( !elem ) {
6408                 continue;
6409             }
6410 
6411             // Convert html string into DOM nodes
6412             // 把html字符串转换为dom节点
6413             if ( typeof elem === "string" ) {
6414                 if ( !rhtml.test( elem ) ) {
6415                     // 创建文本节点
6416                     /*
6417                      * 如果不是HTML标签或特殊符号，则创建文本节点；rhtml = /<|&#?\w+;/；
6418                      * <是HTML标签的起始符号，&#?\w+则是特殊符号的起始符号，例如：
6419                      * 特殊符号     命名实体    十进制编码
6420                      * 空格         &nbsp;      &#160;          
6421                      * <            &lt;        &#60;       
6422                      * >            &gt;        &#62;
6423                      * "            &quot;      &#34;           
6424                      * ×            &times                  
6425                      * ÷            &divide;    
6426                      * ±            &plusmn;    &#177;          
6427                      * &            &amp;
6428                      * © 带圈的C    &copy;      &#169;          
6429                      * ® 带圈的R    &reg;       &#174;
6430                      */
6431 
6432                     elem = context.createTextNode( elem );
6433                 } else {
6434                     // Ensure a safe container in which to render the html
6435                     // 确保将html渲染在一个安全的容器中
6436                     safe = safe || createSafeFragment( context );
6437                     div = context.createElement("div");
6438                     safe.appendChild( div );
6439 
6440                     // Fix "XHTML"-style tags in all browsers
6441                     // 在所有浏览器中处理XHTML格式的标签
6442                     // <div class="abc" style="abc" custome="abc"/>处理后结果为：
6443                     // <div class="abc" style="abc" custome="abc"></div> 
6444                     elem = elem.replace(rxhtmlTag, "<$1></$2>");
6445 
6446                     // Go to html and back, then peel off extra wrappers
6447                     // 匹配html标签，["", ""]是为了保证后面的[1]操作不抛异常
6448                     tag = ( rtagName.exec( elem ) || ["", ""] )[1].toLowerCase();
6449                     // 包裹标签，处理option td之类的需要被包裹的标签，同时需要移动层数
6450                     // wrapMap存放标签配置数据的对象，如果元素不需要包裹，则默认使用div进行包裹
6451                     wrap = wrapMap[ tag ] || wrapMap._default;
6452                     depth = wrap[0];
6453                     div.innerHTML = wrap[1] + elem + wrap[2];
6454 
6455                     // Move to the right depth
6456                     // 包裹标签后通过innerHTML的方式生成dom节点
6457                     // 再去除包裹，拿到要生成的dom元素的父节点
6458                     // td被包裹后通过innerHTML放置到div中，结构为div>table>tbody>tr>td
6459                     // td的depth为3，在div上去除三层包裹，得到tr>td
6460                     while ( depth-- ) {
6461                         div = div.lastChild;
6462                     }
6463 
6464                     // Remove IE's autoinserted <tbody> from table fragments
6465                     // 移除IE在table片段中自动插入的tbody标签
6466                     if ( !jQuery.support.tbody ) {
6467 
6468                         // String was a <table>, *may* have spurious <tbody>
6469                         // elem中含有tbody标签
6470                         hasBody = rtbody.test(elem);
6471 /*
6472 
6473 table                               tbody                       thead/ftoot
6474 从elem解析出来的tag是否table        elem中是否含有tbody         从elem解析出来的tag是否thead/ftoot      
6475 
6476  
6477 true/false                          true                        true/false                              只要elem中自带tbody，不需要删除，所以：[]
6478 
6479 true                                false                       false                                   变量div是DIV元素，firstChild是TABLE元素，IE会自
6480                                                                                                         动添加空tbody，所以：div.firstChild.childNodes
6481 
6482 false                               false                       true                                    变量div是TABLE元素，IE会自动添加空tbody，所以：
6483                                                                                                         div.childNodes
6484 
6485 false                               false                       false                                   如果elem是th/tr/td/col，jQuery自动插入tbody，
6486                                                                                                         变量div是TBODY元素，不需要删除；如果elem是其他标
6487                                                                                                         签，也不需要删除，所以：[]
6488 */
6489                             tbody = tag === "table" && !hasBody ?
6490                                 div.firstChild && div.firstChild.childNodes :
6491 
6492                                 // String was a bare <thead> or <tfoot>
6493                                 // 如果父标签是table（包裹标签），且elem中没有tbody，即elem中是thead/tfoot
6494                                 wrap[1] === "<table>" && !hasBody ?
6495                                     div.childNodes :
6496                                     [];
6497 
6498                         // 在for循环中遍历取到的tbody（可能含有thead/tfoot），删除IE自动添加的空tbody，非空tbody不会删除
6499                         for ( j = tbody.length - 1; j >= 0 ; --j ) {
6500                             if ( jQuery.nodeName( tbody[ j ], "tbody" ) && !tbody[ j ].childNodes.length ) {
6501                                 tbody[ j ].parentNode.removeChild( tbody[ j ] );
6502                             }
6503                         }
6504                     }
6505 
6506                     // IE completely kills leading whitespace when innerHTML is used
6507                     // IE在使用innerHTML时会删除前导空格
6508                     if ( !jQuery.support.leadingWhitespace && rleadingWhitespace.test( elem ) ) {
6509                         div.insertBefore( context.createTextNode( rleadingWhitespace.exec(elem)[0] ), div.firstChild );
6510                     }
6511                     // 返回真正需要创建的标签，如果标记需要包裹，变量div不再指向最初的div元素
6512                     elem = div.childNodes;
6513 
6514                     // Take out of fragment container (we need a fresh div each time)
6515                     // 移除用来生成节点的div
6516                     div.parentNode.removeChild( div );
6517                 }
6518             }
6519 
6520             // 将结果压入或者合并回返回值数组
6521             if ( elem.nodeType ) {
6522                 ret.push( elem );
6523             } else {
6524                 jQuery.merge( ret, elem );
6525             }
6526         }
6527 
6528         // Fix #11356: Clear elements from safeFragment
6529         // 清理用到的临时变量
6530         if ( div ) {
6531             elem = div = safe = null;
6532         }
6533 
6534         // Reset defaultChecked for any radios and checkboxes
6535         // about to be appended to the DOM in IE 6/7 (#8060)
6536         // 修正IE6/7中的radios、checkboxes的defaultChecked属性
6537         if ( !jQuery.support.appendChecked ) {
6538             for ( i = 0; (elem = ret[i]) != null; i++ ) {
6539                 if ( jQuery.nodeName( elem, "input" ) ) {
6540                     fixDefaultChecked( elem );
6541                 } else if ( typeof elem.getElementsByTagName !== "undefined" ) {
6542                     jQuery.grep( elem.getElementsByTagName("input"), fixDefaultChecked );
6543                 }
6544             }
6545         }
6546 
6547         // Append elements to a provided document fragment
6548         // 附加元素到提供的fragment上
6549         if ( fragment ) {
6550             // Special handling of each script element
6551             // 特殊处理每一个脚本元素
6552             handleScript = function( elem ) {
6553                 // Check if we consider it executable
6554                 // 检查脚本是否可执行
6555                 if ( !elem.type || rscriptType.test( elem.type ) ) {
6556                     // Detach the script and store it in the scripts array (if provided) or the fragment
6557                     // Return truthy to indicate that it has been handled
6558                     // 分离脚本，如果提供了scripts数组，则存储到scripts数组中，如果没有，则直接附加
6559                     return scripts ?
6560                         scripts.push( elem.parentNode ? elem.parentNode.removeChild( elem ) : elem ) :
6561                         fragment.appendChild( elem );
6562                 }
6563             };
6564 
6565             for ( i = 0; (elem = ret[i]) != null; i++ ) {
6566                 // Check if we're done after handling an executable script
6567                 // 检查是否处理了所有脚本元素
6568                 if ( !( jQuery.nodeName( elem, "script" ) && handleScript( elem ) ) ) {
6569                     // Append to fragment and handle embedded scripts
6570                     // 附加元素并且处理脚本
6571                     fragment.appendChild( elem );
6572                     if ( typeof elem.getElementsByTagName !== "undefined" ) {
6573                         // handleScript alters the DOM, so use jQuery.merge to ensure snapshot iteration
6574                         // handleScript会改变DOM，所以使用jQuery.merge实现对快照进行遍历
6575                         jsTags = jQuery.grep( jQuery.merge( [], elem.getElementsByTagName("script") ), handleScript );
6576 
6577                         // Splice the scripts into ret after their former ancestor and advance our index beyond them
6578                         // 将scripts插入到他们的正式的祖先后面并且增加index，跳过新增加的元素
6579                         // 通过apply(this,arguments)的形式传递参数，[i+1,0,jsTags ]为splice函数需要使用的参数
6580                         ret.splice.apply( ret, [i + 1, 0].concat( jsTags ) );
6581                         i += jsTags.length;
6582                     }
6583                 }
6584             }
6585         }
6586 
6587         return ret;
6588     },
6589 
6590     cleanData: function( elems, /* internal */ acceptData ) {
6591         var data, id, elem, type,
6592             i = 0,
6593             internalKey = jQuery.expando,
6594             cache = jQuery.cache,
6595             deleteExpando = jQuery.support.deleteExpando,
6596             special = jQuery.event.special;
6597 
6598         for ( ; (elem = elems[i]) != null; i++ ) {
6599 
6600             if ( acceptData || jQuery.acceptData( elem ) ) {
6601 
6602                 id = elem[ internalKey ];
6603                 data = id && cache[ id ];
6604 
6605                 if ( data ) {
6606                     if ( data.events ) {
6607                         for ( type in data.events ) {
6608                             if ( special[ type ] ) {
6609                                 jQuery.event.remove( elem, type );
6610 
6611                             // This is a shortcut to avoid jQuery.event.remove's overhead
6612                             } else {
6613                                 jQuery.removeEvent( elem, type, data.handle );
6614                             }
6615                         }
6616                     }
6617 
6618                     // Remove cache only if it was not already removed by jQuery.event.remove
6619                     if ( cache[ id ] ) {
6620 
6621                         delete cache[ id ];
6622 
6623                         // IE does not allow us to delete expando properties from nodes,
6624                         // nor does it have a removeAttribute function on Document nodes;
6625                         // we must handle all of these cases
6626                         if ( deleteExpando ) {
6627                             delete elem[ internalKey ];
6628 
6629                         } else if ( elem.removeAttribute ) {
6630                             elem.removeAttribute( internalKey );
6631 
6632                         } else {
6633                             elem[ internalKey ] = null;
6634                         }
6635 
6636                         jQuery.deletedIds.push( id );
6637                     }
6638                 }
6639             }
6640         }
6641     }

6659         [];

6730 // return a css property mapped to a potentially vendor prefixed property
6731 function vendorPropName( style, name ) {
6732 
6733     // shortcut for names that are not vendor prefixed
6734     if ( name in style ) {
6735         return name;
6736     }
6737 
6738     // check for vendor prefixed names
6739     var capName = name.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + name.slice(1),
6740         origName = name,
6741         i = cssPrefixes.length;
6742 
6743     while ( i-- ) {
6744         name = cssPrefixes[ i ] + capName;
6745         if ( name in style ) {
6746             return name;
6747         }
6748     }
6749 
6750     return origName;
6751 }

6753 function isHidden( elem, el ) {
6754     elem = el || elem;
6755     return jQuery.css( elem, "display" ) === "none" || !jQuery.contains( elem.ownerDocument, elem );
6756 }

6758 function showHide( elements, show ) {
6759     var elem, display,
6760         values = [],
6761         index = 0,
6762         length = elements.length;
6763 
6764     for ( ; index < length; index++ ) {
6765         elem = elements[ index ];
6766         if ( !elem.style ) {
6767             continue;
6768         }
6769         values[ index ] = jQuery._data( elem, "olddisplay" );
6770         if ( show ) {
6771             // Reset the inline display of this element to learn if it is
6772             // being hidden by cascaded rules or not
6773             if ( !values[ index ] && elem.style.display === "none" ) {
6774                 elem.style.display = "";
6775             }
6776 
6777             // Set elements which have been overridden with display: none
6778             // in a stylesheet to whatever the default browser style is
6779             // for such an element
6780             if ( elem.style.display === "" && isHidden( elem ) ) {
6781                 values[ index ] = jQuery._data( elem, "olddisplay", css_defaultDisplay(elem.nodeName) );
6782             }
6783         } else {
6784             display = curCSS( elem, "display" );
6785 
6786             if ( !values[ index ] && display !== "none" ) {
6787                 jQuery._data( elem, "olddisplay", display );
6788             }
6789         }
6790     }
6791 
6792     // Set the display of most of the elements in a second loop
6793     // to avoid the constant reflow
6794     for ( index = 0; index < length; index++ ) {
6795         elem = elements[ index ];
6796         if ( !elem.style ) {
6797             continue;
6798         }
6799         if ( !show || elem.style.display === "none" || elem.style.display === "" ) {
6800             elem.style.display = show ? values[ index ] || "" : "none";
6801         }
6802     }
6803 
6804     return elements;
6805 }

6810             return value !== undefined ?
6811                 jQuery.style( elem, name, value ) :
6812                 jQuery.css( elem, name );
6813         }, name, value, arguments.length > 1 );
