6815     show: function() {
6816         return showHide( this, true );
6817     },
6818     hide: function() {
6819         return showHide( this );
6820     },
6821     toggle: function( state, fn2 ) {
6822         var bool = typeof state === "boolean";
6823 
6824         if ( jQuery.isFunction( state ) && jQuery.isFunction( fn2 ) ) {
6825             return eventsToggle.apply( this, arguments );
6826         }
6827 
6828         return this.each(function() {
6829             if ( bool ? state : isHidden( this ) ) {
6830                 jQuery( this ).show();
6831             } else {
6832                 jQuery( this ).hide();
6833             }
6834         });
6835     }

6838 jQuery.extend({
6839     // Add in style property hooks for overriding the default
6840     // behavior of getting and setting a style property
6841     cssHooks: {
6842         opacity: {
6843             get: function( elem, computed ) {
6844                 if ( computed ) {
6845                     // We should always get a number back from opacity
6846                     var ret = curCSS( elem, "opacity" );
6847                     return ret === "" ? "1" : ret;
6848 
6849                 }
6850             }
6851         }
6852     },
6853 
6854     // Exclude the following css properties to add px
6855     cssNumber: {
6856         "fillOpacity": true,
6857         "fontWeight": true,
6858         "lineHeight": true,
6859         "opacity": true,
6860         "orphans": true,
6861         "widows": true,
6862         "zIndex": true,
6863         "zoom": true
6864     },
6865 
6866     // Add in properties whose names you wish to fix before
6867     // setting or getting the value
6868     cssProps: {
6869         // normalize float css property
6870         "float": jQuery.support.cssFloat ? "cssFloat" : "styleFloat"
6871     },
6872 
6873     // Get and set the style property on a DOM Node
6874     style: function( elem, name, value, extra ) {
6875         // Don't set styles on text and comment nodes
6876         if ( !elem || elem.nodeType === 3 || elem.nodeType === 8 || !elem.style ) {
6877             return;
6878         }
6879 
6880         // Make sure that we're working with the right name
6881         var ret, type, hooks,
6882             origName = jQuery.camelCase( name ),
6883             style = elem.style;
6884 
6885         name = jQuery.cssProps[ origName ] || ( jQuery.cssProps[ origName ] = vendorPropName( style, origName ) );
6886 
6887         // gets hook for the prefixed version
6888         // followed by the unprefixed version
6889         hooks = jQuery.cssHooks[ name ] || jQuery.cssHooks[ origName ];
6890 
6891         // Check if we're setting a value
6892         if ( value !== undefined ) {
6893             type = typeof value;
6894 
6895             // convert relative number strings (+= or -=) to relative numbers. #7345
6896             if ( type === "string" && (ret = rrelNum.exec( value )) ) {
6897                 value = ( ret[1] + 1 ) * ret[2] + parseFloat( jQuery.css( elem, name ) );
6898                 // Fixes bug #9237
6899                 type = "number";
6900             }
6901 
6902             // Make sure that NaN and null values aren't set. See: #7116
6903             if ( value == null || type === "number" && isNaN( value ) ) {
6904                 return;
6905             }
6906 
6907             // If a number was passed in, add 'px' to the (except for certain CSS properties)
6908             if ( type === "number" && !jQuery.cssNumber[ origName ] ) {
6909                 value += "px";
6910             }
6911 
6912             // If a hook was provided, use that value, otherwise just set the specified value
6913             if ( !hooks || !("set" in hooks) || (value = hooks.set( elem, value, extra )) !== undefined ) {
6914                 // Wrapped to prevent IE from throwing errors when 'invalid' values are provided
6915                 // Fixes bug #5509
6916                 try {
6917                     style[ name ] = value;
6918                 } catch(e) {}
6919             }
6920 
6921         } else {
6922             // If a hook was provided get the non-computed value from there
6923             if ( hooks && "get" in hooks && (ret = hooks.get( elem, false, extra )) !== undefined ) {
6924                 return ret;
6925             }
6926 
6927             // Otherwise just get the value from the style object
6928             return style[ name ];
6929         }
6930     },
6931 
6932     css: function( elem, name, numeric, extra ) {
6933         var val, num, hooks,
6934             origName = jQuery.camelCase( name );
6935 
6936         // Make sure that we're working with the right name
6937         name = jQuery.cssProps[ origName ] || ( jQuery.cssProps[ origName ] = vendorPropName( elem.style, origName ) );
6938 
6939         // gets hook for the prefixed version
6940         // followed by the unprefixed version
6941         hooks = jQuery.cssHooks[ name ] || jQuery.cssHooks[ origName ];
6942 
6943         // If a hook was provided get the computed value from there
6944         if ( hooks && "get" in hooks ) {
6945             val = hooks.get( elem, true, extra );
6946         }
6947 
6948         // Otherwise, if a way to get the computed value exists, use that
6949         if ( val === undefined ) {
6950             val = curCSS( elem, name );
6951         }
6952 
6953         //convert "normal" to computed value
6954         if ( val === "normal" && name in cssNormalTransform ) {
6955             val = cssNormalTransform[ name ];
6956         }
6957 
6958         // Return, converting to number if forced or a qualifier was provided and val looks numeric
6959         if ( numeric || extra !== undefined ) {
6960             num = parseFloat( val );
6961             return numeric || jQuery.isNumeric( num ) ? num || 0 : val;
6962         }
6963         return val;
6964     },
6965 
6966     // A method for quickly swapping in/out CSS properties to get correct calculations
6967     swap: function( elem, options, callback ) {
6968         var ret, name,
6969             old = {};
6970 
6971         // Remember the old values, and insert the new ones
6972         for ( name in options ) {
6973             old[ name ] = elem.style[ name ];
6974             elem.style[ name ] = options[ name ];
6975         }
6976 
6977         ret = callback.call( elem );
6978 
6979         // Revert the old values
6980         for ( name in options ) {
6981             elem.style[ name ] = old[ name ];
6982         }
6983 
6984         return ret;
6985     }

6988 // NOTE: To any future maintainer, we've window.getComputedStyle
6989 // because jsdom on node.js will break without it.
6990 if ( window.getComputedStyle ) {
6991     curCSS = function( elem, name ) {
6992         var ret, width, minWidth, maxWidth,
6993             computed = window.getComputedStyle( elem, null ),
6994             style = elem.style;
6995 
6996         if ( computed ) {
6997 
6998             ret = computed[ name ];
6999             if ( ret === "" && !jQuery.contains( elem.ownerDocument, elem ) ) {
7000                 ret = jQuery.style( elem, name );
7001             }
7002 
7003             // A tribute to the "awesome hack by Dean Edwards"
7004             // Chrome < 17 and Safari 5.0 uses "computed value" instead of "used value" for margin-right
7005             // Safari 5.1.7 (at least) returns percentage for a larger set of values, but width seems to be reliably pixels
7006             // this is against the CSSOM draft spec: http://dev.w3.org/csswg/cssom/#resolved-values
7007             if ( rnumnonpx.test( ret ) && rmargin.test( name ) ) {
7008                 width = style.width;
7009                 minWidth = style.minWidth;
7010                 maxWidth = style.maxWidth;
7011 
7012                 style.minWidth = style.maxWidth = style.width = ret;
7013                 ret = computed.width;
7014 
7015                 style.width = width;
7016                 style.minWidth = minWidth;
7017                 style.maxWidth = maxWidth;
7018             }
7019         }
7020 
7021         return ret;
7022     };
7023 } else if ( document.documentElement.currentStyle ) {
7024     curCSS = function( elem, name ) {
7025         var left, rsLeft,
7026             ret = elem.currentStyle && elem.currentStyle[ name ],
7027             style = elem.style;
7028 
7029         // Avoid setting ret to empty string here
7030         // so we don't default to auto
7031         if ( ret == null && style && style[ name ] ) {
7032             ret = style[ name ];
7033         }
7034 
7035         // From the awesome hack by Dean Edwards
7036         // http://erik.eae.net/archives/2007/07/27/18.54.15/#comment-102291
7037 
7038         // If we're not dealing with a regular pixel number
7039         // but a number that has a weird ending, we need to convert it to pixels
7040         // but not position css attributes, as those are proportional to the parent element instead
7041         // and we can't measure the parent instead because it might trigger a "stacking dolls" problem
7042         if ( rnumnonpx.test( ret ) && !rposition.test( name ) ) {
7043 
7044             // Remember the original values
7045             left = style.left;
7046             rsLeft = elem.runtimeStyle && elem.runtimeStyle.left;
7047 
7048             // Put in the new values to get a computed value out
7049             if ( rsLeft ) {
7050                 elem.runtimeStyle.left = elem.currentStyle.left;
7051             }
7052             style.left = name === "fontSize" ? "1em" : ret;
7053             ret = style.pixelLeft + "px";
7054 
7055             // Revert the changed values
7056             style.left = left;
7057             if ( rsLeft ) {
7058                 elem.runtimeStyle.left = rsLeft;
7059             }
7060         }
7061 
7062         return ret === "" ? "auto" : ret;
7063     };
7064 }

7066 function setPositiveNumber( elem, value, subtract ) {
7067     var matches = rnumsplit.exec( value );
7068     return matches ?
7069             Math.max( 0, matches[ 1 ] - ( subtract || 0 ) ) + ( matches[ 2 ] || "px" ) :
7070             value;
7071 }
7072 
7073 function augmentWidthOrHeight( elem, name, extra, isBorderBox ) {
7074     var i = extra === ( isBorderBox ? "border" : "content" ) ?
7075         // If we already have the right measurement, avoid augmentation
7076         4 :
7077         // Otherwise initialize for horizontal or vertical properties
7078         name === "width" ? 1 : 0,
7079 
7080         val = 0;
7081 
7082     for ( ; i < 4; i += 2 ) {
7083         // both box models exclude margin, so add it if we want it
7084         if ( extra === "margin" ) {
7085             // we use jQuery.css instead of curCSS here
7086             // because of the reliableMarginRight CSS hook!
7087             val += jQuery.css( elem, extra + cssExpand[ i ], true );
7088         }
7089 
7090         // From this point on we use curCSS for maximum performance (relevant in animations)
7091         if ( isBorderBox ) {
7092             // border-box includes padding, so remove it if we want content
7093             if ( extra === "content" ) {
7094                 val -= parseFloat( curCSS( elem, "padding" + cssExpand[ i ] ) ) || 0;
7095             }
7096 
7097             // at this point, extra isn't border nor margin, so remove border
7098             if ( extra !== "margin" ) {
7099                 val -= parseFloat( curCSS( elem, "border" + cssExpand[ i ] + "Width" ) ) || 0;
7100             }
7101         } else {
7102             // at this point, extra isn't content, so add padding
7103             val += parseFloat( curCSS( elem, "padding" + cssExpand[ i ] ) ) || 0;
7104 
7105             // at this point, extra isn't content nor padding, so add border
7106             if ( extra !== "padding" ) {
7107                 val += parseFloat( curCSS( elem, "border" + cssExpand[ i ] + "Width" ) ) || 0;
7108             }
7109         }
7110     }
7111 
7112     return val;
7113 }
7114 
7115 function getWidthOrHeight( elem, name, extra ) {
7116 
7117     // Start with offset property, which is equivalent to the border-box value
7118     var val = name === "width" ? elem.offsetWidth : elem.offsetHeight,
7119         valueIsBorderBox = true,
7120         isBorderBox = jQuery.support.boxSizing && jQuery.css( elem, "boxSizing" ) === "border-box";
7121 
7122     // some non-html elements return undefined for offsetWidth, so check for null/undefined
7123     // svg - https://bugzilla.mozilla.org/show_bug.cgi?id=649285
7124     // MathML - https://bugzilla.mozilla.org/show_bug.cgi?id=491668
7125     if ( val <= 0 || val == null ) {
7126         // Fall back to computed then uncomputed css if necessary
7127         val = curCSS( elem, name );
7128         if ( val < 0 || val == null ) {
7129             val = elem.style[ name ];
7130         }
7131 
7132         // Computed unit is not pixels. Stop here and return.
7133         if ( rnumnonpx.test(val) ) {
7134             return val;
7135         }
7136 
7137         // we need the check for style in case a browser which returns unreliable values
7138         // for getComputedStyle silently falls back to the reliable elem.style
7139         valueIsBorderBox = isBorderBox && ( jQuery.support.boxSizingReliable || val === elem.style[ name ] );
7140 
7141         // Normalize "", auto, and prepare for extra
7142         val = parseFloat( val ) || 0;
7143     }
7144 
7145     // use the active box-sizing model to add/subtract irrelevant styles
7146     return ( val +
7147         augmentWidthOrHeight(
7148             elem,
7149             name,
7150             extra || ( isBorderBox ? "border" : "content" ),
7151             valueIsBorderBox
7152         )
7153     ) + "px";
7154 }

7157 // Try to determine the default display value of an element
7158 function css_defaultDisplay( nodeName ) {
7159     if ( elemdisplay[ nodeName ] ) {
7160         return elemdisplay[ nodeName ];
7161     }
7162 
7163     var elem = jQuery( "<" + nodeName + ">" ).appendTo( document.body ),
7164         display = elem.css("display");
7165     elem.remove();
7166 
7167     // If the simple way fails,
7168     // get element's real default display by attaching it to a temp iframe
7169     if ( display === "none" || display === "" ) {
7170         // Use the already-created iframe if possible
7171         iframe = document.body.appendChild(
7172             iframe || jQuery.extend( document.createElement("iframe"), {
7173                 frameBorder: 0,
7174                 width: 0,
7175                 height: 0
7176             })
7177         );
7178 
7179         // Create a cacheable copy of the iframe document on first call.
7180         // IE and Opera will allow us to reuse the iframeDoc without re-writing the fake HTML
7181         // document to it; WebKit & Firefox won't allow reusing the iframe document.
7182         if ( !iframeDoc || !iframe.createElement ) {
7183             iframeDoc = ( iframe.contentWindow || iframe.contentDocument ).document;
7184             iframeDoc.write("<!doctype html><html><body>");
7185             iframeDoc.close();
7186         }
7187 
7188         elem = iframeDoc.body.appendChild( iframeDoc.createElement(nodeName) );
7189 
7190         display = curCSS( elem, "display" );
7191         document.body.removeChild( iframe );
7192     }
7193 
7194     // Store the correct default display
7195     elemdisplay[ nodeName ] = display;
7196 
7197     return display;
7198 }

7205                 // however, it must have a current display style that would benefit from this

7207                     return jQuery.swap( elem, cssShow, function() {
7208                         return getWidthOrHeight( elem, name, extra );
7209                     });
7210                 } else {
7211                     return getWidthOrHeight( elem, name, extra );
7212                 }
7213             }
7214         },
7215

7220                     name,

7229 if ( !jQuery.support.opacity ) {
7230     jQuery.cssHooks.opacity = {
7231         get: function( elem, computed ) {
7232             // IE uses filters for opacity
7233             return ropacity.test( (computed && elem.currentStyle ? elem.currentStyle.filter : elem.style.filter) || "" ) ?
7234                 ( 0.01 * parseFloat( RegExp.$1 ) ) + "" :
7235                 computed ? "1" : "";
7236         },
7237 
7238         set: function( elem, value ) {
7239             var style = elem.style,
7240                 currentStyle = elem.currentStyle,
7241                 opacity = jQuery.isNumeric( value ) ? "alpha(opacity=" + value * 100 + ")" : "",
7242                 filter = currentStyle && currentStyle.filter || style.filter || "";
7243 
7244             // IE has trouble with opacity if it does not have layout
7245             // Force it by setting the zoom level
7246             style.zoom = 1;
7247 
7248             // if setting opacity to 1, and no other filters exist - attempt to remove filter attribute #6652
7249             if ( value >= 1 && jQuery.trim( filter.replace( ralpha, "" ) ) === "" &&
7250                 style.removeAttribute ) {
7251 
7252                 // Setting style.filter to null, "" & " " still leave "filter:" in the cssText
7253                 // if "filter:" is present at all, clearType is disabled, we want to avoid this
7254                 // style.removeAttribute is IE Only, but so apparently is this code path...
7255                 style.removeAttribute( "filter" );
7256 
7257                 // if there there is no filter style applied in a css rule, we are done
7258                 if ( currentStyle && !currentStyle.filter ) {
7259                     return;
7260                 }
7261             }
7262 
7263             // otherwise, set new filter values
7264             style.filter = ralpha.test( filter ) ?
7265                 filter.replace( ralpha, opacity ) :
7266                 filter + " " + opacity;
7267         }
7268     };
7269 }

7344 var r20 = /%20/g,
7345     rbracket = /\[\]$/,
7346     rCRLF = /\r?\n/g,
7347     rinput = /^(?:color|date|datetime|datetime-local|email|hidden|month|number|password|range|search|tel|text|time|url|week)$/i,

7362         })

7369                     jQuery.map( val, function( val, i ){
7370                         return { name: elem.name, value: val.replace( rCRLF, "\r\n" ) };
7371                     }) :
7372                     { name: elem.name, value: val.replace( rCRLF, "\r\n" ) };

7377 //Serialize an array of form elements or a set of
7378 //key/values into a query string
7379 jQuery.param = function( a, traditional ) {
7380     var prefix,
7381         s = [],
7382         add = function( key, value ) {
7383             // If value is a function, invoke it and return its value
7384             value = jQuery.isFunction( value ) ? value() : ( value == null ? "" : value );
7385             s[ s.length ] = encodeURIComponent( key ) + "=" + encodeURIComponent( value );
7386         };
7387 
7388     // Set traditional to true for jQuery <= 1.3.2 behavior.
7389     if ( traditional === undefined ) {
7390         traditional = jQuery.ajaxSettings && jQuery.ajaxSettings.traditional;
7391     }
7392 
7393     // If an array was passed in, assume that it is an array of form elements.
7394     if ( jQuery.isArray( a ) || ( a.jquery && !jQuery.isPlainObject( a ) ) ) {
7395         // Serialize the form elements
7396         jQuery.each( a, function() {
7397             add( this.name, this.value );
7398         });
7399 
7400     } else {
7401         // If traditional, encode the "old" way (the way 1.3.2 or older
7402         // did it), otherwise encode params recursively.
7403         for ( prefix in a ) {
7404             buildParams( prefix, a[ prefix ], traditional, add );
7405         }
7406     }
7407 
7408     // Return the resulting serialization
7409     return s.join( "&" ).replace( r20, "+" );
7410 };
7411 
7412 function buildParams( prefix, obj, traditional, add ) {
7413     var name;
7414 
7415     if ( jQuery.isArray( obj ) ) {
7416         // Serialize array item.
7417         jQuery.each( obj, function( i, v ) {
7418             if ( traditional || rbracket.test( prefix ) ) {
7419                 // Treat each array item as a scalar.
7420                 add( prefix, v );
7421 
7422             } else {
7423                 // If array item is non-scalar (array or object), encode its
7424                 // numeric index to resolve deserialization ambiguity issues.
7425                 // Note that rack (as of 1.0.0) can't currently deserialize
7426                 // nested arrays properly, and attempting to do so may cause
7427                 // a server error. Possible fixes are to modify rack's
7428                 // deserialization algorithm or to provide an option or flag
7429                 // to force array serialization to be shallow.
7430                 buildParams( prefix + "[" + ( typeof v === "object" ? i : "" ) + "]", v, traditional, add );
7431             }
7432         });
7433 
7434     } else if ( !traditional && jQuery.type( obj ) === "object" ) {
7435         // Serialize object item.
7436         for ( name in obj ) {
7437             buildParams( prefix + "[" + name + "]", obj[ name ], traditional, add );
7438         }
7439 
7440     } else {
7441         // Serialize scalar item.
7442         add( prefix, obj );
7443     }
7444 }
7445 var // Document location
7446     ajaxLocation,
7447     // Document location segments

7451     rheaders = /^(.*?):[ \t]*([^\r\n]*)\r?$/mg, // IE leaves an \r character at EOL
7452     // #7653, #8125, #8152: local protocol detection
7453     rlocalProtocol = /^(?:about|app|app\-storage|.+\-extension|file|res|widget):$/,
7454     rnoContent = /^(?:GET|HEAD)$/,
7455     rprotocol = /^\/\//,
7456     rquery = /\?/,
7457     rscript = /<script\b[^<]*(?:(?!<\/script>)<[^<]*)*<\/script>/gi,
7458     rts = /([?&])_=[^&]*/,
7459     rurl = /^([\w\+\.\-]+:)(?:\/\/([^\/?#:]*)(?::(\d+)|)|)/,

7462     _load = jQuery.fn.load,

7464     /* Prefilters
7465      * 1) They are useful to introduce custom dataTypes (see ajax/jsonp.js for an example)
7466      * 2) These are called:
7467      *    - BEFORE asking for a transport
7468      *    - AFTER param serialization (s.data is a string if s.processData is true)
7469      * 3) key is the dataType
7470      * 4) the catchall symbol "*" can be used
7471      * 5) execution will start with transport dataType and THEN continue down to "*" if needed
7472      */
7473     prefilters = {},
7474 
7475     /* Transports bindings
7476      * 1) key is the dataType
7477      * 2) the catchall symbol "*" can be used
7478      * 3) selection will start with transport dataType and THEN go to "*" if needed
7479      */
7480     transports = {},
7481 
7482     // Avoid comment-prolog char sequence (#10098); must appease lint and evade compression
7483     allTypes = ["*/"] + ["*"];

7485 // #8138, IE may throw an exception when accessing
7486 // a field from window.location if document.domain has been set
7487 try {
7488     ajaxLocation = location.href;
7489 } catch( e ) {
7490     // Use the href attribute of an A element
7491     // since IE will modify it given document.location
7492     ajaxLocation = document.createElement( "a" );
7493     ajaxLocation.href = "";
7494     ajaxLocation = ajaxLocation.href;
7495 }

7498 ajaxLocParts = rurl.exec( ajaxLocation.toLowerCase() ) || [];

7500 // Base "constructor" for jQuery.ajaxPrefilter and jQuery.ajaxTransport
7501 function addToPrefiltersOrTransports( structure ) {
7502 
7503     // dataTypeExpression is optional and defaults to "*"
7504     return function( dataTypeExpression, func ) {
7505 
7506         if ( typeof dataTypeExpression !== "string" ) {
7507             func = dataTypeExpression;
7508             dataTypeExpression = "*";
7509         }
7510 
7511         var dataType, list, placeBefore,
7512             dataTypes = dataTypeExpression.toLowerCase().split( core_rspace ),
7513             i = 0,
7514             length = dataTypes.length;
7515 
7516         if ( jQuery.isFunction( func ) ) {
7517             // For each dataType in the dataTypeExpression
7518             for ( ; i < length; i++ ) {
7519                 dataType = dataTypes[ i ];
7520                 // We control if we're asked to add before
7521                 // any existing element
7522                 placeBefore = /^\+/.test( dataType );
7523                 if ( placeBefore ) {
7524                     dataType = dataType.substr( 1 ) || "*";
7525                 }
7526                 list = structure[ dataType ] = structure[ dataType ] || [];
7527                 // then we add to the structure accordingly
7528                 list[ placeBefore ? "unshift" : "push" ]( func );
7529             }
7530         }
7531     };
7532 }
7533 
7534 // Base inspection function for prefilters and transports
7535 function inspectPrefiltersOrTransports( structure, options, originalOptions, jqXHR,
7536         dataType /* internal */, inspected /* internal */ ) {
7537 
7538     dataType = dataType || options.dataTypes[ 0 ];
7539     inspected = inspected || {};
7540 
7541     inspected[ dataType ] = true;
7542 
7543     var selection,
7544         list = structure[ dataType ],
7545         i = 0,
7546         length = list ? list.length : 0,
7547         executeOnly = ( structure === prefilters );
7548 
7549     for ( ; i < length && ( executeOnly || !selection ); i++ ) {
7550         selection = list[ i ]( options, originalOptions, jqXHR );
7551         // If we got redirected to another dataType
7552         // we try there if executing only and not done already
7553         if ( typeof selection === "string" ) {
7554             if ( !executeOnly || inspected[ selection ] ) {
7555                 selection = undefined;
7556             } else {
7557                 options.dataTypes.unshift( selection );
7558                 selection = inspectPrefiltersOrTransports(
7559                         structure, options, originalOptions, jqXHR, selection, inspected );
7560             }
7561         }
7562     }
7563     // If we're only executing or nothing was selected
7564     // we try the catchall dataType if not done already
7565     if ( ( executeOnly || !selection ) && !inspected[ "*" ] ) {
7566         selection = inspectPrefiltersOrTransports(
7567                 structure, options, originalOptions, jqXHR, "*", inspected );
7568     }
7569     // unnecessary when only executing (prefilters)
7570     // but it'll be ignored by the caller in that case
7571     return selection;
7572 }

7574 // A special extend for ajax options
7575 // that takes "flat" options (not to be deep extended)
7576 // Fixes #9887
7577 function ajaxExtend( target, src ) {
7578     var key, deep,
7579         flatOptions = jQuery.ajaxSettings.flatOptions || {};
7580     for ( key in src ) {
7581         if ( src[ key ] !== undefined ) {
7582             ( flatOptions[ key ] ? target : ( deep || ( deep = {} ) ) )[ key ] = src[ key ];
7583         }
7584     }
7585     if ( deep ) {
7586         jQuery.extend( true, target, deep );
7587     }
7588 }

7590 jQuery.fn.load = function( url, params, callback ) {
7591     if ( typeof url !== "string" && _load ) {
7592         return _load.apply( this, arguments );
7593     }
7594 
7595     // Don't do a request if no elements are being requested
7596     if ( !this.length ) {
7597         return this;
7598     }
7599 
7600     var selector, type, response,
7601         self = this,
7602         off = url.indexOf(" ");
7603 
7604     if ( off >= 0 ) {
7605         selector = url.slice( off, url.length );
7606         url = url.slice( 0, off );
7607     }
7608 
7609     // If it's a function
7610     if ( jQuery.isFunction( params ) ) {
7611 
7612         // We assume that it's the callback
7613         callback = params;
7614         params = undefined;
7615 
7616     // Otherwise, build a param string
7617     } else if ( params && typeof params === "object" ) {
7618         type = "POST";
7619     }
7620 
7621     // Request the remote document
7622     jQuery.ajax({
7623         url: url,
7624 
7625         // if "type" variable is undefined, then "GET" method will be used
7626         type: type,
7627         dataType: "html",
7628         data: params,
7629         complete: function( jqXHR, status ) {
7630             if ( callback ) {
7631                 self.each( callback, response || [ jqXHR.responseText, status, jqXHR ] );
7632             }
7633         }
7634     }).done(function( responseText ) {
7635 
7636         // Save response for use in complete callback
7637         response = arguments;
7638 
7639         // See if a selector was specified
7640         self.html( selector ?
7641 
7642             // Create a dummy div to hold the results
7643             jQuery("<div>")
7644 
7645                 // inject the contents of the document in, removing the scripts
7646                 // to avoid any 'Permission Denied' errors in IE
7647                 .append( responseText.replace( rscript, "" ) )
7648 
7649                 // Locate the specified elements
7650                 .find( selector ) :
7651 
7652             // If not, just inject the full result
7653             responseText );
7654 
7655     });
7656 
7657     return this;
7658 };

7662     jQuery.fn[ o ] = function( f ){
7663         return this.on( o, f );
7664     };

7696     // Creates a full fledged settings object into target
7697     // with both ajaxSettings and settings fields.

7699     ajaxSetup: function( target, settings ) {
7700         if ( settings ) {
7701             // Building a settings object
7702             ajaxExtend( target, jQuery.ajaxSettings );
7703         } else {
7704             // Extending ajaxSettings
7705             settings = target;
7706             target = jQuery.ajaxSettings;

7715         global: true,

7731

7749         },
7750 
7751         // List of data converters
7752         // 1) key format is "source_type destination_type" (a single space in-between)
7753         // 2) the catchall symbol "*" can be used for source_type
7754         converters: {
7755 
7756             // Convert anything to text
7757             "* text": window.String,
7758 
7759             // Text to html (true = no transformation)
7760             "text html": true,
7761 
7762             // Evaluate text as a json expression
7763             "text json": jQuery.parseJSON,
7764

7766             "text xml": jQuery.parseXML
7767         },

7770         // you can add your own custom options here if
7771         // and when you create one that shouldn't be
7772         // deep extended (see ajaxExtend)

7774             context: true,
7775             url: true
7776         }

7779     ajaxPrefilter: addToPrefiltersOrTransports( prefilters ),
7780     ajaxTransport: addToPrefiltersOrTransports( transports ),
7781 
7782     // Main method
7783     ajax: function( url, options ) {
7784 
7785         // If url is an object, simulate pre-1.5 signature
7786         if ( typeof url === "object" ) {
7787             options = url;
7788             url = undefined;
7789         }
7790 
7791         // Force options to be an object
7792         options = options || {};
7793 
7794         var // ifModified key
7795             ifModifiedKey,
7796             // Response headers
7797             responseHeadersString,
7798             responseHeaders,
7799             // transport
7800             transport,
7801             // timeout handle
7802             timeoutTimer,
7803             // Cross-domain detection vars
7804             parts,
7805             // To know if global events are to be dispatched
7806             fireGlobals,
7807             // Loop variable
7808             i,
7809             // Create the final options object
7810             s = jQuery.ajaxSetup( {}, options ),
7811             // Callbacks context
7812             callbackContext = s.context || s,
7813             // Context for global events
7814             // It's the callbackContext if one was provided in the options
7815             // and if it's a DOM node or a jQuery collection
7816             globalEventContext = callbackContext !== s &&
7817                 ( callbackContext.nodeType || callbackContext instanceof jQuery ) ?
7818                         jQuery( callbackContext ) : jQuery.event,
7819             // Deferreds
7820             deferred = jQuery.Deferred(),
7821             completeDeferred = jQuery.Callbacks( "once memory" ),
7822             // Status-dependent callbacks
7823             statusCode = s.statusCode || {},
7824             // Headers (they are sent all at once)
7825             requestHeaders = {},
7826             requestHeadersNames = {},
7827             // The jqXHR state
7828             state = 0,
7829             // Default abort message
7830             strAbort = "canceled",
7831             // Fake xhr
7832             jqXHR = {
7833 
7834                 readyState: 0,
7835 
7836                 // Caches the header
7837                 setRequestHeader: function( name, value ) {
7838                     if ( !state ) {
7839                         var lname = name.toLowerCase();
7840                         name = requestHeadersNames[ lname ] = requestHeadersNames[ lname ] || name;
7841                         requestHeaders[ name ] = value;
7842                     }
7843                     return this;
7844                 },
7845 
7846                 // Raw string
7847                 getAllResponseHeaders: function() {
7848                     return state === 2 ? responseHeadersString : null;
7849                 },
7850 
7851                 // Builds headers hashtable if needed
7852                 getResponseHeader: function( key ) {
7853                     var match;
7854                     if ( state === 2 ) {
7855                         if ( !responseHeaders ) {
7856                             responseHeaders = {};
7857                             while( ( match = rheaders.exec( responseHeadersString ) ) ) {
7858                                 responseHeaders[ match[1].toLowerCase() ] = match[ 2 ];
7859                             }
7860                         }
7861                         match = responseHeaders[ key.toLowerCase() ];
7862                     }
7863                     return match === undefined ? null : match;
7864                 },
7865 
7866                 // Overrides response content-type header
7867                 overrideMimeType: function( type ) {
7868                     if ( !state ) {
7869                         s.mimeType = type;
7870                     }
7871                     return this;
7872                 },
7873 
7874                 // Cancel the request
7875                 abort: function( statusText ) {
7876                     statusText = statusText || strAbort;
7877                     if ( transport ) {
7878                         transport.abort( statusText );
7879                     }
7880                     done( 0, statusText );
7881                     return this;
7882                 }
7883             };
7884 
7885         // Callback for when everything is done
7886         // It is defined here because jslint complains if it is declared
7887         // at the end of the function (which would be more logical and readable)
7888         function done( status, nativeStatusText, responses, headers ) {
7889             var isSuccess, success, error, response, modified,
7890                 statusText = nativeStatusText;
7891 
7892             // Called once
7893             if ( state === 2 ) {
7894                 return;
7895             }
7896 
7897             // State is "done" now
7898             state = 2;
7899 
7900             // Clear timeout if it exists
7901             if ( timeoutTimer ) {
7902                 clearTimeout( timeoutTimer );
7903             }
7904 
7905             // Dereference transport for early garbage collection
7906             // (no matter how long the jqXHR object will be used)
7907             transport = undefined;
7908 
7909             // Cache response headers
7910             responseHeadersString = headers || "";
7911 
7912             // Set readyState
7913             jqXHR.readyState = status > 0 ? 4 : 0;
7914 
7915             // Get response data
7916             if ( responses ) {
7917                 response = ajaxHandleResponses( s, jqXHR, responses );
7918             }
7919 
7920             // If successful, handle type chaining
7921             if ( status >= 200 && status < 300 || status === 304 ) {
7922 
7923                 // Set the If-Modified-Since and/or If-None-Match header, if in ifModified mode.
7924                 if ( s.ifModified ) {
7925 
7926                     modified = jqXHR.getResponseHeader("Last-Modified");
7927                     if ( modified ) {
7928                         jQuery.lastModified[ ifModifiedKey ] = modified;
7929                     }
7930                     modified = jqXHR.getResponseHeader("Etag");
7931                     if ( modified ) {
7932                         jQuery.etag[ ifModifiedKey ] = modified;
7933                     }
7934                 }
7935 
7936                 // If not modified
7937                 if ( status === 304 ) {
7938 
7939                     statusText = "notmodified";
7940                     isSuccess = true;
7941 
7942                 // If we have data
7943                 } else {
7944 
7945                     isSuccess = ajaxConvert( s, response );
7946                     statusText = isSuccess.state;
7947                     success = isSuccess.data;
7948                     error = isSuccess.error;
7949                     isSuccess = !error;
7950                 }
7951             } else {
7952                 // We extract error from statusText
7953                 // then normalize statusText and status for non-aborts
7954                 error = statusText;
7955                 if ( !statusText || status ) {
7956                     statusText = "error";
7957                     if ( status < 0 ) {
7958                         status = 0;
7959                     }
7960                 }
7961             }
7962 
7963             // Set data for the fake xhr object
7964             jqXHR.status = status;
7965             jqXHR.statusText = "" + ( nativeStatusText || statusText );
7966 
7967             // Success/Error
7968             if ( isSuccess ) {
7969                 deferred.resolveWith( callbackContext, [ success, statusText, jqXHR ] );
7970             } else {
7971                 deferred.rejectWith( callbackContext, [ jqXHR, statusText, error ] );
7972             }
7973 
7974             // Status-dependent callbacks
7975             jqXHR.statusCode( statusCode );
7976             statusCode = undefined;
7977 
7978             if ( fireGlobals ) {
7979                 globalEventContext.trigger( "ajax" + ( isSuccess ? "Success" : "Error" ),
7980                         [ jqXHR, s, isSuccess ? success : error ] );
7981             }
7982 
7983             // Complete
7984             completeDeferred.fireWith( callbackContext, [ jqXHR, statusText ] );
7985 
7986             if ( fireGlobals ) {
7987                 globalEventContext.trigger( "ajaxComplete", [ jqXHR, s ] );
7988                 // Handle the global AJAX counter
7989                 if ( !( --jQuery.active ) ) {
7990                     jQuery.event.trigger( "ajaxStop" );
7991                 }
7992             }
7993         }
7994 
7995         // Attach deferreds
7996         deferred.promise( jqXHR );
7997         jqXHR.success = jqXHR.done;
7998         jqXHR.error = jqXHR.fail;
7999         jqXHR.complete = completeDeferred.add;
8000 
8001         // Status-dependent callbacks
8002         jqXHR.statusCode = function( map ) {
8003             if ( map ) {
8004                 var tmp;
8005                 if ( state < 2 ) {
8006                     for ( tmp in map ) {
8007                         statusCode[ tmp ] = [ statusCode[tmp], map[tmp] ];
8008                     }
8009                 } else {
8010                     tmp = map[ jqXHR.status ];
8011                     jqXHR.always( tmp );
8012                 }
8013             }
8014             return this;
8015         };
8016 
8017         // Remove hash character (#7531: and string promotion)
8018         // Add protocol if not provided (#5866: IE7 issue with protocol-less urls)
8019         // We also use the url parameter if available
8020         s.url = ( ( url || s.url ) + "" ).replace( rhash, "" ).replace( rprotocol, ajaxLocParts[ 1 ] + "//" );
8021 
8022         // Extract dataTypes list
8023         s.dataTypes = jQuery.trim( s.dataType || "*" ).toLowerCase().split( core_rspace );
8024 
8025         // Determine if a cross-domain request is in order
8026         if ( s.crossDomain == null ) {
8027             parts = rurl.exec( s.url.toLowerCase() );
8028             s.crossDomain = !!( parts &&
8029                 ( parts[ 1 ] != ajaxLocParts[ 1 ] || parts[ 2 ] != ajaxLocParts[ 2 ] ||
8030                     ( parts[ 3 ] || ( parts[ 1 ] === "http:" ? 80 : 443 ) ) !=
8031                         ( ajaxLocParts[ 3 ] || ( ajaxLocParts[ 1 ] === "http:" ? 80 : 443 ) ) )
8032             );
8033         }
8034 
8035         // Convert data if not already a string
8036         if ( s.data && s.processData && typeof s.data !== "string" ) {
8037             s.data = jQuery.param( s.data, s.traditional );
8038         }
8039 
8040         // Apply prefilters
8041         inspectPrefiltersOrTransports( prefilters, s, options, jqXHR );
8042 
8043         // If request was aborted inside a prefilter, stop there
8044         if ( state === 2 ) {
8045             return jqXHR;
8046         }
8047 
8048         // We can fire global events as of now if asked to
8049         fireGlobals = s.global;
8050 
8051         // Uppercase the type
8052         s.type = s.type.toUpperCase();
8053 
8054         // Determine if request has content
8055         s.hasContent = !rnoContent.test( s.type );
8056 
8057         // Watch for a new set of requests
8058         if ( fireGlobals && jQuery.active++ === 0 ) {
8059             jQuery.event.trigger( "ajaxStart" );
8060         }
8061 
8062         // More options handling for requests with no content
8063         if ( !s.hasContent ) {
8064 
8065             // If data is available, append data to url
8066             if ( s.data ) {
8067                 s.url += ( rquery.test( s.url ) ? "&" : "?" ) + s.data;
8068                 // #9682: remove data so that it's not used in an eventual retry
8069                 delete s.data;
8070             }
8071 
8072             // Get ifModifiedKey before adding the anti-cache parameter
8073             ifModifiedKey = s.url;
8074 
8075             // Add anti-cache in url if needed
8076             if ( s.cache === false ) {
8077 
8078                 var ts = jQuery.now(),
8079                     // try replacing _= if it is there
8080                     ret = s.url.replace( rts, "$1_=" + ts );
8081 
8082                 // if nothing was replaced, add timestamp to the end
8083                 s.url = ret + ( ( ret === s.url ) ? ( rquery.test( s.url ) ? "&" : "?" ) + "_=" + ts : "" );
8084             }
8085         }
8086 
8087         // Set the correct header, if data is being sent
8088         if ( s.data && s.hasContent && s.contentType !== false || options.contentType ) {
8089             jqXHR.setRequestHeader( "Content-Type", s.contentType );
8090         }
8091 
8092         // Set the If-Modified-Since and/or If-None-Match header, if in ifModified mode.
8093         if ( s.ifModified ) {
8094             ifModifiedKey = ifModifiedKey || s.url;
8095             if ( jQuery.lastModified[ ifModifiedKey ] ) {
8096                 jqXHR.setRequestHeader( "If-Modified-Since", jQuery.lastModified[ ifModifiedKey ] );
8097             }
8098             if ( jQuery.etag[ ifModifiedKey ] ) {
8099                 jqXHR.setRequestHeader( "If-None-Match", jQuery.etag[ ifModifiedKey ] );
8100             }
8101         }
8102 
8103         // Set the Accepts header for the server, depending on the dataType
8104         jqXHR.setRequestHeader(
8105             "Accept",
8106             s.dataTypes[ 0 ] && s.accepts[ s.dataTypes[0] ] ?
8107                 s.accepts[ s.dataTypes[0] ] + ( s.dataTypes[ 0 ] !== "*" ? ", " + allTypes + "; q=0.01" : "" ) :
8108                 s.accepts[ "*" ]
8109         );
8110 
8111         // Check for headers option
8112         for ( i in s.headers ) {
8113             jqXHR.setRequestHeader( i, s.headers[ i ] );
8114         }
8115 
8116         // Allow custom headers/mimetypes and early abort
8117         if ( s.beforeSend && ( s.beforeSend.call( callbackContext, jqXHR, s ) === false || state === 2 ) ) {
8118                 // Abort if not done already and return
8119                 return jqXHR.abort();
8120 
8121         }
8122 
8123         // aborting is no longer a cancellation
8124         strAbort = "abort";
8125 
8126         // Install callbacks on deferreds
8127         for ( i in { success: 1, error: 1, complete: 1 } ) {
8128             jqXHR[ i ]( s[ i ] );
8129         }
8130 
8131         // Get transport
8132         transport = inspectPrefiltersOrTransports( transports, s, options, jqXHR );
8133 
8134         // If no transport, we auto-abort
8135         if ( !transport ) {
8136             done( -1, "No Transport" );
8137         } else {
8138             jqXHR.readyState = 1;
8139             // Send global event
8140             if ( fireGlobals ) {
8141                 globalEventContext.trigger( "ajaxSend", [ jqXHR, s ] );
8142             }
8143             // Timeout
8144             if ( s.async && s.timeout > 0 ) {
8145                 timeoutTimer = setTimeout( function(){
8146                     jqXHR.abort( "timeout" );
8147                 }, s.timeout );
8148             }
8149 
8150             try {
8151                 state = 1;
8152                 transport.send( requestHeaders, done );
8153             } catch (e) {
8154                 // Propagate exception as error if not done
8155                 if ( state < 2 ) {
8156                     done( -1, e );
8157                 // Simply rethrow otherwise
8158                 } else {
8159                     throw e;
8160                 }
8161             }
8162         }
8163 
8164         return jqXHR;
8165     },
8166 
8167     // Counter for holding the number of active queries
8168     active: 0,
8169 
8170     // Last-Modified header cache for next request
8171     lastModified: {},
8172     etag: {}
8173 
8174 });
8175 
8176 /* Handles responses to an ajax request:
8177  * - sets all responseXXX fields accordingly
8178  * - finds the right dataType (mediates between content-type and expected dataType)
8179  * - returns the corresponding response
8180  */
8181 function ajaxHandleResponses( s, jqXHR, responses ) {
8182 
8183     var ct, type, finalDataType, firstDataType,
8184         contents = s.contents,
8185         dataTypes = s.dataTypes,
8186         responseFields = s.responseFields;
8187 
8188     // Fill responseXXX fields
8189     for ( type in responseFields ) {
8190         if ( type in responses ) {
8191             jqXHR[ responseFields[type] ] = responses[ type ];
8192         }
8193     }
8194 
8195     // Remove auto dataType and get content-type in the process
8196     while( dataTypes[ 0 ] === "*" ) {
8197         dataTypes.shift();
8198         if ( ct === undefined ) {
8199             ct = s.mimeType || jqXHR.getResponseHeader( "content-type" );
8200         }
8201     }
8202 
8203     // Check if we're dealing with a known content-type
8204     if ( ct ) {
8205         for ( type in contents ) {
8206             if ( contents[ type ] && contents[ type ].test( ct ) ) {
8207                 dataTypes.unshift( type );
8208                 break;
8209             }
8210         }
8211     }
8212 
8213     // Check to see if we have a response for the expected dataType
8214     if ( dataTypes[ 0 ] in responses ) {
8215         finalDataType = dataTypes[ 0 ];
8216     } else {
8217         // Try convertible dataTypes
8218         for ( type in responses ) {
8219             if ( !dataTypes[ 0 ] || s.converters[ type + " " + dataTypes[0] ] ) {
8220                 finalDataType = type;
8221                 break;
8222             }
8223             if ( !firstDataType ) {
8224                 firstDataType = type;
8225             }
8226         }
8227         // Or just use first one
8228         finalDataType = finalDataType || firstDataType;
8229     }
8230 
8231     // If we found a dataType
8232     // We add the dataType to the list if needed
8233     // and return the corresponding response
8234     if ( finalDataType ) {
8235         if ( finalDataType !== dataTypes[ 0 ] ) {
8236             dataTypes.unshift( finalDataType );
8237         }
8238         return responses[ finalDataType ];
8239     }
8240 }
8241 
8242 // Chain conversions given the request and the original response
8243 function ajaxConvert( s, response ) {
8244 
8245     var conv, conv2, current, tmp,
8246         // Work with a copy of dataTypes in case we need to modify it for conversion
8247         dataTypes = s.dataTypes.slice(),
8248         prev = dataTypes[ 0 ],
8249         converters = {},
8250         i = 0;
8251 
8252     // Apply the dataFilter if provided
8253     if ( s.dataFilter ) {
8254         response = s.dataFilter( response, s.dataType );
8255     }
8256 
8257     // Create converters map with lowercased keys
8258     if ( dataTypes[ 1 ] ) {
8259         for ( conv in s.converters ) {
8260             converters[ conv.toLowerCase() ] = s.converters[ conv ];
8261         }
8262     }
8263 
8264     // Convert to each sequential dataType, tolerating list modification
8265     for ( ; (current = dataTypes[++i]); ) {
8266 
8267         // There's only work to do if current dataType is non-auto
8268         if ( current !== "*" ) {
8269 
8270             // Convert response if prev dataType is non-auto and differs from current
8271             if ( prev !== "*" && prev !== current ) {
8272 
8273                 // Seek a direct converter
8274                 conv = converters[ prev + " " + current ] || converters[ "* " + current ];
8275 
8276                 // If none found, seek a pair
8277                 if ( !conv ) {
8278                     for ( conv2 in converters ) {
8279 
8280                         // If conv2 outputs current
8281                         tmp = conv2.split(" ");
8282                         if ( tmp[ 1 ] === current ) {
8283 
8284                             // If prev can be converted to accepted input
8285                             conv = converters[ prev + " " + tmp[ 0 ] ] ||
8286                                 converters[ "* " + tmp[ 0 ] ];
8287                             if ( conv ) {
8288                                 // Condense equivalence converters
8289                                 if ( conv === true ) {
8290                                     conv = converters[ conv2 ];
8291 
8292                                 // Otherwise, insert the intermediate dataType
8293                                 } else if ( converters[ conv2 ] !== true ) {
8294                                     current = tmp[ 0 ];
8295                                     dataTypes.splice( i--, 0, current );
8296                                 }
8297 
8298                                 break;
8299                             }
8300                         }
8301                     }
8302                 }
8303 
8304                 // Apply converter (if not an equivalence)
8305                 if ( conv !== true ) {
8306 
8307                     // Unless errors are allowed to bubble, catch and return them
8308                     if ( conv && s["throws"] ) {
8309                         response = conv( response );
8310                     } else {
8311                         try {
8312                             response = conv( response );
8313                         } catch ( e ) {
8314                             return { state: "parsererror", error: conv ? e : "No conversion from " + prev + " to " + current };
8315                         }
8316                     }
8317                 }
8318             }
8319 
8320             // Update prev for next iteration
8321             prev = current;
8322         }
8323     }
8324 
8325     return { state: "success", data: response };
8326 }
8327 var oldCallbacks = [],
8328     rquestion = /\?/,
8329     rjsonp = /(=)\?(?=&|$)|\?\?/,
8330     nonce = jQuery.now();
8331 
8332 // Default jsonp settings
8333 jQuery.ajaxSetup({
8334     jsonp: "callback",
8335     jsonpCallback: function() {
8336         var callback = oldCallbacks.pop() || ( jQuery.expando + "_" + ( nonce++ ) );
8337         this[ callback ] = true;
8338         return callback;
8339     }
8340 });

8342 // Detect, normalize options and install callbacks for jsonp requests
8343 jQuery.ajaxPrefilter( "json jsonp", function( s, originalSettings, jqXHR ) {
8344 
8345     var callbackName, overwritten, responseContainer,
8346         data = s.data,
8347         url = s.url,
8348         hasCallback = s.jsonp !== false,
8349         replaceInUrl = hasCallback && rjsonp.test( url ),
8350         replaceInData = hasCallback && !replaceInUrl && typeof data === "string" &&
8351             !( s.contentType || "" ).indexOf("application/x-www-form-urlencoded") &&
8352             rjsonp.test( data );
8353 
8354     // Handle iff the expected data type is "jsonp" or we have a parameter to set
8355     if ( s.dataTypes[ 0 ] === "jsonp" || replaceInUrl || replaceInData ) {
8356 
8357         // Get callback name, remembering preexisting value associated with it
8358         callbackName = s.jsonpCallback = jQuery.isFunction( s.jsonpCallback ) ?
8359             s.jsonpCallback() :
8360             s.jsonpCallback;
8361         overwritten = window[ callbackName ];
8362 
8363         // Insert callback into url or form data
8364         if ( replaceInUrl ) {
8365             s.url = url.replace( rjsonp, "$1" + callbackName );
8366         } else if ( replaceInData ) {
8367             s.data = data.replace( rjsonp, "$1" + callbackName );
8368         } else if ( hasCallback ) {
8369             s.url += ( rquestion.test( url ) ? "&" : "?" ) + s.jsonp + "=" + callbackName;
8370         }
8371 
8372         // Use data converter to retrieve json after script execution
8373         s.converters["script json"] = function() {
8374             if ( !responseContainer ) {
8375                 jQuery.error( callbackName + " was not called" );
8376             }
8377             return responseContainer[ 0 ];
8378         };
8379 
8380         // force json dataType
8381         s.dataTypes[ 0 ] = "json";
8382 
8383         // Install callback
8384         window[ callbackName ] = function() {
8385             responseContainer = arguments;
8386         };
8387 
8388         // Clean-up function (fires after converters)
8389         jqXHR.always(function() {
8390             // Restore preexisting value
8391             window[ callbackName ] = overwritten;
8392 
8393             // Save back as free
8394             if ( s[ callbackName ] ) {
8395                 // make sure that re-using the options doesn't screw things around
8396                 s.jsonpCallback = originalSettings.jsonpCallback;
8397 
8398                 // save the callback name for future use
8399                 oldCallbacks.push( callbackName );
8400             }
8401 
8402             // Call if it was a function and we have a response
8403             if ( responseContainer && jQuery.isFunction( overwritten ) ) {
8404                 overwritten( responseContainer[ 0 ] );
8405             }
8406 
8407             responseContainer = overwritten = undefined;
8408         });
8409 
8410         // Delegate to script
8411         return "script";
8412     }
8413 });

8441 // Bind script tag hack transport
8442 jQuery.ajaxTransport( "script", function(s) {
8443 
8444     // This transport only deals with cross domain requests
8445     if ( s.crossDomain ) {
8446 
8447         var script,
8448             head = document.head || document.getElementsByTagName( "head" )[0] || document.documentElement;
8449 
8450         return {
8451 
8452             send: function( _, callback ) {
8453 
8454                 script = document.createElement( "script" );
8455 
8456                 script.async = "async";
8457 
8458                 if ( s.scriptCharset ) {
8459                     script.charset = s.scriptCharset;
8460                 }
8461 
8462                 script.src = s.url;
8463 
8464                 // Attach handlers for all browsers
8465                 script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = function( _, isAbort ) {
8466 
8467                     if ( isAbort || !script.readyState || /loaded|complete/.test( script.readyState ) ) {
8468 
8469                         // Handle memory leak in IE
8470                         script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = null;
8471 
8472                         // Remove the script
8473                         if ( head && script.parentNode ) {
8474                             head.removeChild( script );
8475                         }
8476 
8477                         // Dereference the script
8478                         script = undefined;
8479 
8480                         // Callback if not abort
8481                         if ( !isAbort ) {
8482                             callback( 200, "success" );
8483                         }
8484                     }
8485                 };
8486                 // Use insertBefore instead of appendChild  to circumvent an IE6 bug.
8487                 // This arises when a base node is used (#2709 and #4378).
8488                 head.insertBefore( script, head.firstChild );
8489             },
8490 
8491             abort: function() {
8492                 if ( script ) {
8493                     script.onload( 0, 1 );
8494                 }
8495             }
8496         };
8497     }

8509 // Functions to create xhrs
8510 function createStandardXHR() {
8511     try {
8512         return new window.XMLHttpRequest();
8513     } catch( e ) {}

8516 function createActiveXHR() {
8517     try {
8518         return new window.ActiveXObject( "Microsoft.XMLHTTP" );

8522 // Create the request object
8523 // (This is still attached to ajaxSettings for backward compatibility)
8524 jQuery.ajaxSettings.xhr = window.ActiveXObject ?
8525     /* Microsoft failed to properly
8526      * implement the XMLHttpRequest in IE7 (can't request local files),
8527      * so we use the ActiveXObject when it is available
8528      * Additionally XMLHttpRequest can be disabled in IE7/IE8 so
8529      * we need a fallback.

8531     function() {
8532         return !this.isLocal && createStandardXHR() || createActiveXHR();

8537 // Determine support properties
8538 (function( xhr ) {
8539     jQuery.extend( jQuery.support, {
8540         ajax: !!xhr,
8541         cors: !!xhr && ( "withCredentials" in xhr )
8542     });
