8545 // Create transport if the browser can provide an xhr
8546 if ( jQuery.support.ajax ) {
8547 
8548     jQuery.ajaxTransport(function( s ) {
8549         // Cross domain only allowed if supported through XMLHttpRequest
8550         if ( !s.crossDomain || jQuery.support.cors ) {
8551 
8552             var callback;
8553 
8554             return {
8555                 send: function( headers, complete ) {
8556 
8557                     // Get a new xhr
8558                     var handle, i,
8559                         xhr = s.xhr();
8560 
8561                     // Open the socket
8562                     // Passing null username, generates a login popup on Opera (#2865)
8563                     if ( s.username ) {
8564                         xhr.open( s.type, s.url, s.async, s.username, s.password );
8565                     } else {
8566                         xhr.open( s.type, s.url, s.async );
8567                     }
8568 
8569                     // Apply custom fields if provided
8570                     if ( s.xhrFields ) {
8571                         for ( i in s.xhrFields ) {
8572                             xhr[ i ] = s.xhrFields[ i ];
8573                         }
8574                     }
8575 
8576                     // Override mime type if needed
8577                     if ( s.mimeType && xhr.overrideMimeType ) {
8578                         xhr.overrideMimeType( s.mimeType );
8579                     }
8580 
8581                     // X-Requested-With header
8582                     // For cross-domain requests, seeing as conditions for a preflight are
8583                     // akin to a jigsaw puzzle, we simply never set it to be sure.
8584                     // (it can always be set on a per-request basis or even using ajaxSetup)
8585                     // For same-domain requests, won't change header if already provided.
8586                     if ( !s.crossDomain && !headers["X-Requested-With"] ) {
8587                         headers[ "X-Requested-With" ] = "XMLHttpRequest";
8588                     }
8589 
8590                     // Need an extra try/catch for cross domain requests in Firefox 3
8591                     try {
8592                         for ( i in headers ) {
8593                             xhr.setRequestHeader( i, headers[ i ] );
8594                         }
8595                     } catch( _ ) {}
8596 
8597                     // Do send the request
8598                     // This may raise an exception which is actually
8599                     // handled in jQuery.ajax (so no try/catch here)
8600                     xhr.send( ( s.hasContent && s.data ) || null );
8601 
8602                     // Listener
8603                     callback = function( _, isAbort ) {
8604 
8605                         var status,
8606                             statusText,
8607                             responseHeaders,
8608                             responses,
8609                             xml;
8610 
8611                         // Firefox throws exceptions when accessing properties
8612                         // of an xhr when a network error occurred
8613                         // http://helpful.knobs-dials.com/index.php/Component_returned_failure_code:_0x80040111_(NS_ERROR_NOT_AVAILABLE)
8614                         try {
8615 
8616                             // Was never called and is aborted or complete
8617                             if ( callback && ( isAbort || xhr.readyState === 4 ) ) {
8618 
8619                                 // Only called once
8620                                 callback = undefined;
8621 
8622                                 // Do not keep as active anymore
8623                                 if ( handle ) {
8624                                     xhr.onreadystatechange = jQuery.noop;
8625                                     if ( xhrOnUnloadAbort ) {
8626                                         delete xhrCallbacks[ handle ];
8627                                     }
8628                                 }
8629 
8630                                 // If it's an abort
8631                                 if ( isAbort ) {
8632                                     // Abort it manually if needed
8633                                     if ( xhr.readyState !== 4 ) {
8634                                         xhr.abort();
8635                                     }
8636                                 } else {
8637                                     status = xhr.status;
8638                                     responseHeaders = xhr.getAllResponseHeaders();
8639                                     responses = {};
8640                                     xml = xhr.responseXML;
8641 
8642                                     // Construct response list
8643                                     if ( xml && xml.documentElement /* #4958 */ ) {
8644                                         responses.xml = xml;
8645                                     }
8646 
8647                                     // When requesting binary data, IE6-9 will throw an exception
8648                                     // on any attempt to access responseText (#11426)
8649                                     try {
8650                                         responses.text = xhr.responseText;
8651                                     } catch( _ ) {
8652                                     }
8653 
8654                                     // Firefox throws an exception when accessing
8655                                     // statusText for faulty cross-domain requests
8656                                     try {
8657                                         statusText = xhr.statusText;
8658                                     } catch( e ) {
8659                                         // We normalize with Webkit giving an empty statusText
8660                                         statusText = "";
8661                                     }
8662 
8663                                     // Filter status for non standard behaviors
8664 
8665                                     // If the request is local and we have data: assume a success
8666                                     // (success with no data won't get notified, that's the best we
8667                                     // can do given current implementations)
8668                                     if ( !status && s.isLocal && !s.crossDomain ) {
8669                                         status = responses.text ? 200 : 404;
8670                                     // IE - #1450: sometimes returns 1223 when it should be 204
8671                                     } else if ( status === 1223 ) {
8672                                         status = 204;
8673                                     }
8674                                 }
8675                             }
8676                         } catch( firefoxAccessException ) {
8677                             if ( !isAbort ) {
8678                                 complete( -1, firefoxAccessException );
8679                             }
8680                         }
8681 
8682                         // Call complete if needed
8683                         if ( responses ) {
8684                             complete( status, statusText, responses, responseHeaders );
8685                         }
8686                     };
8687 
8688                     if ( !s.async ) {
8689                         // if we're in sync mode we fire the callback
8690                         callback();
8691                     } else if ( xhr.readyState === 4 ) {
8692                         // (IE6 & IE7) if it's in cache and has been
8693                         // retrieved directly we need to fire the callback
8694                         setTimeout( callback, 0 );
8695                     } else {
8696                         handle = ++xhrId;
8697                         if ( xhrOnUnloadAbort ) {
8698                             // Create the active xhrs callbacks list if needed
8699                             // and attach the unload handler
8700                             if ( !xhrCallbacks ) {
8701                                 xhrCallbacks = {};
8702                                 jQuery( window ).unload( xhrOnUnloadAbort );
8703                             }
8704                             // Add to list of active xhrs callbacks
8705                             xhrCallbacks[ handle ] = callback;
8706                         }
8707                         xhr.onreadystatechange = callback;
8708                     }
8709                 },
8710 
8711                 abort: function() {
8712                     if ( callback ) {
8713                         callback(0,1);
8714                     }
8715                 }
8716             };
8717         }
8718     });
8719 }
8720 var fxNow, timerId,
8721     rfxtypes = /^(?:toggle|show|hide)$/,
8722     rfxnum = new RegExp( "^(?:([-+])=|)(" + core_pnum + ")([a-z%]*)$", "i" ),
8723     rrun = /queueHooks$/,
8724     animationPrefilters = [ defaultPrefilter ],
8725     tweeners = {
8726         "*": [function( prop, value ) {
8727             var end, unit, prevScale,
8728                 tween = this.createTween( prop, value ),
8729                 parts = rfxnum.exec( value ),
8730                 target = tween.cur(),
8731                 start = +target || 0,
8732                 scale = 1;
8733 
8734             if ( parts ) {
8735                 end = +parts[2];
8736                 unit = parts[3] || ( jQuery.cssNumber[ prop ] ? "" : "px" );
8737 
8738                 // We need to compute starting value
8739                 if ( unit !== "px" && start ) {
8740                     // Iteratively approximate from a nonzero starting point
8741                     // Prefer the current property, because this process will be trivial if it uses the same units
8742                     // Fallback to end or a simple constant
8743                     start = jQuery.css( tween.elem, prop, true ) || end || 1;
8744 
8745                     do {
8746                         // If previous iteration zeroed out, double until we get *something*
8747                         // Use a string for doubling factor so we don't accidentally see scale as unchanged below
8748                         prevScale = scale = scale || ".5";
8749 
8750                         // Adjust and apply
8751                         start = start / scale;
8752                         jQuery.style( tween.elem, prop, start + unit );
8753 
8754                         // Update scale, tolerating zeroes from tween.cur()
8755                         scale = tween.cur() / target;
8756 
8757                     // Stop looping if we've hit the mark or scale is unchanged
8758                     } while ( scale !== 1 && scale !== prevScale );
8759                 }
8760 
8761                 tween.unit = unit;
8762                 tween.start = start;
8763                 // If a +=/-= token was provided, we're doing a relative animation
8764                 tween.end = parts[1] ? start + ( parts[1] + 1 ) * end : end;
8765             }
8766             return tween;
8767         }]
8768     };
8769 
8770 // Animations created synchronously will run synchronously
8771 function createFxNow() {
8772     setTimeout(function() {
8773         fxNow = undefined;
8774     }, 0 );
8775     return ( fxNow = jQuery.now() );
8776 }
8777 
8778 function createTweens( animation, props ) {
8779     jQuery.each( props, function( prop, value ) {
8780         var collection = ( tweeners[ prop ] || [] ).concat( tweeners[ "*" ] ),
8781             index = 0,
8782             length = collection.length;
8783         for ( ; index < length; index++ ) {
8784             if ( collection[ index ].call( animation, prop, value ) ) {
8785 
8786                 // we're done with this property
8787                 return;
8788             }
8789         }
8790     });
8791 }
8792 
8793 function Animation( elem, properties, options ) {
8794     var result,
8795         index = 0,
8796         tweenerIndex = 0,
8797         length = animationPrefilters.length,
8798         deferred = jQuery.Deferred().always( function() {
8799             // don't match elem in the :animated selector
8800             delete tick.elem;
8801         }),
8802         tick = function() {
8803             var currentTime = fxNow || createFxNow(),
8804                 remaining = Math.max( 0, animation.startTime + animation.duration - currentTime ),
8805                 percent = 1 - ( remaining / animation.duration || 0 ),
8806                 index = 0,
8807                 length = animation.tweens.length;
8808 
8809             for ( ; index < length ; index++ ) {
8810                 animation.tweens[ index ].run( percent );
8811             }
8812 
8813             deferred.notifyWith( elem, [ animation, percent, remaining ]);
8814 
8815             if ( percent < 1 && length ) {
8816                 return remaining;
8817             } else {
8818                 deferred.resolveWith( elem, [ animation ] );
8819                 return false;
8820             }
8821         },
8822         animation = deferred.promise({
8823             elem: elem,
8824             props: jQuery.extend( {}, properties ),
8825             opts: jQuery.extend( true, { specialEasing: {} }, options ),
8826             originalProperties: properties,
8827             originalOptions: options,
8828             startTime: fxNow || createFxNow(),
8829             duration: options.duration,
8830             tweens: [],
8831             createTween: function( prop, end, easing ) {
8832                 var tween = jQuery.Tween( elem, animation.opts, prop, end,
8833                         animation.opts.specialEasing[ prop ] || animation.opts.easing );
8834                 animation.tweens.push( tween );
8835                 return tween;
8836             },
8837             stop: function( gotoEnd ) {
8838                 var index = 0,
8839                     // if we are going to the end, we want to run all the tweens
8840                     // otherwise we skip this part
8841                     length = gotoEnd ? animation.tweens.length : 0;
8842 
8843                 for ( ; index < length ; index++ ) {
8844                     animation.tweens[ index ].run( 1 );
8845                 }
8846 
8847                 // resolve when we played the last frame
8848                 // otherwise, reject
8849                 if ( gotoEnd ) {
8850                     deferred.resolveWith( elem, [ animation, gotoEnd ] );
8851                 } else {
8852                     deferred.rejectWith( elem, [ animation, gotoEnd ] );
8853                 }
8854                 return this;
8855             }
8856         }),
8857         props = animation.props;
8858 
8859     propFilter( props, animation.opts.specialEasing );
8860 
8861     for ( ; index < length ; index++ ) {
8862         result = animationPrefilters[ index ].call( animation, elem, props, animation.opts );
8863         if ( result ) {
8864             return result;
8865         }
8866     }
8867 
8868     createTweens( animation, props );
8869 
8870     if ( jQuery.isFunction( animation.opts.start ) ) {
8871         animation.opts.start.call( elem, animation );
8872     }
8873 
8874     jQuery.fx.timer(
8875         jQuery.extend( tick, {
8876             anim: animation,
8877             queue: animation.opts.queue,
8878             elem: elem
8879         })
8880     );
8881 
8882     // attach callbacks from options
8883     return animation.progress( animation.opts.progress )
8884         .done( animation.opts.done, animation.opts.complete )
8885         .fail( animation.opts.fail )
8886         .always( animation.opts.always );
8887 }
8888 
8889 function propFilter( props, specialEasing ) {
8890     var index, name, easing, value, hooks;
8891 
8892     // camelCase, specialEasing and expand cssHook pass
8893     for ( index in props ) {
8894         name = jQuery.camelCase( index );
8895         easing = specialEasing[ name ];
8896         value = props[ index ];
8897         if ( jQuery.isArray( value ) ) {
8898             easing = value[ 1 ];
8899             value = props[ index ] = value[ 0 ];
8900         }
8901 
8902         if ( index !== name ) {
8903             props[ name ] = value;
8904             delete props[ index ];
8905         }
8906 
8907         hooks = jQuery.cssHooks[ name ];
8908         if ( hooks && "expand" in hooks ) {
8909             value = hooks.expand( value );
8910             delete props[ name ];
8911 
8912             // not quite $.extend, this wont overwrite keys already present.
8913             // also - reusing 'index' from above because we have the correct "name"
8914             for ( index in value ) {
8915                 if ( !( index in props ) ) {
8916                     props[ index ] = value[ index ];
8917                     specialEasing[ index ] = easing;
8918                 }
8919             }
8920         } else {
8921             specialEasing[ name ] = easing;
8922         }
8923     }
8924 }
8925 
8926 jQuery.Animation = jQuery.extend( Animation, {
8927 
8928     tweener: function( props, callback ) {
8929         if ( jQuery.isFunction( props ) ) {
8930             callback = props;
8931             props = [ "*" ];
8932         } else {
8933             props = props.split(" ");
8934         }
8935 
8936         var prop,
8937             index = 0,
8938             length = props.length;
8939 
8940         for ( ; index < length ; index++ ) {
8941             prop = props[ index ];
8942             tweeners[ prop ] = tweeners[ prop ] || [];
8943             tweeners[ prop ].unshift( callback );
8944         }
8945     },
8946 
8947     prefilter: function( callback, prepend ) {
8948         if ( prepend ) {
8949             animationPrefilters.unshift( callback );
8950         } else {
8951             animationPrefilters.push( callback );
8952         }
8953     }
8954 });
8955 
8956 function defaultPrefilter( elem, props, opts ) {
8957     var index, prop, value, length, dataShow, tween, hooks, oldfire,
8958         anim = this,
8959         style = elem.style,
8960         orig = {},
8961         handled = [],
8962         hidden = elem.nodeType && isHidden( elem );
8963 
8964     // handle queue: false promises
8965     if ( !opts.queue ) {
8966         hooks = jQuery._queueHooks( elem, "fx" );
8967         if ( hooks.unqueued == null ) {
8968             hooks.unqueued = 0;
8969             oldfire = hooks.empty.fire;
8970             hooks.empty.fire = function() {
8971                 if ( !hooks.unqueued ) {
8972                     oldfire();
8973                 }
8974             };
8975         }
8976         hooks.unqueued++;
8977 
8978         anim.always(function() {
8979             // doing this makes sure that the complete handler will be called
8980             // before this completes
8981             anim.always(function() {
8982                 hooks.unqueued--;
8983                 if ( !jQuery.queue( elem, "fx" ).length ) {
8984                     hooks.empty.fire();
8985                 }
8986             });
8987         });
8988     }
8989 
8990     // height/width overflow pass
8991     if ( elem.nodeType === 1 && ( "height" in props || "width" in props ) ) {
8992         // Make sure that nothing sneaks out
8993         // Record all 3 overflow attributes because IE does not
8994         // change the overflow attribute when overflowX and
8995         // overflowY are set to the same value
8996         opts.overflow = [ style.overflow, style.overflowX, style.overflowY ];
8997 
8998         // Set display property to inline-block for height/width
8999         // animations on inline elements that are having width/height animated
9000         if ( jQuery.css( elem, "display" ) === "inline" &&
9001                 jQuery.css( elem, "float" ) === "none" ) {
9002 
9003             // inline-level elements accept inline-block;
9004             // block-level elements need to be inline with layout
9005             if ( !jQuery.support.inlineBlockNeedsLayout || css_defaultDisplay( elem.nodeName ) === "inline" ) {
9006                 style.display = "inline-block";
9007 
9008             } else {
9009                 style.zoom = 1;
9010             }
9011         }
9012     }
9013 
9014     if ( opts.overflow ) {
9015         style.overflow = "hidden";
9016         if ( !jQuery.support.shrinkWrapBlocks ) {
9017             anim.done(function() {
9018                 style.overflow = opts.overflow[ 0 ];
9019                 style.overflowX = opts.overflow[ 1 ];
9020                 style.overflowY = opts.overflow[ 2 ];
9021             });
9022         }
9023     }
9024 
9025 
9026     // show/hide pass
9027     for ( index in props ) {
9028         value = props[ index ];
9029         if ( rfxtypes.exec( value ) ) {
9030             delete props[ index ];
9031             if ( value === ( hidden ? "hide" : "show" ) ) {
9032                 continue;
9033             }
9034             handled.push( index );
9035         }
9036     }
9037 
9038     length = handled.length;
9039     if ( length ) {
9040         dataShow = jQuery._data( elem, "fxshow" ) || jQuery._data( elem, "fxshow", {} );
9041         if ( hidden ) {
9042             jQuery( elem ).show();
9043         } else {
9044             anim.done(function() {
9045                 jQuery( elem ).hide();
9046             });
9047         }
9048         anim.done(function() {
9049             var prop;
9050             jQuery.removeData( elem, "fxshow", true );
9051             for ( prop in orig ) {
9052                 jQuery.style( elem, prop, orig[ prop ] );
9053             }
9054         });
9055         for ( index = 0 ; index < length ; index++ ) {
9056             prop = handled[ index ];
9057             tween = anim.createTween( prop, hidden ? dataShow[ prop ] : 0 );
9058             orig[ prop ] = dataShow[ prop ] || jQuery.style( elem, prop );
9059 
9060             if ( !( prop in dataShow ) ) {
9061                 dataShow[ prop ] = tween.start;
9062                 if ( hidden ) {
9063                     tween.end = tween.start;
9064                     tween.start = prop === "width" || prop === "height" ? 1 : 0;
9065                 }
9066             }
9067         }
9068     }
9069 }
9070 
9071 function Tween( elem, options, prop, end, easing ) {
9072     return new Tween.prototype.init( elem, options, prop, end, easing );
9073 }
9074 jQuery.Tween = Tween;
9075 
9076 Tween.prototype = {
9077     constructor: Tween,
9078     init: function( elem, options, prop, end, easing, unit ) {
9079         this.elem = elem;
9080         this.prop = prop;
9081         this.easing = easing || "swing";
9082         this.options = options;
9083         this.start = this.now = this.cur();
9084         this.end = end;
9085         this.unit = unit || ( jQuery.cssNumber[ prop ] ? "" : "px" );
9086     },
9087     cur: function() {
9088         var hooks = Tween.propHooks[ this.prop ];
9089 
9090         return hooks && hooks.get ?
9091             hooks.get( this ) :
9092             Tween.propHooks._default.get( this );
9093     },
9094     run: function( percent ) {
9095         var eased,
9096             hooks = Tween.propHooks[ this.prop ];
9097 
9098         if ( this.options.duration ) {
9099             this.pos = eased = jQuery.easing[ this.easing ](
9100                 percent, this.options.duration * percent, 0, 1, this.options.duration
9101             );
9102         } else {
9103             this.pos = eased = percent;
9104         }
9105         this.now = ( this.end - this.start ) * eased + this.start;
9106 
9107         if ( this.options.step ) {
9108             this.options.step.call( this.elem, this.now, this );
9109         }
9110 
9111         if ( hooks && hooks.set ) {
9112             hooks.set( this );
9113         } else {
9114             Tween.propHooks._default.set( this );
9115         }
9116         return this;
9117     }
9118 };
9119 
9120 Tween.prototype.init.prototype = Tween.prototype;
9121 
9122 Tween.propHooks = {
9123     _default: {
9124         get: function( tween ) {
9125             var result;
9126 
9127             if ( tween.elem[ tween.prop ] != null &&
9128                 (!tween.elem.style || tween.elem.style[ tween.prop ] == null) ) {
9129                 return tween.elem[ tween.prop ];
9130             }
9131 
9132             // passing any value as a 4th parameter to .css will automatically
9133             // attempt a parseFloat and fallback to a string if the parse fails
9134             // so, simple values such as "10px" are parsed to Float.
9135             // complex values such as "rotate(1rad)" are returned as is.
9136             result = jQuery.css( tween.elem, tween.prop, false, "" );
9137             // Empty strings, null, undefined and "auto" are converted to 0.
9138             return !result || result === "auto" ? 0 : result;
9139         },
9140         set: function( tween ) {
9141             // use step hook for back compat - use cssHook if its there - use .style if its
9142             // available and use plain properties where available
9143             if ( jQuery.fx.step[ tween.prop ] ) {
9144                 jQuery.fx.step[ tween.prop ]( tween );
9145             } else if ( tween.elem.style && ( tween.elem.style[ jQuery.cssProps[ tween.prop ] ] != null || jQuery.cssHooks[ tween.prop ] ) ) {
9146                 jQuery.style( tween.elem, tween.prop, tween.now + tween.unit );
9147             } else {
9148                 tween.elem[ tween.prop ] = tween.now;
9149             }
9150         }
9151     }
9152 };
9153 
9154 // Remove in 2.0 - this supports IE8's panic based approach
9155 // to setting things on disconnected nodes
9156 
9157 Tween.propHooks.scrollTop = Tween.propHooks.scrollLeft = {
9158     set: function( tween ) {
9159         if ( tween.elem.nodeType && tween.elem.parentNode ) {
9160             tween.elem[ tween.prop ] = tween.now;
9161         }
9162     }
9163 };
9164 
9165 jQuery.each([ "toggle", "show", "hide" ], function( i, name ) {
9166     var cssFn = jQuery.fn[ name ];
9167     jQuery.fn[ name ] = function( speed, easing, callback ) {
9168         return speed == null || typeof speed === "boolean" ||
9169             // special check for .toggle( handler, handler, ... )
9170             ( !i && jQuery.isFunction( speed ) && jQuery.isFunction( easing ) ) ?
9171             cssFn.apply( this, arguments ) :
9172             this.animate( genFx( name, true ), speed, easing, callback );
9173     };
9174 });
9175 
9176 jQuery.fn.extend({
9177     fadeTo: function( speed, to, easing, callback ) {
9178 
9179         // show any hidden elements after setting opacity to 0
9180         return this.filter( isHidden ).css( "opacity", 0 ).show()
9181 
9182             // animate to the value specified
9183             .end().animate({ opacity: to }, speed, easing, callback );
9184     },
9185     animate: function( prop, speed, easing, callback ) {
9186         var empty = jQuery.isEmptyObject( prop ),
9187             optall = jQuery.speed( speed, easing, callback ),
9188             doAnimation = function() {
9189                 // Operate on a copy of prop so per-property easing won't be lost
9190                 var anim = Animation( this, jQuery.extend( {}, prop ), optall );
9191 
9192                 // Empty animations resolve immediately
9193                 if ( empty ) {
9194                     anim.stop( true );
9195                 }
9196             };
9197 
9198         return empty || optall.queue === false ?
9199             this.each( doAnimation ) :
9200             this.queue( optall.queue, doAnimation );
9201     },
9202     stop: function( type, clearQueue, gotoEnd ) {
9203         var stopQueue = function( hooks ) {
9204             var stop = hooks.stop;
9205             delete hooks.stop;
9206             stop( gotoEnd );
9207         };
9208 
9209         if ( typeof type !== "string" ) {
9210             gotoEnd = clearQueue;
9211             clearQueue = type;
9212             type = undefined;
9213         }
9214         if ( clearQueue && type !== false ) {
9215             this.queue( type || "fx", [] );
9216         }
9217 
9218         return this.each(function() {
9219             var dequeue = true,
9220                 index = type != null && type + "queueHooks",
9221                 timers = jQuery.timers,
9222                 data = jQuery._data( this );
9223 
9224             if ( index ) {
9225                 if ( data[ index ] && data[ index ].stop ) {
9226                     stopQueue( data[ index ] );
9227                 }
9228             } else {
9229                 for ( index in data ) {
9230                     if ( data[ index ] && data[ index ].stop && rrun.test( index ) ) {
9231                         stopQueue( data[ index ] );
9232                     }
9233                 }
9234             }
9235 
9236             for ( index = timers.length; index--; ) {
9237                 if ( timers[ index ].elem === this && (type == null || timers[ index ].queue === type) ) {
9238                     timers[ index ].anim.stop( gotoEnd );
9239                     dequeue = false;
9240                     timers.splice( index, 1 );
9241                 }
9242             }
9243 
9244             // start the next in the queue if the last step wasn't forced
9245             // timers currently will call their complete callbacks, which will dequeue
9246             // but only if they were gotoEnd
9247             if ( dequeue || !gotoEnd ) {
9248                 jQuery.dequeue( this, type );
9249             }
9250         });
9251     }
9252 });
9253 
9254 // Generate parameters to create a standard animation
9255 function genFx( type, includeWidth ) {
9256     var which,
9257         attrs = { height: type },
9258         i = 0;
9259 
9260     // if we include width, step value is 1 to do all cssExpand values,
9261     // if we don't include width, step value is 2 to skip over Left and Right
9262     includeWidth = includeWidth? 1 : 0;
9263     for( ; i < 4 ; i += 2 - includeWidth ) {
9264         which = cssExpand[ i ];
9265         attrs[ "margin" + which ] = attrs[ "padding" + which ] = type;
9266     }
9267 
9268     if ( includeWidth ) {
9269         attrs.opacity = attrs.width = type;
9270     }
9271 
9272     return attrs;
9273 }
9274 
9275 // Generate shortcuts for custom animations
9276 jQuery.each({
9277     slideDown: genFx("show"),
9278     slideUp: genFx("hide"),
9279     slideToggle: genFx("toggle"),
9280     fadeIn: { opacity: "show" },
9281     fadeOut: { opacity: "hide" },
9282     fadeToggle: { opacity: "toggle" }
9283 }, function( name, props ) {
9284     jQuery.fn[ name ] = function( speed, easing, callback ) {
9285         return this.animate( props, speed, easing, callback );
9286     };
9287 });
9288 
9289 jQuery.speed = function( speed, easing, fn ) {
9290     var opt = speed && typeof speed === "object" ? jQuery.extend( {}, speed ) : {
9291         complete: fn || !fn && easing ||
9292             jQuery.isFunction( speed ) && speed,
9293         duration: speed,
9294         easing: fn && easing || easing && !jQuery.isFunction( easing ) && easing
9295     };
9296 
9297     opt.duration = jQuery.fx.off ? 0 : typeof opt.duration === "number" ? opt.duration :
9298         opt.duration in jQuery.fx.speeds ? jQuery.fx.speeds[ opt.duration ] : jQuery.fx.speeds._default;
9299 
9300     // normalize opt.queue - true/undefined/null -> "fx"
9301     if ( opt.queue == null || opt.queue === true ) {
9302         opt.queue = "fx";
9303     }
9304 
9305     // Queueing
9306     opt.old = opt.complete;
9307 
9308     opt.complete = function() {
9309         if ( jQuery.isFunction( opt.old ) ) {
9310             opt.old.call( this );
9311         }
9312 
9313         if ( opt.queue ) {
9314             jQuery.dequeue( this, opt.queue );
9315         }
9316     };
9317 
9318     return opt;
9319 };
9320 
9321 jQuery.easing = {
9322     linear: function( p ) {
9323         return p;
9324     },
9325     swing: function( p ) {
9326         return 0.5 - Math.cos( p*Math.PI ) / 2;
9327     }
9328 };

9330 jQuery.timers = [];
9331 jQuery.fx = Tween.prototype.init;
9332 jQuery.fx.tick = function() {
9333     var timer,
9334         timers = jQuery.timers,
9335         i = 0;
9336 
9337     for ( ; i < timers.length; i++ ) {
9338         timer = timers[ i ];
9339         // Checks the timer has not already been removed
9340         if ( !timer() && timers[ i ] === timer ) {
9341             timers.splice( i--, 1 );
9342         }
9343     }
9344 
9345     if ( !timers.length ) {
9346         jQuery.fx.stop();
9347     }
9348 };
9349 
9350 jQuery.fx.timer = function( timer ) {
9351     if ( timer() && jQuery.timers.push( timer ) && !timerId ) {
9352         timerId = setInterval( jQuery.fx.tick, jQuery.fx.interval );
9353     }
9354 };
9355 
9356 jQuery.fx.interval = 13;
9357 
9358 jQuery.fx.stop = function() {
9359     clearInterval( timerId );
9360     timerId = null;
9361 };

9363 jQuery.fx.speeds = {
9364     slow: 600,
9365     fast: 200,
9366     // Default speed
9367     _default: 400
9368 };

9371 jQuery.fx.step = {};

9373 if ( jQuery.expr && jQuery.expr.filters ) {
9374     jQuery.expr.filters.animated = function( elem ) {
9375         return jQuery.grep(jQuery.timers, function( fn ) {
9376             return elem === fn.elem;
9377         }).length;
9378     };

9380 var rroot = /^(?:body|html)$/i;
9381 
9382 jQuery.fn.offset = function( options ) {
9383     if ( arguments.length ) {
9384         return options === undefined ?
9385             this :
9386             this.each(function( i ) {
9387                 jQuery.offset.setOffset( this, options, i );
9388             });
9389     }
9390 
9391     var box, docElem, body, win, clientTop, clientLeft, scrollTop, scrollLeft, top, left,
9392         elem = this[ 0 ],
9393         doc = elem && elem.ownerDocument;
9394 
9395     if ( !doc ) {
9396         return;
9397     }
9398 
9399     if ( (body = doc.body) === elem ) {
9400         return jQuery.offset.bodyOffset( elem );
9401     }
9402 
9403     docElem = doc.documentElement;
9404 
9405     // Make sure we're not dealing with a disconnected DOM node
9406     if ( !jQuery.contains( docElem, elem ) ) {
9407         return { top: 0, left: 0 };
9408     }
9409 
9410     box = elem.getBoundingClientRect();
9411     win = getWindow( doc );
9412     clientTop  = docElem.clientTop  || body.clientTop  || 0;
9413     clientLeft = docElem.clientLeft || body.clientLeft || 0;
9414     scrollTop  = win.pageYOffset || docElem.scrollTop;
9415     scrollLeft = win.pageXOffset || docElem.scrollLeft;
9416     top  = box.top  + scrollTop  - clientTop;
9417     left = box.left + scrollLeft - clientLeft;
9418 
9419     return { top: top, left: left };
9420 };
9421 
9422 jQuery.offset = {
9423 
9424     bodyOffset: function( body ) {
9425         var top = body.offsetTop,
9426             left = body.offsetLeft;
9427 
9428         if ( jQuery.support.doesNotIncludeMarginInBodyOffset ) {
9429             top  += parseFloat( jQuery.css(body, "marginTop") ) || 0;
9430             left += parseFloat( jQuery.css(body, "marginLeft") ) || 0;
9431         }
9432 
9433         return { top: top, left: left };
9434     },
9435 
9436     setOffset: function( elem, options, i ) {
9437         var position = jQuery.css( elem, "position" );
9438 
9439         // set position first, in-case top/left are set even on static elem
9440         if ( position === "static" ) {
9441             elem.style.position = "relative";
9442         }
9443 
9444         var curElem = jQuery( elem ),
9445             curOffset = curElem.offset(),
9446             curCSSTop = jQuery.css( elem, "top" ),
9447             curCSSLeft = jQuery.css( elem, "left" ),
9448             calculatePosition = ( position === "absolute" || position === "fixed" ) && jQuery.inArray("auto", [curCSSTop, curCSSLeft]) > -1,
9449             props = {}, curPosition = {}, curTop, curLeft;
9450 
9451         // need to be able to calculate position if either top or left is auto and position is either absolute or fixed
9452         if ( calculatePosition ) {
9453             curPosition = curElem.position();
9454             curTop = curPosition.top;
9455             curLeft = curPosition.left;
9456         } else {
9457             curTop = parseFloat( curCSSTop ) || 0;
9458             curLeft = parseFloat( curCSSLeft ) || 0;
9459         }
9460 
9461         if ( jQuery.isFunction( options ) ) {
9462             options = options.call( elem, i, curOffset );
9463         }
9464 
9465         if ( options.top != null ) {
9466             props.top = ( options.top - curOffset.top ) + curTop;
9467         }
9468         if ( options.left != null ) {
9469             props.left = ( options.left - curOffset.left ) + curLeft;
9470         }
9471 
9472         if ( "using" in options ) {
9473             options.using.call( elem, props );
9474         } else {
9475             curElem.css( props );
9476         }
9477     }
9478 };
9479 
9480 
9481 jQuery.fn.extend({
9482 
9483     position: function() {
9484         if ( !this[0] ) {
9485             return;
9486         }
9487 
9488         var elem = this[0],
9489 
9490         // Get *real* offsetParent
9491         offsetParent = this.offsetParent(),
9492 
9493         // Get correct offsets
9494         offset       = this.offset(),
9495         parentOffset = rroot.test(offsetParent[0].nodeName) ? { top: 0, left: 0 } : offsetParent.offset();
9496 
9497         // Subtract element margins
9498         // note: when an element has margin: auto the offsetLeft and marginLeft
9499         // are the same in Safari causing offset.left to incorrectly be 0
9500         offset.top  -= parseFloat( jQuery.css(elem, "marginTop") ) || 0;
9501         offset.left -= parseFloat( jQuery.css(elem, "marginLeft") ) || 0;
9502 
9503         // Add offsetParent borders
9504         parentOffset.top  += parseFloat( jQuery.css(offsetParent[0], "borderTopWidth") ) || 0;
9505         parentOffset.left += parseFloat( jQuery.css(offsetParent[0], "borderLeftWidth") ) || 0;
9506 
9507         // Subtract the two offsets
9508         return {
9509             top:  offset.top  - parentOffset.top,
9510             left: offset.left - parentOffset.left
9511         };
9512     },
9513 
9514     offsetParent: function() {
9515         return this.map(function() {
9516             var offsetParent = this.offsetParent || document.body;
9517             while ( offsetParent && (!rroot.test(offsetParent.nodeName) && jQuery.css(offsetParent, "position") === "static") ) {
9518                 offsetParent = offsetParent.offsetParent;
9519             }
9520             return offsetParent || document.body;
9521         });
9522     }
9523 });
9524 
9525 
9526 // Create scrollLeft and scrollTop methods
9527 jQuery.each( {scrollLeft: "pageXOffset", scrollTop: "pageYOffset"}, function( method, prop ) {
9528     var top = /Y/.test( prop );
9529 
9530     jQuery.fn[ method ] = function( val ) {
9531         return jQuery.access( this, function( elem, method, val ) {
9532             var win = getWindow( elem );
9533 
9534             if ( val === undefined ) {
9535                 return win ? (prop in win) ? win[ prop ] :
9536                     win.document.documentElement[ method ] :
9537                     elem[ method ];
9538             }
9539 
9540             if ( win ) {
9541                 win.scrollTo(
9542                     !top ? val : jQuery( win ).scrollLeft(),
9543                      top ? val : jQuery( win ).scrollTop()
9544                 );
9545 
9546             } else {
9547                 elem[ method ] = val;
9548             }
9549         }, method, val, arguments.length, null );
9550     };
9551 });
9552 
9553 function getWindow( elem ) {
9554     return jQuery.isWindow( elem ) ?
9555         elem :
9556         elem.nodeType === 9 ?
9557             elem.defaultView || elem.parentWindow :
9558             false;
9559 }
9560 // Create innerHeight, innerWidth, height, width, outerHeight and outerWidth methods
9561 jQuery.each( { Height: "height", Width: "width" }, function( name, type ) {
9562     jQuery.each( { padding: "inner" + name, content: type, "": "outer" + name }, function( defaultExtra, funcName ) {
9563         // margin is only for outerHeight, outerWidth
9564         jQuery.fn[ funcName ] = function( margin, value ) {
9565             var chainable = arguments.length && ( defaultExtra || typeof margin !== "boolean" ),
9566                 extra = defaultExtra || ( margin === true || value === true ? "margin" : "border" );
9567 
9568             return jQuery.access( this, function( elem, type, value ) {
9569                 var doc;
9570 
9571                 if ( jQuery.isWindow( elem ) ) {
9572                     // As of 5/8/2012 this will yield incorrect results for Mobile Safari, but there
9573                     // isn't a whole lot we can do. See pull request at this URL for discussion:
9574                     // https://github.com/jquery/jquery/pull/764
9575                     return elem.document.documentElement[ "client" + name ];
9576                 }
9577 
9578                 // Get document width or height
9579                 if ( elem.nodeType === 9 ) {
9580                     doc = elem.documentElement;
9581 
9582                     // Either scroll[Width/Height] or offset[Width/Height] or client[Width/Height], whichever is greatest
9583                     // unfortunately, this causes bug #3838 in IE6/8 only, but there is currently no good, small way to fix it.
9584                     return Math.max(
9585                         elem.body[ "scroll" + name ], doc[ "scroll" + name ],
9586                         elem.body[ "offset" + name ], doc[ "offset" + name ],
9587                         doc[ "client" + name ]
9588                     );
9589                 }
9590 
9591                 return value === undefined ?
9592                     // Get width or height on the element, requesting but not forcing parseFloat
9593                     jQuery.css( elem, type, value, extra ) :
9594 
9595                     // Set width or height on the element
9596                     jQuery.style( elem, type, value, extra );
9597             }, type, chainable ? margin : undefined, chainable, null );
9598         };
9599     });
9600 });
9601 // Expose jQuery to the global object
9602 window.jQuery = window.$ = jQuery;
9603 
9604 // Expose jQuery as an AMD module, but only for AMD loaders that
9605 // understand the issues with loading multiple versions of jQuery
9606 // in a page that all might call define(). The loader will indicate
9607 // they have special allowances for multiple jQuery versions by
9608 // specifying define.amd.jQuery = true. Register as a named module,
9609 // since jQuery can be concatenated with other files that may use define,
9610 // but not use a proper concatenation script that understands anonymous
9611 // AMD modules. A named AMD is safest and most robust way to register.
9612 // Lowercase jquery is used because AMD module names are derived from
9613 // file names, and jQuery is normally delivered in a lowercase file name.
9614 // Do this after creating the global so that if an AMD module wants to call
9615 // noConflict to hide this version of jQuery, it will work.
9616 if ( typeof define === "function" && define.amd && define.amd.jQuery ) {
9617     define( "jquery", [], function () { return jQuery; } );
9618 }
9619 
9620 })( window );
